It operates as: (a) collective national proud-might — the community's structural power becoming the inner ground for arrogant self-confidence and resistance to God (Lev 26:19, vc=33982; Eze 30:6, vc=33996; Eze 33:28, vc=33999); (b) individual/national wealth-pride — material success causing the heart to become proud (Eze 28:5, vc=34046; 1Ti 6:17, vc=60878) or generating declarations of self-sufficiency (Isa 47:8, vc=9563); (c) positional-height pride — physical and social elevation as a strategy of self-secured power that generates pride (Jer 49:16, vc=34167; Obd 3, vc=65674; Hab 2:9, vc=34169). Cross-register flag: M23 (strength/power/dominion) — several terms remain in M08 because their verses evidence strength misused as self-exaltation.

---

#### T1.3 — Boundary

##### T1.3.1 — What is the structural opposite of this characteristic — the inner-being reality that stands against or excludes it?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The structural opposite is explicitly named in the evidence. Psa 131:1 (vc=34059, M08-A1-VCG-03; vc=34224, M08-A2-VCG-01) names it in both the heart and eye registers simultaneously: "my heart is not lifted up; my eyes are not raised too high; I do not occupy myself with things too great and too marvelous for me" — the deliberate inner lowering of the heart and restraint of the gaze as the opposite of CHAR-1's upward movement. Jam 4:6 (vc=33931, M08-A4-VCG-01) and 1Pe 5:5 (vc=33934, M08-A4-VCG-01) name it explicitly: "God opposes the proud but gives grace to the humble" — humility (M09) is CHAR-1's named opposite, receiving what CHAR-1 forfeits. Pro 29:23 (vc=33960, M08-A4-VCG-04): "one's pride will bring him low, but he who is lowly in spirit will obtain honour" — the honour that CHAR-1 reaches for is received by its structural opposite. The verse evidence consistently identifies M09 (humility/lowliness of spirit) as CHAR-1's structural opposite.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

The structural opposite is evidenced through contrast. Deu 17:13 (vc=34124, M08-B-VCG-01): "all the people shall hear and fear and not act presumptuously again" — fear (reverent submission) is the opposite inner posture that prevents CHAR-2. Psa 19:13 (vc=34095, M08-B-VCG-02): "keep back your servant also from presumptuous sins; let them not have dominion over me" — the humble servant who seeks God's restraining grace is the structural opposite of the presumptuous person. Pro 11:2 (vc=34109, M08-B-VCG-02): "when arrogance [za.don] comes, disgrace follows, but with the humble is wisdom" — humility is explicitly paired against za.don as its structural opposite. 2Pe 2:10 (vc=42739, M08-B-VCG-03): "self-willed [authadēs], they do not tremble" — trembling reverence before authority is the opposite of self-willed defiance.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

The structural opposite is evidenced through contrast. Pro 27:2 (adjacent context to Pro 27:1, vc=33359, M08-C-VCG-01): "let another praise you, and not your own mouth" — receiving praise from others rather than self-asserting is the structural opposite of boasting. 1Cor 4:7 (vc=33871, M08-C-VCG-01): "what do you have that you did not receive?" — the opposite posture to CHAR-3 is the receiver's acknowledgment of received goods as received; gratitude rather than self-glorification. The full opposite of CHAR-3 is VCG-03's God-directed boasting (1Cor 1:31: "let the one who boasts, boast in the Lord") — the glorying-impulse directed wholly away from self toward God is CHAR-3's structural redemption and structural opposite simultaneously.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

The structural opposite is named directly in the evidence. Rom 12:3 (vc=60866, M08-D-VCG-02): "think with sober judgment [sōphrosynē], each according to the measure of faith that God has assigned" — sober-mindedness within God-assigned measure is the precise opposite of huperfroneō (thinking above). 1Cor 8:1 (vc=33935, M08-D-VCG-01): "love builds up" — love-directed cognition that builds the other is the opposite of knowledge-conceit that inflates the self. 1Cor 13:4 (vc=33936, M08-D-VCG-01): "love is not arrogant [fusioō]" — love as CHAR-4's direct structural opposite at the cognitive level.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

The structural opposite is evidenced through contrast. 1Ti 6:17 (vc=60878, M08-E-VCG-02): "not to be haughty, nor to set their hopes on the uncertainty of riches, but on God, who richly provides everything to enjoy" — trust in God as provider rather than in riches as the ground of self-sufficiency is the named structural opposite. Eze 16:49 (vc=33979, M08-E-VCG-01): the structural opposite of Sodom's power-pride-and-ease is aiding the poor and needy — using structural goods in service of others rather than as the ground for self-exaltation. The structural opposite of CHAR-5 is the stewardship posture: receiving structural goods from God as gifts to be stewarded for others, not claimed as self-sufficient grounds for elevation.

---

##### T1.3.2 — What does this characteristic explicitly exclude or resist?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

CHAR-1 explicitly excludes five realities that the verse evidence names directly. First, gratitude: Deu 8:14 (vc=34223, M08-A1-VCG-01) — "your heart will be lifted up and you forget the Lord your God who brought you out of the land of Egypt" — the lifted heart displaces the memory of divine provision; Hos 13:6 (vc=34232, M08-A1-VCG-01): "their heart was lifted up; therefore they forgot me." Second, hearing and repentance: Jer 13:15 (vc=34053, M08-A4-VCG-04) — "be not proud, for the Lord has spoken" — pride blocks attentiveness to God's word; Hos 7:10 (vc=34001, M08-A3-VCG-03): "the pride of Israel testifies to his face; yet they do not return to the Lord." Third, seeking God: Psa 10:4 (vc=34074, M08-A2-VCG-02) — "the wicked does not seek him; all his thoughts are, 'there is no God.'" Fourth, wisdom: Eze 28:17 (vc=34047, M08-A1-VCG-02) — "your heart was proud... you corrupted your wisdom for the sake of your splendour." Fifth, the fear of the Lord: Pro 8:13 (vc=33958, M08-A4-VCG-04) — "Pride and arrogance and the way of evil and perverted speech I hate" — wisdom's voice names CHAR-1 as categorically incompatible with fearing God.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

CHAR-2 explicitly excludes and resists four things named in the evidence: (a) Obedience to revealed divine commands: Deu 1:43 (vc=34123, M08-B-VCG-01) — Israel's presumption means they did not obey God's explicit prohibition; Neh 9:16 (vc=34120) — "did not obey your commandments"; (b) Submission to appointed authority: Deu 17:12 (vc=34110, M08-B-VCG-02) — "the man who acts presumptuously by not obeying the priest who stands to minister there before the Lord your God"; (c) Reverence/fear of God: Psa 86:14 (vc=34097, M08-B-VCG-02) — "they do not set God before them"; 2Pe 2:10 (vc=42739, M08-B-VCG-03) — "they do not tremble before the glorious ones"; (d) Wisdom: Pro 11:2 (vc=34109, M08-B-VCG-02) — arrogance excludes the wisdom that accompanies the humble.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

CHAR-3 (VCG-01 form) excludes and resists: (a) Honest self-assessment: 2Cor 10:12 (context of vc=33888, M08-C-VCG-02): comparing oneself with others and measuring oneself by oneself — Paul identifies this as the epistemic failure underlying self-commendation; (b) Acknowledgment of received goods: 1Cor 4:7 (vc=33871, M08-C-VCG-01): "why do you boast as if you did not receive it?" — self-directed boasting denies the received quality of one's capacities; (c) Integrity between inner and outer: 2Cor 5:12 (vc=33872, M08-C-VCG-02): Paul contrasts boasting in outward appearance with what is in the heart — CHAR-3's surface-boasting resists inward honesty; (d) Patience: Pro 27:1 (vc=33359, M08-C-VCG-01): boasting about tomorrow resists the patient non-claim over an uncertain future.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

CHAR-4 excludes: (a) Accurate self-knowledge: Rom 12:3 (vc=60866, M08-D-VCG-02) — thinking within God-assigned measure is what CHAR-4 exceeds; (b) Understanding/comprehension: 1Ti 6:4 (vc=33925, M08-D-VCG-02) — conceit paired with "understanding nothing" (mēden epistamenos) — CHAR-4 produces comprehensive epistemic failure; (c) Love's other-orientation: 1Cor 8:1 (vc=33935, M08-D-VCG-01) — "knowledge puffs up, but love builds up" — CHAR-4 is the cognitive turning-inward that resists love's outward building; 1Cor 13:4 (vc=33936): "love is not arrogant [fusioō]"; (d) Mourning/appropriate grief: 1Cor 5:2 (vc=33940, M08-D-VCG-01): puffed-up community that should be mourning — CHAR-4 resists the appropriate affective response to genuine failure.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

CHAR-5 explicitly excludes: (a) Trust in God as the genuine source of power and wealth: 1Ti 6:17 (vc=60878, M08-E-VCG-02) — "set their hopes on the uncertainty of riches" rather than God; Lev 26:19 (vc=33982, M08-E-VCG-01): "the pride of your power" is broken by God — implying it resisted acknowledging God as the source; (b) Service to the vulnerable: Eze 16:49 (vc=33979, M08-E-VCG-01) — Sodom's power-pride paired with failure to aid the poor and needy; (c) Humility before God's power: the repeated "God will bring down proud might" pattern (Eze 30:6; 30:18; 32:12) implies CHAR-5 resists the recognition that God's power supersedes structural human power.

---

##### T1.3.3 — What is this characteristic not — where does it end and something else begin?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Three boundaries are evidenced. First, CHAR-1 ends where legitimate creaturely standing and God-given dignity begin: 1Sa 16:7 (vc=12091, M08-A1-VCG-03) — God does not prize what humans prize in outward height and rejects that standard, but the verse implies God does look at the heart for what genuinely matters. The evidence is silent on treating all self-awareness or self-regard as CHAR-1. Second, CHAR-1 is distinct from CHAR-3 (boasting and self-display — M08-C): Isa 16:6 (vc=33969, vc=33989, M08-A3-VCG-01) — Moab's foundational pride (CHAR-1) generates "arrogance, his pride, and his insolence; in his idle boasting" as its output — the disposition (CHAR-1) precedes and produces the verbal expression (CHAR-3). Third, CHAR-1 is distinct from CHAR-2 (presumptuous defiance — M08-B): CHAR-1 is the elevated inner self as a settled condition, while CHAR-2 is the self boiling over against a specific divine-established limit. The zid/za.don/zed vocabulary of M08-B names the act-of-wilful-transgression; the ga.on/rum/ga.vah vocabulary of M08-A names the inner disposition that may or may not result in such transgression.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Three boundaries are evidenced. First, CHAR-2 ends where CHAR-1 begins: CHAR-1 is the elevated inner disposition (what the self is and claims); CHAR-2 is the active will asserting itself against a specific external limit (what the self does against authority). A person may have CHAR-1 without any specific act of CHAR-2; CHAR-2 typically presupposes CHAR-1 as its dispositional substrate but is analytically distinct. Second, CHAR-2 is not the same as inadvertent sin: the zid vocabulary specifically names the boiling-over quality of wilful intention — Deu 17:12 (vc=34110) contrasts the presumptuous man with less intentional failure. Third, CHAR-2 ends where archō in its non-M08 sense begins: the archō register in §3.A includes only M08-relational verses (Mat 16:22, Mar 8:32, etc.) where the NT term evidences presumptuous self-assertion; other archō uses (temporal narrative markers) were excluded at Phase 5.5 as non-M08 content.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Three boundaries. First, CHAR-3 ends where God-directed glorying begins: VCG-03 (Rom 5:2; 1Cor 1:31; Phili 3:3) is not CHAR-3 in its condemned form — the same kauchaomai verb, directed toward God and received grace, is evidenced as appropriate and commanded. The boundary is the direction of the boast, not the act of boasting itself. Second, CHAR-3 ends where legitimate relational commendation within examined grounds begins: VCG-02 (2Cor 10:13, vc=33888: Paul constrains his boasting to God-assigned spheres) is examined, bounded self-commendation rather than condemned self-boasting. Third, CHAR-3 ends where CHAR-1 (inner disposition) begins: Jam 4:16 (vc=33886) sequences "arrogance" (CHAR-1 substrate) → "you boast" (CHAR-3 act); the boasting is CHAR-3, the arrogance its CHAR-1 source.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Three boundaries. First, CHAR-4 ends where CHAR-1 begins: CHAR-1 is the dispositional elevation of the self (the heart lifted above proper station — a settled posture); CHAR-4 is the cognitive inflation of the self (the mind's false picture of itself — an epistemic failure). The heart's arrogance (CHAR-1) generates the mind's conceit (CHAR-4) as its cognitive expression. Second, CHAR-4 ends where CHAR-3 begins: CHAR-4 is the inner cognitive state (the inflated self-picture); CHAR-3 is its verbal/social expression (boasting). 1Cor 4:19 (vc=33939, M08-D-VCG-01): Paul will expose the inflated people not by their "talk" (CHAR-3) but by their "power" — the talk is CHAR-3's expression; the inflation is CHAR-4. Third, CHAR-4 is distinct from ordinary self-confidence: Rom 12:3 (vc=60866) implies that appropriate self-assessment within God-assigned measure is not CHAR-4; only exceeding that measure constitutes CHAR-4.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Three boundaries. First, CHAR-5 ends where legitimate stewardship of power and wealth begins: possessing strength, authority, or wealth is not CHAR-5; CHAR-5 is the inner arrogance that uses those goods as the ground for self-exaltation. 1Ti 6:17 (vc=60878, M08-E-VCG-02) implies that the wealthy can avoid CHAR-5 through proper hope-placement. Second, CHAR-5 ends where CHAR-1 begins: CHAR-1 is the general dispositional elevation of the self; CHAR-5 is the specific form of that elevation grounded in structural power. The relationship is that CHAR-5 is a specific instance of CHAR-1's dispositional pattern through the medium of structural goods. Third, CHAR-5 is distinct from M23 (strength/power/dominion) content: the cross-register flag identifies that several CHAR-5 terms primarily belong to M23; they remain in M08 specifically because the §3.D verses evidence strength misused as self-exaltation, not strength in its legitimate exercise.

---

#### T1.4 — Modes of Operation

##### T1.4.1 — In what distinct ways does this characteristic operate within the inner person?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The verse evidence evidences five distinct operational modes. (a) Prosperity-triggered heart-elevation: fullness causes the heart to lift (Deu 8:14, vc=34223, M08-A1-VCG-01; Hos 13:6, vc=34232, M08-A1-VCG-01) — a satisfaction-to-self-exaltation sequence. (b) Power/achievement-triggered royal elevation: growing strong activates heart-pride (2Ch 26:16, vc=34044, M08-A1-VCG-01; Dan 11:12, vc=34234, M08-A1-VCG-02: "his heart shall be exalted" after military victory). (c) Volitional declaration against God: the will asserting its intent to self-exalt (Isa 14:13, vc=34233, M08-A4-VCG-05: "I will ascend to heaven"; Num 15:30, vc=65731, M08-A4-VCG-05: acting "with a high hand" equivalent to reviling God). (d) Ocular and postural expression: pride manifesting in the gaze and bearing (Pro 6:17, vc=34247, M08-A2-VCG-01: "haughty eyes" first in list God hates; Isa 3:16, vc=34052, M08-A2-VCG-02: outstretched necks and wanton glances). (e) Collective inner attribution: entire peoples characterised by pride as their defining inner posture (Isa 16:6, vc=33989, M08-A3-VCG-01; Hos 5:5, vc=34000, M08-A3-VCG-03: "the pride of Israel testifies to his face").

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Three distinct operational modes are evidenced. (a) The boiling-will mode: the will seizes on a prohibited act and executes it in direct defiance of a named divine command (Deu 1:43, vc=34123, M08-B-VCG-01: going up to battle despite God's prohibition; Deu 18:20, vc=34119: speaking a word God did not command). (b) The contemptuous-disregard mode: the will settles into a habitual posture of treating divine law and its agents as objects of scorn and opposition (Psa 119:85, vc=34102, M08-B-VCG-02: "the insolent have dug pitfalls for me... they do not live according to your law"; Psa 119:51: "the insolent utterly deride me"). (c) The domineering-authority mode: the will expresses CHAR-2 by claiming and exercising authority over others in a way that bypasses legitimate constraint (Mar 10:42, vc=55588, M08-B-VCG-03: rulers "who lord it over" and "exercise authority over" — the domineering as self-authorised power; 2Pe 2:10, vc=42739: self-willed dismissal of authority and refusal to tremble).

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Five distinct operational modes are evidenced. (a) Achievement-credential boasting: Jer 9:23 (vc=33342, M08-C-VCG-01): boasting in wisdom, might, wealth — the three forms of creaturely capacity claimed as grounds for self-glorification. (b) Premature glorification: 1Ki 20:11 (vc=33353, M08-C-VCG-01): "let not him who puts on his armour boast like him who takes it off" — boasting before the outcome is achieved. (c) Empty social self-promotion: Pro 25:14 (vc=33358, M08-C-VCG-01): boasting of a gift never given; Pro 20:14 (vc=33357, M08-C-VCG-01): the buyer's boast of a bargain as social duplicity. (d) Future-certainty presumption: Pro 27:1 (vc=33359, M08-C-VCG-01): boasting about tomorrow as if the future is secure. (e) Inner boasting-disposition: alazoneia (Jam 4:16, vc=33866; 1Jo 2:16, vc=33865) — the settled inner orientation of self-glorifying display as a way of being in the world.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Four distinct operational modes. (a) Knowledge-conceit: 1Cor 8:1 (vc=33935, M08-D-VCG-01): received knowledge inflating the self-picture without the relational anchor of love. (b) Partisan-attachment conceit: 1Cor 4:6 (vc=33937, M08-D-VCG-01): puffed up in favour of one leader against another — the cognitive self-assessment becomes inflated through tribal/partisan alignment. (c) Contemptuous confidence: 1Cor 4:18 (vc=33938, M08-D-VCG-01): presuming on an authority's absence — the mind incorrectly assessing its own freedom from accountability. (d) Ungrounded spiritual-experience inflation: Col 2:18 (vc=33941, M08-D-VCG-01): "inflated by his sensuous mind" — without factual basis, through claimed spiritual experiences that generate a false cognitive picture of the self's spiritual standing.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Five distinct operational modes evidenced. (a) National military-might pride: collective inner confidence generated by structural national power (Eze 30:6, vc=33996, M08-E-VCG-01: Egypt's "proud might" as national inner confidence; Lev 26:19, vc=33982: Israel's "pride of power"). (b) Wealth-induced heart-elevation: material success generating inner pride (Eze 28:5, vc=34046, M08-E-VCG-02: "wealth gained through wisdom caused the heart to become proud"; 1Ti 6:17, vc=60878: wealth generating haughty self-regard). (c) Physical-height strategy: using physical or social elevation as a power strategy that generates proud self-security (Jer 49:16, vc=34167, M08-E-VCG-02; Obd 3, vc=65674; Hab 2:9, vc=34169). (d) Ease-grounded self-sufficiency: voluptuous ease and material abundance generating the inner declaration of self-completeness (Isa 47:8, vc=9563: "I am, and there is no one besides me"; Eze 16:49, vc=33979). (e) Self-willed impetuousness: imperious self-assertion from a position of power (Eze 16:30, vc=57959, M08-E-VCG-02: shal.le.tet — impetuousness in the heart expressed as brazen self-will).

---

##### T1.4.2 — Does this characteristic operate differently depending on context, direction, or constitutional level?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes. By context: CHAR-1's trigger varies — prosperity (Deu 8:14, vc=34223, M08-A1-VCG-01), power (2Ch 26:16, vc=34044, M08-A1-VCG-01), beauty (Eze 28:17, vc=34047, M08-A1-VCG-02), military victory (Dan 11:12, vc=34234, M08-A1-VCG-02) each generates the same inner movement from a different occasion. By direction: CHAR-1 operates vertically against God (Dan 11:36, vc=34235, M08-A1-VCG-02: "exalts himself above every god"; Num 15:30, vc=65731, M08-A4-VCG-05: "with a high hand... reviles the Lord") and horizontally against other human beings (Deu 17:20, vc=34231, M08-A1-VCG-01: king's heart above "his brothers"; Psa 10:2, vc=33963, M08-A4-VCG-03: arrogance driving pursuit of the poor). By constitutional level: from the deep heart and spirit (M08-A1; Ecc 7:8, vc=12087, M08-A4-VCG-04: "proud in spirit") through the visible gaze (M08-A2) to public speech and act (1Sa 2:3, vc=12084, M08-A4-VCG-05: arrogance "from your mouth"; Psa 75:5, vc=34165, M08-A4-VCG-05: "speak with haughty neck").

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Yes. By context: CHAR-2 operates in prophetic contexts (false prophet presuming to speak God's word — Deu 18:20, vc=34119), legal-judicial contexts (defying the appointed judge — Deu 17:12, vc=34110), military contexts (advancing despite God's prohibition — Deu 1:43, vc=34123), community contexts (social insolence and oppression — Psa 119 corpus), and NT narrative contexts (Peter presuming to correct Jesus — Mar 8:32, vc=55607; the wicked servant abusing fellow servants — Mat 24:49, vc=55613, M08-B-VCG-03). By direction: CHAR-2 operates vertically against God (Deu 18:20; Jer 50:27, vc=34127: "you have striven against the Lord") and horizontally against appointed human authorities (Deu 17:12) and against social others (Psa 119:69: "the arrogant smear me with lies"). By constitutional level: the will is the primary constitutional seat, but CHAR-2 moves outward through speech (Deu 18:20), physical action (Deu 1:43), and relational aggression (Psa 119:85).

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Yes, significantly. By direction: the kauchaomai family operates identically at the linguistic level across three directions — self-directed (condemned, VCG-01), God-directed (approved, VCG-03), examined-within-limits (VCG-02). The direction entirely determines the moral valence. By context: ha.lal self-directed in Hebrew wisdom literature names premature, creaturely-asset, and empty boasting (Jer 9:23, Pro 20:14, 25:14, 27:1); the Pauline kauchaomai discourse (2Cor 10–12, VCG-02) operates in the specific context of apostolic self-defence against false teachers whose boasting claims challenged Paul's authority. By constitutional level: alazoneia is the dispositional (inner) substrate; kauchaomai is the speech-act expression; self-display is the social/visible form.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Yes. By context: intellectual contexts generate knowledge-conceit (1Cor 8:1, vc=33935); community contexts generate partisan-conceit (1Cor 4:6, vc=33937) and relational-disorder conceit (2Cor 12:20, vc=33942); leadership contexts generate leadership-conceit (1Ti 3:6, vc=33924); spiritual-experience contexts generate Col 2:18 (vc=33941) ungrounded inflation. By direction: all CHAR-4 operates inward (the mind's self-assessment) and then outward into relational dysfunction (strife, controversy, communal disorder) and epistemic failure (understanding nothing). By constitutional level: CHAR-4 operates at the cognitive/mind level, making it constitutionally distinct from CHAR-1 (heart/spirit) and CHAR-2 (will).

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Yes. By context: military/national (Eze 30:6 — Egypt's military-power pride; Lev 26:19 — Israel's collective power), economic (Eze 28:5 — Tyre's wealth; 1Ti 6:17 — individual wealthy persons), geographical (Jer 49:16 — Edom's mountain fortress; Obd 3 — the same), and ease (Eze 16:49 — Sodom's material abundance). By direction: CHAR-5 operates vertically against God (Isa 47:8: the self-sufficiency declaration against God; Lev 26:19: pride that resists God's commands) and horizontally against others (Eze 16:49: contempt for the poor). By constitutional level: from the deep heart (Eze 28:5: heart proud; Eze 16:30: impetuousness in the heart) through the collective social posture (ga.on national proud-might) to physical-structural expression (fortified heights).

---

##### T1.4.3 — Does this characteristic have a communicative or speech-based mode of operation — and if so, how does it function?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes. The verse evidence evidences a direct speech mode with four forms. First, defiant declaration against God: Isa 14:13 (vc=34233, M08-A4-VCG-05) — "You said in your heart, 'I will ascend to heaven'" — the will's internal speech escalating to external declaration; Dan 11:36 (vc=34235, M08-A1-VCG-02): the king "shall speak astonishing things against the God of gods." Second, prohibitive warning indicating CHAR-1's speech form: 1Sa 2:3 (vc=12084, M08-A4-VCG-05) — "talk no more so very proudly, let not arrogance come from your mouth" — arrogant speech as the expected outward expression. Third, the proud heart's defiant communal speech: Isa 9:9 (vc=33967, M08-A1-VCG-03) — Ephraim and Samaria "who say in pride and in arrogance of heart" — the inner posture generating the speech-act. Fourth, contemptuous speech against others: Psa 17:10 (vc=34028, M08-A1-VCG-03) — "with their mouths they speak arrogantly" — arrogant speech as the relational weapon of the proud inner person.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Yes. Speech is a primary vehicle for CHAR-2. Deu 18:20 (vc=34119, M08-B-VCG-01): the false prophet who "presumes to speak a word in my name that I have not commanded" — speech as the medium of presumptuous transgression against divine revelation. Psa 119:69 (vc=34100, M08-B-VCG-02): "the insolent smear me with lies" — speech as the vehicle of CHAR-2's social aggression. Psa 119:51 (vc=34099): "the insolent utterly deride me" — contemptuous speech. Jer 43:2 (vc=34105, M08-B-VCG-02): "the insolent men said to Jeremiah, 'You are telling a lie'" — CHAR-2 expressed as direct contradiction of prophetic authority. Luk 3:8 (vc=55578, M08-B-VCG-03): "do not begin to say within yourselves, 'We have Abraham as our father'" — CHAR-2 as the presumptuous internal claim articulated in speech.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Yes — speech is CHAR-3's primary operational mode. The kauchaomai verb is inherently communicative: one boasts to someone, before someone, about something. 1Ki 20:11 (vc=33353, M08-C-VCG-01): the proverbial warning against boasting "like him who takes off his armour" — boasting as public speech addressed to those who can hear. Pro 25:14 (vc=33358): boasting of a gift never given — the false social claim requires a listener. 2Ti 3:2 (vc=33868, M08-C-VCG-01): alazōn in the vice catalogue — the braggart as a social person-type whose characteristic is public self-assertion. Even the inner-disposition form (alazoneia) generates its expression through speech and social display.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Partially. 1Cor 4:19 (vc=33939, M08-D-VCG-01): Paul distinguishes between the inflated persons' "talk" and their actual "power" — the inflated self-assessment generates inflated speech, but the speech is CHAR-3's expression of CHAR-4's inner state, not CHAR-4 itself. 1Ti 6:4 (vc=33925, M08-D-VCG-02): conceit produces "an unhealthy craving for controversy and for quarrels about words" — verbal controversy as CHAR-4's relational outworking. CHAR-4 operates primarily in the cognitive register, with speech as its secondary expression (which overlaps with CHAR-3).

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Yes. Isa 47:8 (vc=9563, M08-E-VCG-02): Babylon's self-declaration — "I am, and there is no one besides me" — is a speech-act of power-grounded self-sufficiency. The declaration is the verbal expression of CHAR-5's inner posture: the structural power generates the confident inner claim, which is then declared in speech. This is CHAR-5's overlap with CHAR-3 (verbal expression): the power-grounded inner arrogance expresses itself verbally as the declaration of self-completeness.

---

#### T1.5 — Immediate Response

##### T1.5.1 — What is the first or most immediate inner-being response to receiving or encountering this characteristic?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The evidence distinguishes by direction. When CHAR-1 is encountered as its victim: the immediate response is crushing inner experience — Psa 123:4 (vc=33953, M08-A4-VCG-03): "our soul has had more than enough of the scorn of those who are at ease, of the contempt of the proud" — overwhelming inner saturation under contempt; Psa 13:2 (vc=34241, M08-A4-VCG-03): "how long must I take counsel in my soul and have sorrow in my heart all the day? How long shall my enemy be exalted over me?" — inner sorrow and helplessness as the immediate response. When CHAR-1 is one's own inner state: the evidence is largely silent on any immediate internal recognition or discomfort in the proud person. 2Ch 26:16 (vc=34044, M08-A1-VCG-01) shows Uzziah acting from his pride without recorded inner resistance; Jer 49:16 (vc=34054, M08-A1-VCG-03) names "the horror you inspire has deceived you" — the proud person is deceived, not alarmed, by their own state. CHAR-1 appears to generate no immediate internal counter-signal in its possessor.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

From the perspective of those who encounter CHAR-2 from another: the psalmist's response in the Psa 119 corpus is sustained anguish and the turn to God for rescue. Psa 119:122 (vc=34103, M08-B-VCG-02): "be a pledge for your servant for good; let not the insolent oppress me" — the victim's immediate response is appeal to God for protection. Psa 86:14 (vc=34097, M08-B-VCG-02): "a band of ruthless men seek my life" — the immediate experience is one of threat and vulnerability. From within the person exercising CHAR-2: the evidence suggests the will's assertion carries its own internal momentum — Deu 1:43 (vc=34123) evidences the people going up "presumptuously" without recorded inner hesitation after God's prohibition.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

From the perspective of those who encounter CHAR-3: the Pauline discourse evidences the complexity of reception. 2Cor 11:1 (context of VCG-02 corpus): Paul asks the Corinthians to "bear with him in a little foolishness" — the audience's immediate response to boasting is to perceive it as foolish or socially uncomfortable; 2Cor 11:16 (vc=33893, M08-C-VCG-02): Paul anticipates that even legitimate examined boasting will be received as foolishness. 1Cor 5:6 (vc=33903, M08-C-VCG-01): "your boasting is not good" — the community's internal boasting produces a discomfort addressed directly.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

1Cor 5:2 (vc=33940, M08-D-VCG-01) provides the most direct evidence: the Corinthians are puffed up (CHAR-4 active) instead of mourning — implying that the appropriate immediate response to a community's moral failure is grief, not the self-inflating confidence they are displaying. The inflation specifically prevents the grief response. 1Cor 4:18 (vc=33938, M08-D-VCG-01): some are puffed up presuming Paul will not return — the immediate inner state is contemptuous confidence, not anxiety or appropriate humility.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (S)

The verse evidence in §3.D is largely silent on the immediate inner-being response of those who encounter CHAR-5 from another. The evidence focuses on God's response (breaking the pride — Lev 26:19, vc=33982) and the structural consequences (desolation — Eze 33:28, vc=33999), not on the victim's immediate inner experience.

---

##### T1.5.2 — Is the immediate response consistent across the verse evidence, or does it vary?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The response varies by direction and subject. For victims of CHAR-1's contempt, the immediate response is consistently overwhelming inner suffering (Psa 123:4, vc=33953, M08-A4-VCG-03; Psa 36:11, vc=33966, M08-A4-VCG-03: arrogance personified as "the foot of arrogance" pressing upon the psalmist). For God's response, it is consistent and active: 2Sa 22:28 (vc=34236, M08-A4-VCG-02) — "your eyes are on the haughty to bring them down"; Luk 1:51 (vc=33930, M08-A1-VCG-03) — God "has scattered the proud in the thoughts of their hearts" — immediate divine opposition is the consistent divine response. For the proud person's own experience: the evidence is consistently silent on immediate self-recognition. CHAR-1 appears to be experientially invisible to its possessor in the moment — its consequences (destruction, humiliation, forgetfulness of God) arrive without the person perceiving the trajectory.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

The response varies by role. For victims of CHAR-2: consistently turn to God as rescuer and judge (Psa 119:122 — pleading for protection; Psa 86:14 — appealing for deliverance). For the person exercising CHAR-2: no evidence of immediate internal counter-response; CHAR-2 appears to execute without internal resistance, consistent with the "boiling over" quality of zid that implies momentum rather than deliberation. For God's response: consistently punitive and corrective — Deu 17:12 (vc=34110): the presumptuous person "shall die"; Neh 9:10 (vc=34125): "you performed signs and wonders" as corrective response to Egypt's CHAR-2.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

The response varies by register. For VCG-01 condemned boasting: the wisdom tradition consistently names it as foolishness (1Ki 20:11: the premature boaster is a fool) and its social reception is negative when exposed. For VCG-02 examined boasting: reception is mixed — some receive Paul's self-defence as legitimate, others as foolishness (2Cor 11:16/17, vc=33893/33922). For VCG-03 God-directed boasting: reception is positive within the community of faith — mutual boasting between Paul and his communities is affirmed (2Cor 7:4, vc=33917; 1Th 2:19, vc=33913, M08-C-VCG-03).

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

The verse evidence is largely silent on the inner phenomenology of the person experiencing CHAR-4 in the moment. The evidence names the cognitive state (inflation, false self-picture) and its relational consequences, not the subjective felt experience of the inflated person.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (S)

Silent. See T1.5.1.

---

##### T1.5.3 — Where the verse evidence is silent on immediate response, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (S)

The verse evidence is silent on the proud person's immediate internal recognition of their own pride in the moment of its exercise. No verse in §3 evidences the proud person perceiving or being disturbed by their own CHAR-1 as it operates. This silence is analytically significant: it suggests CHAR-1 is phenomenologically self-concealing in its possessor, operating without generating the internal signals that would alert the person to its presence. The wisdom corpus's emphasis on external consequences (Pro 16:18, vc=34073: "pride goes before destruction") as the primary corrective signal is consistent with this absence — if internal recognition occurred, external catastrophe would not need to serve as the sole correction mechanism.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (S)

The verse evidence is silent on the immediate internal experience of the presumptuous person during the act of CHAR-2. No verse in §3.A describes the inner phenomenology of the will in the moment of its boiling-over transgression. The evidence focuses on the external act, its characterisation, and its consequences rather than the felt inner experience.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (S)

The verse evidence is largely silent on the inner phenomenology of the person exercising VCG-01 condemned boasting in the moment of its execution. The evidence focuses on what is boasted about and why it is wrong, not the felt inner experience of the boasting act.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

The verse evidence is silent on the immediate internal experience of the person exercising CHAR-4. What is named is the cognitive state (inflated self-picture) and external consequence (controversy, blindness, communal disorder), not the felt inner experience. Confirmed.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (S)

The verse evidence is silent on the immediate inner-being response of those who encounter CHAR-5 from another. Confirmed.

---

#### T1.6 — Sustained Effect

##### T1.6.1 — What does this characteristic produce in the inner being over time?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The verse evidence evidences four sustained inner consequences. First, forgetfulness of God: Deu 8:14 (vc=34223, M08-A1-VCG-01) — the lifted heart "forgets the Lord your God"; Hos 13:6 (vc=34232, M08-A1-VCG-01) — "their heart was lifted up; therefore they forgot me" — CHAR-1 progressively displaces God from the inner person's awareness. Second, wisdom corruption: Eze 28:17 (vc=34047, M08-A1-VCG-02) — "your heart was proud because of your beauty; you corrupted your wisdom for the sake of your splendour" — the cognitive-discernment faculty is damaged by sustained CHAR-1. Third, deepening repentance-resistance: Hos 7:10 (vc=34001, M08-A3-VCG-03) — "the pride of Israel testifies to his face; yet they do not return to the Lord their God, nor seek him, for all this" — sustained CHAR-1 hardens the inner person against relational restoration. Fourth, habituation into a permanent inner gait: Dan 4:37 (vc=34094, M08-A4-VCG-04) — "those who walk in pride" — implying that sustained CHAR-1 becomes the manner in which the person moves through all experience.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Three sustained consequences are evidenced. (a) Hardening: Neh 9:16 (vc=34120, M08-B-VCG-01) and Neh 9:29 (vc=34126) evidence repeated presumption across generations — "even after warnings, they acted presumptuously again" — the characteristic deepens rather than diminishing with time. (b) Dispositional scoffer identity: Pro 21:24 (vc=34096, vc=34114, M08-B-VCG-02): sustained CHAR-2 produces the scoffer as a stable identity type — "haughty, arrogant, 'scoffer' is his name; he acts with arrogant pride [za.don]." (c) Organic growth of arrogance: Eze 7:10 (vc=34118, M08-B-VCG-02): "arrogance has blossomed, pride has budded" — the image of organic growth suggests CHAR-2 compounds over time into a fully matured dispositional characteristic.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

For VCG-01 condemned self-boasting: 1Cor 5:6 (vc=33903, M08-C-VCG-01): "your boasting is not good. Do you not know that a little leaven leavens the whole lump?" — boasting spreads corruption through the inner community over time. 2Ti 3:2 (vc=33868, M08-C-VCG-01): alazōn appears in an end-times character list as a stable identity trait — sustained VCG-01 boasting produces the braggart as a settled social-identity type. The alazoneia disposition (Jam 4:16, vc=33866; 1Jo 2:16, vc=33865) implies a sustained inner orientation that generates repeated boasting acts.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Three sustained consequences evidenced. (a) Epistemic blindness: 1Ti 6:4 (vc=33925, M08-D-VCG-02): "understanding nothing [mēden epistamenos]" — sustained CHAR-4 produces comprehensive intellectual blindness; the inflated self-picture prevents genuine understanding. (b) Controversy-craving: 1Ti 6:4: "an unhealthy craving for controversy and for quarrels about words" — sustained conceit generates an inner orientation toward intellectual combat as self-validation. (c) Communal relational disorder: 2Cor 12:20 (vc=33942, M08-D-VCG-02): fusiōsis in a cluster including "quarreling, jealousy, anger, hostility, slander, gossip, conceit, disorder" — sustained CHAR-4 embeds the person within a web of relational dysfunction.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Two sustained consequences evidenced. (a) Deepening self-sufficiency and blindness to God: Isa 47:8 (vc=9563, M08-E-VCG-02): "you who say in your heart, 'I am, and there is no one besides me'" — the inner declaration of self-completeness that sustained CHAR-5 produces; (b) Total desolation when structural power is removed: Eze 33:28 (vc=33999, M08-E-VCG-01): "I will make the land a desolation... and her proud might shall come to an end" — the structural power that CHAR-5 rests on is its only inner anchor; when God removes it, the inner person collapses with the external structure. CHAR-5's inner sustainability is entirely dependent on the continued existence of the structural power it claims — unlike CHAR-1 (which generates from internal self-love regardless of external circumstances).

---

##### T1.6.2 — What states, qualities, capacities, or orientations does sustained exposure to or possession of this characteristic establish?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Sustained CHAR-1 establishes: (a) An inner condition of self-sufficiency that crowds out dependence on God — Hos 13:6 (vc=34232, M08-A1-VCG-01): prosperity → fullness → heart lifted → God forgotten — the self-contained inner state. (b) A relational posture of contempt toward others — Psa 123:4 (vc=33953, M08-A4-VCG-03): the proud's contempt as a chronic social orientation; Psa 10:2 (vc=33963, M08-A4-VCG-03): "in arrogance the wicked hotly pursue the poor" — sustained CHAR-1 generates an actively predatory relational mode. (c) A perceptual closure that removes God from the inner horizon — Psa 10:4 (vc=34074, M08-A2-VCG-02): "all his thoughts are, 'there is no God'" — functional atheism as a sustained cognitive-perceptual state. (d) Divine relational estrangement — Psa 138:6 (vc=12086, vc=34300, M08-A4-VCG-02): "the haughty he knows from afar" — God's sustained relational distance as the structural consequence.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Sustained CHAR-2 establishes: (a) The scoffer's contempt posture — Pro 21:24 (vc=34096, M08-B-VCG-02): the identity of the one who acts with deliberate arrogant pride; (b) Strife as the relational mode — Pro 13:10 (vc=34113, M08-B-VCG-02): "by insolence [za.don] comes nothing but strife"; (c) Deception as a social strategy — Psa 119:69 (vc=34100, M08-B-VCG-02): "the insolent smear me with lies"; Psa 119:78 (vc=34101): "the insolent have wronged me with falsehood"; (d) Active predation against the godly — Psa 119:85 (vc=34102): "the insolent have dug pitfalls for me, men who do not live according to your law."

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

For VCG-01: the braggart's identity (2Ti 3:2, vc=33868 — alazōn as a stable character type); the community of corruption (1Cor 5:6 — leaven spreading through the lump); the empty social presentation disconnected from reality (Pro 25:14 — clouds and wind without rain; Pro 20:14 — the duplicitous buyer). For VCG-02's examined result: sustained examined boasting within God-given limits produces a ground of legitimate conscience-testimony (2Cor 1:12, vc=33912: boasting in conscience's testimony to sincere conduct) — an inner confidence grounded in God-enabled integrity.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Sustained CHAR-4 establishes: (a) The controversy-oriented cognitive posture: 1Ti 6:4 (vc=33925, M08-D-VCG-02): "unhealthy craving for controversy" as a settled orientation; (b) Epistemic incompetence masked as competence: 1Ti 6:4: "understanding nothing" while the inflated self-picture maintains the illusion of competence; (c) Relational strife as a stable social pattern: 2Cor 12:20 (vc=33942): fusiōsis embedded in a stable cluster of relational failure-modes. The community of Pro 13:10 context — CHAR-4 generates "nothing but strife" as a settled social output.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Sustained CHAR-5 establishes: (a) the inner posture of self-sufficiency — Isa 47:8 (vc=9563, M08-E-VCG-02): "I am, and there is no one besides me; I shall not sit as a widow or know the loss of children" — the confident claim of complete, self-sustaining existence; (b) contempt for the vulnerable — Eze 16:49 (vc=33979, M08-E-VCG-01): Sodom's ease-grounded pride "did not aid the poor and needy" — sustained CHAR-5 establishes a settled inner posture of superiority that produces active neglect of the vulnerable; (c) the false security of structural height — Obd 3 (vc=65674, M08-E-VCG-02): "you who live in the clefts of the rock... who say in your heart, 'Who will bring me down?'" — the inner conviction of invulnerability.

---

##### T1.6.3 — Does the sustained effect differ from the immediate response — and if so, how?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes, significantly. The immediate response for the proud person is absent (T1.5.3 — CHAR-1 is self-concealing). The sustained effect is progressive and deepening. 2Ch 26:16 (vc=34044, M08-A1-VCG-01): Uzziah's pride "grew" as he became strong — progressive intensification without immediate resistance. The Eze 28 sequence (M08-A1-VCG-02) evidences the progression: initial heart-pride (v.2, vc=34040: "your heart is proud") → wisdom corruption (v.17, vc=34047: "you corrupted your wisdom for the sake of your splendour") → catastrophic public humiliation — a sequence that moves from an invisible inner condition to consequential collapse over time. The sustained effect is therefore more catastrophic than the immediate state: CHAR-1 is least dangerous in its initial appearance (when it is self-concealing) and most dangerous when it has established the four states above, by which point the person lacks the inner resources to recognise or resist it.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Yes. The immediate response is a single episode of the will boiling over (Deu 1:43: going up despite prohibition; Deu 18:20: speaking an unauthorised word). The sustained effect over time is the formation of a stable inner identity (the scoffer — Pro 21:24, vc=34096), a relational mode (strife and predation), and a deepening dispositional hardening (Neh 9:16 and 9:29: repeated presumption after repeated warning). The sustained effect is more comprehensive than the initial act: it moves from episodic act to settled character.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Yes. The immediate response to VCG-01 boasting may not register as problematic to the boaster (the premature glorifier of 1Ki 20:11 presumably feels confident, not troubled). The sustained effect is deeper corruption (1Cor 5:6: leaven spreading) and the eventual exposure of emptiness (2Cor 9:4, vc=33920: if the Macedonians find the Corinthians unprepared, the boast is exposed as empty). The sustained effect is more consequential — either confirmed integrity (for VCG-02) or exposed hollowness (for VCG-01).

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Yes. The immediate form of CHAR-4 may feel like confident knowledge or legitimate spiritual experience (1Cor 8:1, vc=33935: the person who "knows" feels competent; Col 2:18, vc=33941: the spiritual-experience inflation feels genuine). The sustained effect is comprehensive epistemic failure (1Ti 6:4: understanding nothing) and relational disorder (2Cor 12:20). The gap between the immediate experienced confidence and the sustained actual incompetence is what makes CHAR-4 dangerous: it feels like knowledge while producing blindness.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Yes. The immediate experience of CHAR-5 may feel like legitimate confidence in genuine structural goods (a nation's actual military strength, a person's actual wealth). The sustained effect is the deepening inner claim of self-sufficiency (Isa 47:8: "I am, and there is no one besides me") that detaches from God as the source of those goods. Eze 28:5 (vc=34046, M08-E-VCG-02): Tyre's wealth-induced pride evidences the progressive sequence: wealth gained → heart became proud — the sustained internal consequence is a deeply rooted inner arrogance that replaces appropriate gratitude with self-referential confidence.

---

#### T1.7 — Conditions of Reception

##### T1.7.1 — What inner conditions or orientations enable genuine reception of this characteristic?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The verse evidence evidences four enabling conditions. First, material prosperity or fullness: Deu 8:14 (vc=34223, M08-A1-VCG-01) — "when you have eaten and are full... then your heart will be lifted up"; Hos 13:6 (vc=34232, M08-A1-VCG-01) — "when they had grazed, they became full, they were filled, and their heart was lifted up." Second, the achievement of power or strength: 2Ch 26:16 (vc=34044, M08-A1-VCG-01) — "when he was strong, he grew proud." Third, impressive qualities such as beauty: Eze 28:17 (vc=34047, M08-A1-VCG-02) — "your heart was proud because of your beauty." Fourth, self-love as the generative root that underlies all the above: 2Ti 3:2 (vc=1899, M08-A4-VCG-01) — filautos heads the vice list from which arrogance and pride flow — the inward orientation toward the self as the root condition from which prosperity/power/beauty activate CHAR-1.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Three enabling conditions are evidenced. (a) Absence of God-directed fear: Psa 86:14 (vc=34097, M08-B-VCG-02) — "they do not set God before them"; 2Pe 2:10 (vc=42739, M08-B-VCG-03) — "they do not tremble before the glorious ones" — the removal of reverent fear enables CHAR-2's uninhibited self-assertion. (b) Contempt for divine law: Psa 119:21 (vc=34098, M08-B-VCG-02) — the arrogant "wander from your commandments"; Psa 119:85: "they do not live according to your law" — active rejection of the constraining framework. (c) Self-certainty in one's own authority: Obd 3 (vc=34108, M08-B-VCG-02) — arrogance "located in the heart as self-deceptive confidence in physical inaccessibility"; Jer 49:16 (vc=34115, M08-B-VCG-02): "the arrogance of your heart has deceived you" — a distorted inner self-assessment that overestimates one's own position and right.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

For VCG-01 condemned boasting: (a) alazoneia as the inner disposition — Jam 4:16 (vc=33866, M08-C-VCG-01): arrogance generates the boasting; (b) trust in creaturely assets — Psa 49:6 (vc=33355, M08-C-VCG-01): "those who trust in their wealth and boast of the abundance of their riches"; (c) worldly orientation — 1Jo 2:16 (vc=33865): "the pride of life is not from the Father but is from the world"; (d) self-origination illusion — 1Cor 4:7 (vc=33871): boasting as if gifts were not received — the failure to acknowledge the received quality of one's goods.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Four enabling conditions evidenced. (a) Received knowledge without love: 1Cor 8:1 (vc=33935, M08-D-VCG-01): "knowledge puffs up" — the reception of knowledge without the love-anchor inflates the cognitive self-picture. (b) Partisan tribal attachment: 1Cor 4:6 (vc=33937, M08-D-VCG-01): inflation "in favour of one against another" — competitive loyalty to a leader inflates the follower's own self-estimate. (c) Rapid elevation without formation: 1Ti 3:6 (vc=33924, M08-D-VCG-02): a new convert given leadership too quickly — insufficient formation for the cognitive demands of the role. (d) Ungrounded spiritual experience: Col 2:18 (vc=33941, M08-D-VCG-01): inflation "by his sensuous mind" without factual basis — sensory/visionary experience generating an inflated sense of spiritual standing.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Four enabling conditions evidenced. (a) Structural power or military might: Eze 30:6 (vc=33996, M08-E-VCG-01) — Egypt's military power as the ground; Lev 26:19 (vc=33982): Israel's structural power. (b) Material wealth generated by wisdom/trade: Eze 28:5 (vc=34046, M08-E-VCG-02): "your heart became proud" after wealth gained through wisdom. (c) Physical fortification / strategic elevation: Jer 49:16 (vc=34167); Obd 3 (vc=65674); Hab 2:9 (vc=34169, M08-E-VCG-02): holding fortified heights or building a secure stronghold. (d) Material ease and abundance: Eze 16:49 (vc=33979, M08-E-VCG-01): Sodom's "excess of food and prosperous ease"; Isa 47:8 (vc=9563): Babylon's love of pleasures.

---

##### T1.7.2 — What inner conditions block, distort, or prevent reception?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The verse evidence evidences three blocking conditions. First, deliberate inner self-lowering: Psa 131:1 (vc=34059, M08-A1-VCG-03; vc=34224, M08-A2-VCG-01) — "my heart is not lifted up; my eyes are not raised too high; I do not occupy myself with things too great and too marvelous for me" — the active, chosen restraint of the heart's and eyes' upward movement blocks CHAR-1's entry. Second, reverent fear of God: Rom 11:20 (vc=60876, M08-A4-VCG-01) — Paul warns against becoming high-minded and commands: "do not become proud, but fear" — the fear of God as the active counter-disposition that prevents elevation of self. Third, humility/lowliness of spirit (M09): Jam 4:6 (vc=33931, M08-A4-VCG-01); 1Pe 5:5 (vc=33934, M08-A4-VCG-01) — "God... gives grace to the humble" — the humble inner posture draws the opposite of what CHAR-1 draws (divine grace vs divine opposition).

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Two blocking conditions are explicitly evidenced. (a) Fear of God: Deu 17:13 (vc=34124, M08-B-VCG-01): "all the people shall hear and fear and not act presumptuously again" — fear of divine consequence blocks presumptuous re-offending; Psa 19:13 (vc=34095, M08-B-VCG-02): "keep back your servant also from presumptuous sins" — the servant's posture of seeking divine restraint is the blocking condition. (b) Submission to appointed authority: Tit 1:7 (vc=42740, M08-B-VCG-03): the overseer must not be authadēs (self-willed) — the blocking condition is the accepting of legitimate relational constraint.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

For VCG-01 blocked by: (a) acknowledgment of received goods — 1Cor 4:7 (vc=33871): if you know what you have was received, you cannot boast as if it was self-generated; (b) God-directed glorying — 1Cor 1:31 (vc=33878, M08-C-VCG-03): "let the one who boasts, boast in the Lord" — God-directed boasting displaces self-boasting; (c) the cross's evacuation of human credential-ground — Gal 6:14 (vc=33869, M08-C-VCG-02): the world crucified to Paul — all worldly boasting-grounds evacuated.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

(a) Love as the anchor for received knowledge: 1Cor 8:1 (vc=33935, M08-D-VCG-01): "love builds up" — love-directed cognition prevents knowledge from inflating the self; (b) Sober judgment within God-assigned measure: Rom 12:3 (vc=60866, M08-D-VCG-02): the commanded alternative — accurate self-assessment according to faith-measure; (c) Genuine formation before leadership elevation: 1Ti 3:6 (vc=33924) implies that adequate formation (not being a recent convert) prevents leadership-conceit.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

1Ti 6:17 (vc=60878, M08-E-VCG-02) provides the most direct evidence: "not to be haughty [hupsēlofroneō], nor to set their hopes on the uncertainty of riches, but on God, who richly provides everything to enjoy" — hope in God rather than in riches as the blocking condition. The structural equivalent for the national register is evidenced by contrast: Lev 26:19 (vc=33982) implies that Israel's pride would not have been broken if they had not relied on their power rather than on God. Acknowledging God as the source of all structural goods prevents CHAR-5 from generating.

---

##### T1.7.3 — What is the inner-being state of the person who encounters this characteristic but does not receive it?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Psa 131:1 (vc=34059, M08-A1-VCG-03; vc=34224, M08-A2-VCG-01) evidences the alternative inner-being state directly: "my heart is not lifted up; my eyes are not raised too high; I do not occupy myself with things too great and too marvelous for me" — a state of active, deliberate, calm self-lowering; the heart and eyes held below the level that CHAR-1 would occupy. Pro 29:23 (vc=33960, M08-A4-VCG-04) names the alternative state: "he who is lowly in spirit will obtain honour" — the inner posture of lowliness of spirit. Dan 4:37 (vc=34094, M08-A4-VCG-04) evidences the post-humbling alternative from the experiential inside: Nebuchadnezzar now "praises and extols and honours the King of heaven" — the God-directed inner orientation that follows CHAR-1's reversal. These are not passive states; the evidence shows them as actively held and deliberately maintained against CHAR-1's pull.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Psa 19:13 (vc=34095, M08-B-VCG-02) most directly evidences this: "keep back your servant also from presumptuous sins; let them not have dominion over me, then I shall be blameless" — the person who successfully resists CHAR-2 is the humble servant who actively seeks divine restraining grace, lives under God's authority, and thereby attains blamelessness. Psa 119:51 (vc=34099, M08-B-VCG-02): "the insolent utterly deride me, but I do not turn away from your law" — the person who encounters CHAR-2 from others but does not receive it holds steadfastly to the divine law that CHAR-2 despises, finding in that adherence the inner stability that CHAR-2 cannot overcome.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Gal 6:14 (vc=33869, M08-C-VCG-02) most directly evidences the alternative: "may I never boast except in the cross of our Lord Jesus Christ, by which the world has been crucified to me, and I to the world" — the person who does not receive VCG-01 boasting is the one for whom the cross has evacuated all worldly boasting-grounds. Phili 3:3 (vc=33879, M08-C-VCG-03): "worship by the Spirit of God and glory in Christ Jesus and put no confidence in the flesh" — the alternative inner state is wholly Christ-directed glorying with no self-directed alternative.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Rom 12:3 (vc=60866, M08-D-VCG-02) provides the positive alternative directly: "think of yourself with sober judgment, each according to the measure of faith that God has assigned" — the person who does not receive CHAR-4 is in a state of accurate, God-referenced self-assessment. 1Cor 8:1 (vc=33935, M08-D-VCG-01): "love builds up" — the alternative is the cognitive-social posture of love-directed, other-building engagement with knowledge.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

1Ti 6:17–18 (context of vc=60878, M08-E-VCG-02) evidences the alternative inner posture most directly: the wealthy person who does not develop hupsēlofroneō (CHAR-5) is one who places hope in God, is ready to give generously and share, and stores up treasure for the future. The alternative inner state is generous, God-directed stewardship — using received structural goods in service of others rather than as the ground for self-exaltation.

---

#### T1.8 — Dimension Classification

##### T1.8.1 — What is the primary inner-being dimension of this characteristic from the programme's dimension vocabulary?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The primary inner-being dimension is dispositional/volitional — CHAR-1 is a settled inner orientation of the self toward its own elevation, characterised by the will's agency. The dispositional classification is directly supported: Dan 4:37 (vc=34094, M08-A4-VCG-04): "those who walk in pride" — a habitual dispositional gait; Pro 16:5 (vc=12083, M08-A1-VCG-03): "everyone who is arrogant in heart" — a constitutive inner quality attributed universally to all who bear it. The volitional dimension is directly supported: Dan 11:36 (vc=34235, M08-A1-VCG-02): the king "exalts himself... by his own will" — the will as the driving agency; Isa 14:13 (vc=34233, M08-A4-VCG-05): "you said in your heart, 'I will ascend to heaven'" — the will's inner declaration as the core of CHAR-1 at its most extreme. The wisdom maxim pattern (Pro 16:18, vc=34073; Pro 29:23, vc=33960; Job 22:29, vc=34093, M08-A4-VCG-04) treats CHAR-1 as a stable inner characteristic with predictable causal consequences, which is the diagnostic marker of a dispositional rather than episodic phenomenon.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

The primary inner-being dimension is volitional — CHAR-2 is constitutively an act of the will's self-assertion against a known authority. The zid root (boiling, seething) directly names a volitional quality: the will's energised, forceful push against a limit. Deu 18:20 (vc=34119, M08-B-VCG-01): "presumes to speak" — the will authorising what is not authorised; Dan 11:36 (vc=34235, in CHAR-1 corpus — not cited here) and the parallel Deu 1:43 (vc=34123, M08-B-VCG-01): "you acted presumptuously and went up" — the will executing a prohibited action. Pro 21:24 (vc=34114, M08-B-VCG-02): "arrogance is the defining inner quality of the scoffer — the verse shows pride acting itself out with deliberate, premeditated force" — the deliberate quality is volitional at its core.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

The primary dimension is communicative/expressive — CHAR-3 is constitutively a speech-act and social-display phenomenon. Its vocabulary (kauchaomai: to boast, to exult aloud; ha.lal: to shine, to celebrate publicly) names acts of public assertion. This distinguishes CHAR-3 from CHAR-1 (dispositional) and CHAR-2 (volitional-transgressive): CHAR-3 is the outward-verbal expression that the other two characteristics generate. The alazoneia/alazōn terms (inner boasting disposition/braggart person-type) name the dispositional substrate but the characteristic itself is primarily the speech-act: Jam 4:16 (vc=33886, M08-C-VCG-01): "you boast [kauchaomai] in your arrogance. All such boasting is evil."

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

The primary inner-being dimension is cognitive/epistemic — CHAR-4 is constitutively a mental phenomenon, a false inner picture of the self. The froneō vocabulary (huperfroneō: Rom 12:3, vc=60866) directly names the thinking/mind faculty. The fusioō/tufoō inflation metaphors name cognitive states (the mind inflated beyond its actual content). This distinguishes CHAR-4 from all other M08 characteristics: CHAR-4 is the only characteristic primarily located in the cognitive/mind register rather than the dispositional (CHAR-1), volitional (CHAR-2), communicative (CHAR-3), or power-structural (CHAR-5) registers.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

The primary dimension is dispositional — CHAR-5 is a settled inner posture of power-grounded self-confidence and self-sufficiency. The ga.on proud-might vocabulary names both the inner confidence (dispositional) and its structural basis. Eze 33:28 (vc=33999, M08-E-VCG-01): "her proud might shall come to an end" — the proud might is a settled characteristic, not a momentary state. Isa 47:8 (vc=9563, M08-E-VCG-02): "you who say in your heart" — the self-sufficiency declaration is an inner dispositional claim, not an episodic response. CHAR-5 is the M08 characteristic that most extensively involves structural/collective subjects — entire nations (Egypt, Israel, Sodom, Babylon, Edom) are named as having CHAR-5 as their defining inner posture.

---

##### T1.8.2 — What evidence from the verse evidence supports this classification?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Four lines of evidence support the dispositional/volitional classification. First, the habitual-gait language: Dan 4:37 (vc=34094, M08-A4-VCG-04) — "those who walk in pride"; Isa 16:6 (vc=33943, M08-A4-VCG-04) — "how proud he is" — a reported settled characteristic. Second, the constitutive inner-quality language: Pro 16:5 (vc=12083, M08-A1-VCG-03) — "arrogant in heart... an abomination to the Lord" — CHAR-1 as a deep, constitutive inner condition; Mar 7:22 (vc=33928, M08-A4-VCG-01) — pride among the "evils that flow out of a person" — constitutively internal. Third, the universal-scope wisdom maxims: Pro 16:18 (vc=34073, M08-A1-VCG-03) — "pride goes before destruction" — stated as a structural law, not a situational observation; Job 33:17 (vc=34092, M08-A4-VCG-04) — God acts to "conceal pride from a man" — treating CHAR-1 as a persistent embedded disposition requiring active suppression. Fourth, the volitional-will language: Dan 11:36 (vc=34235, M08-A1-VCG-02) — the king exalts himself "by his own will" — the will as the constitutional driver.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

The zid vocabulary (M08-B-VCG-01) directly evidences the volitional dimension through its boiling-will root meaning. Deu 1:43 (vc=34123): "you acted presumptuously and went up" — wilful action against explicit prohibition. Deu 18:20 (vc=34119): "the prophet who presumes to speak" — the will claiming unauthorised speech-right. Exo 21:14 (vc=34122, M08-B-VCG-01): "willful, premeditated attack — a 'boiling' presumption in the will that plans cunning murder against a neighbour." Authadēs (Tit 1:7, vc=42740, M08-B-VCG-03): "self-willed — asserting one's own preferences without regard for legitimate authority or communal constraint." The will as primary constitutional driver is consistently evidenced across all three VCGs.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Kauchaomai is fundamentally a speech-act verb — to boast, to assert publicly, to exult in something before others. Pro 27:1 (vc=33359, M08-C-VCG-01): "do not boast about tomorrow" — boasting is addressed as a speech-act directed toward others. 1Ki 20:11 (vc=33353, M08-C-VCG-01): "let not him who puts on his armour boast" — prohibitive instruction about speech. 2Cor 10:13 (vc=33888, M08-C-VCG-02): Paul "constrains his boasting to the sphere God assigned" — boasting as a public act with geographic/relational scope. Rom 1:30 (vc=33867, M08-C-VCG-01): alazōn in a social-behaviour vice catalogue — the braggart's social presence as the characteristic's primary form.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Rom 12:3 (vc=60866, M08-D-VCG-02): huperfroneō — the thinking faculty addressed directly. 1Ti 6:4 (vc=33925, M08-D-VCG-02): conceit paired with "understanding nothing" — the epistemic failure confirms the cognitive register. Col 2:18 (vc=33941, M08-D-VCG-01): "inflated by his sensuous mind [nous]" — nous (mind) explicitly named as the seat of the inflation. 1Cor 8:1 (vc=33935, M08-D-VCG-01): knowledge inflating — the cognitive content of knowledge is what inflates.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Ga.on proud-might in the national register (Eze 30:6, vc=33996; 30:18, vc=33997; 32:12, vc=33998; 33:28, vc=33999) consistently names a settled collective dispositional inner confidence — "Egypt's proud might" — as a known, characteristic quality of the nation. Eze 16:49 (vc=33979, M08-E-VCG-01): Sodom's pride as its "root sin" — a dispositional characteristic generating the community's other failures. Isa 47:8 (vc=9563, M08-E-VCG-02): "you who say in your heart" — the internal declaration of self-sufficiency as a settled inner posture.

---

##### T1.8.3 — Does this characteristic carry secondary dimensions — and if so, what are they, and do they compete with the primary classification?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes, secondary dimensions are evidenced. Cognitive/perceptual: Psa 10:4 (vc=34074, M08-A2-VCG-02) — pride closes the perceptive faculty for God ("all his thoughts are, 'there is no God'"); Eze 28:17 (vc=34047, M08-A1-VCG-02) — pride corrupts wisdom (the highest cognitive faculty). Relational: Deu 17:20 (vc=34231, M08-A1-VCG-01) — the king's heart lifted "above his brothers" — CHAR-1 as inherently comparative and relational in its elevation; Psa 123:4 (vc=33953, M08-A4-VCG-03) — contempt's relational impact. Motivational/agency: Psa 10:2 (vc=33963, M08-A4-VCG-03) — "in arrogance the wicked hotly pursue the poor" — CHAR-1 generating energised predatory agency. These secondary dimensions do not compete with the dispositional/volitional primary: they are expressions of the dispositional core through different inner-being faculties. CHAR-1 begins as a disposition in the heart and will, then manifests through cognitive distortion (second), relational damage (third), and energised agency (fourth).

---

## T2 — Constitutional Location and Movement (31 prompts)

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Yes. Relational dimension: CHAR-2 is inherently relational — it requires an authority to defy and consistently generates strife (Pro 13:10, vc=34113, M08-B-VCG-02), contempt (Psa 119:51, vc=34099), and predatory oppression (Psa 119:85, vc=34102) in the relational field. Cognitive dimension: CHAR-2 involves self-deceptive miscalculation — Obd 3 (vc=34108, M08-B-VCG-02): "arrogance located in the heart as self-deceptive confidence in physical inaccessibility" — the person misjudges their actual exposure to divine judgment; Mal 3:15 (vc=34106, M08-B-VCG-02): the arrogant "seem to prosper" in the observers' perception, a cognitive distortion. These secondary dimensions (relational and cognitive) complement the primary volitional dimension without displacing it.
