## T2 — Constitutional Location and Movement (31 prompts)

---

### T2

#### T2.1 — Spirit-Level Location

##### T2.1.1 — Is this characteristic explicitly located at the spirit level in the verse evidence?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes. Three verses explicitly name the spirit as a location of CHAR-1. Pro 16:18 (vc=34073, M08-A1-VCG-03): "Pride goes before destruction, and a haughty spirit before a fall" — go.vah here names the spirit (ruach) in its haughty elevation as the immediate precursor to collapse. Ecc 7:8 (vc=12087, M08-A4-VCG-04): "the patient in spirit is better than the proud in spirit" — pride and patience placed as two contrasting orientations of the spirit, confirming CHAR-1 as operable at the spirit level. Dan 5:20 (vc=34129, M08-A1-VCG-02): "when his heart was lifted up and his spirit was hardened so that he dealt proudly, he was brought down from his kingly throne" — heart and spirit operating simultaneously in the production of Belshazzar's CHAR-1, with the spirit's hardening paired with the heart's elevation as the constitutional location of the pride that caused his deposition.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (S)

The verse evidence in §3.A does not explicitly name the spirit (ruach) as the location of CHAR-2. The closest evidential language is the stiff neck idiom: Neh 9:16 (vc=34120, M08-B-VCG-01) — "they acted presumptuously and stiffened their neck" — which in the Hebrew anthropological tradition implies a hardening of the deep inner person, but this is not a direct spirit-level naming. The spirit as a distinct constitutional location is not evidenced in the 45-verse §3.A corpus for CHAR-2.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (S)

The verse evidence in §3.B does not explicitly name the spirit (ruach/pneuma) as the constitutional location of CHAR-3. The alazoneia/alazōn terms (inner boasting disposition) are not specifically assigned to the spirit level in the evidence. The spirit-level location is not evidenced.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

The verse evidence in §3.C does not explicitly name the spirit (ruach/pneuma) as the constitutional location of CHAR-4. The 12 verses address the cognitive/mind register (fusioō, tufoō, huperfroneō, nous in Col 2:18) rather than the spirit specifically.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (S)

The verse evidence in §3.D does not explicitly name the spirit (ruach) as the constitutional location of CHAR-5. The 17 verses address primarily the heart and the structural/collective register rather than the spirit specifically.

---

##### T2.1.2 — Does the evidence indicate that this characteristic originates in or is primarily a spirit-level phenomenon?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The evidence does not indicate that CHAR-1 originates primarily at the spirit level. The heart is named far more frequently as the constitutional seat (M08-A1: 30 verses with explicit heart-location, compared to three spirit-level references). The spirit-level evidence (Pro 16:18, vc=34073; Ecc 7:8, vc=12087; Dan 5:20, vc=34129) is complementary — naming the spirit as a site where CHAR-1 also registers — rather than primary. Dan 5:20 (vc=34129, M08-A1-VCG-02) is the most instructive: it presents heart-lifting and spirit-hardening as simultaneous co-occurrents, not as a spirit-origin generating a secondary heart-manifestation. The evidence supports CHAR-1 as a phenomenon primarily headquartered in the heart, with secondary extension to the spirit.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (S)

The evidence is silent on spirit-level origination for CHAR-2. The will (volitional faculty) is the primary named constitutional driver, not the spirit. The stiff-neck idiom (Neh 9:16, vc=34120, M08-B-VCG-01; Neh 9:29, vc=34126) may carry spirit-level resonances within the broader constitutional framework but is not named as such within §3.A.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (S)

The evidence does not indicate spirit-level origination. The primary constitutional substrate evidenced is the inner disposition (alazoneia), the cognitive self-assessment process (2Cor 10:12), and the heart's orientational state (2Cor 5:12, vc=33872). Not spirit-level.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

No evidence of spirit-level origination. CHAR-4 originates in the cognitive/mind faculty — Col 2:18 (vc=33941, M08-D-VCG-01): "inflated by his sensuous mind [nous]" — the mind is the named origin-site.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (S)

No evidence of spirit-level origination. CHAR-5 originates in the heart (Eze 28:5; Eze 16:30; Isa 47:8), activated by external structural goods.

---

##### T2.1.3 — What does spirit-level location reveal about the nature and depth of this characteristic?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Spirit-level location in Pro 16:18 (vc=34073, M08-A1-VCG-03) and Dan 5:20 (vc=34129, M08-A1-VCG-02) reveals that CHAR-1 reaches to the deepest constitutional level of the human person — the spirit as the innermost register. This deepens the finding beyond a merely cognitive or emotional phenomenon: pride in the spirit (Ecc 7:8, vc=12087, M08-A4-VCG-04) names an orientation at the person's deepest relational capacity. Dan 5:20's pairing of spirit-hardening with heart-lifting suggests that CHAR-1 at its most entrenched involves simultaneous engagement at both levels — the heart as the seat of the conscious self-elevation and the spirit as the deepened hardening that makes reversal increasingly resistant.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (S)

Given the silence on spirit-level location (T2.1.1–2), this prompt cannot be answered from the evidence. The absence of explicit spirit-level naming in §3.A may indicate that CHAR-2 operates primarily at the volitional level (constitutionally shallower than the spirit, or at least named at a different constitutional register than the spirit).

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (S)

Given the silence on spirit-level location (T2.1.1–2), this prompt cannot be answered from the evidence. CHAR-3 appears to operate primarily at the communicative/expressive and dispositional levels rather than the deepest spirit level.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

Given the silence on spirit-level location (T2.1.1–2), this prompt cannot be answered from the evidence. CHAR-4 appears to operate at the cognitive/mind level rather than the deepest spirit level.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (S)

Given the silence on spirit-level location (T2.1.1–2), this prompt cannot be answered from the evidence. CHAR-5 appears to operate primarily at the heart/dispositional level.

---

##### T2.1.4 — If the evidence is silent on spirit-level location, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The evidence is not silent: spirit-level location is confirmed in Pro 16:18 (vc=34073), Ecc 7:8 (vc=12087), and Dan 5:20 (vc=34129). This prompt is closed by T2.1.1–3.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (S)

The verse evidence is silent on explicit spirit-level location for CHAR-2. Confirmed.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (S)

The verse evidence in §3.B is silent on explicit spirit-level location for CHAR-3. Confirmed.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

The verse evidence is silent on explicit spirit-level location for CHAR-4. Confirmed.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (S)

The verse evidence is silent on explicit spirit-level location for CHAR-5. Confirmed.

---

#### T2.2 — Soul-Level Location

##### T2.2.1 — Is this characteristic identified in the verse evidence as a soul-level phenomenon?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (S)

The verse evidence does not locate CHAR-1 constitutionally in the soul (nephesh). The four §3 occurrences of soul-language are all in the perspective of CHAR-1's victims: Jer 13:17 (vc=34091, M08-A3-VCG-03) — the prophet's soul weeps over the people's pride; Psa 13:2 (vc=34241, M08-A4-VCG-03) — the psalmist takes counsel in his soul and has sorrow in his heart as the experience of being dominated by an enemy's exaltation; Psa 123:4 (vc=33953, M08-A4-VCG-03) — the soul overwhelmed by the contempt of the proud. In each case, soul-language describes the inner experience of those crushed by CHAR-1, not the constitutional location of CHAR-1 in its possessor. The proud person's soul is not named as the seat of their pride. This is noted as a silence.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (S)

The verse evidence does not explicitly locate CHAR-2 in the soul (nephesh). No verse in §3.A names the soul as the constitutional seat of presumptuous defiance.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Partially. Psa 10:3 (vc=33354, M08-C-VCG-01): "the wicked person boasts of what his own soul [nephesh] desires" — the soul's desires are named as the object and generative ground of the boast. The soul (nephesh) here is the seat of the desires that CHAR-3 then publicly asserts. This is not CHAR-3 located in the soul as its constitutional seat, but the soul's desires as the content that CHAR-3 voices.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

The verse evidence does not explicitly locate CHAR-4 in the soul (nephesh/psychē). The psychological vocabulary in §3.C (nous, froneō) specifically addresses the mind/cognitive faculty rather than the soul as a distinct location.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (S)

The verse evidence does not explicitly locate CHAR-5 in the soul (nephesh) within §3.D. The primary named location is the heart (lev).

---

##### T2.2.2 — What does soul-level location reveal about this characteristic's place in the innermost personal experience?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (S)

Since the verse evidence is silent on CHAR-1 being constitutionally located in the soul of its possessor, this prompt cannot be answered from evidence. The significance of the silence remains uncertain within the programme's constitutional framework — the evidence may simply not happen to use nephesh in describing the proud person's inner constitution, without that absence being analytically determinative about CHAR-1's depth of penetration into the soul. What can be noted is that the evidence consistently uses lev (heart) and ruach (spirit) rather than nephesh when naming CHAR-1's constitutional seat.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (S)

The evidence is silent on soul-level location. The significance of this absence is uncertain — CHAR-2 may penetrate to soul depth through the will's volitional acts without being explicitly named at that level in this corpus.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Psa 10:3 (vc=33354, M08-C-VCG-01): "boasts of what his own soul desires" — the connection between soul-level desires and the boasting act reveals that CHAR-3 is the public assertion of what the soul privately craves. The soul's desires become the boasting-content; CHAR-3 is the soul's cravings seeking social validation and public acknowledgment. This reveals CHAR-3 as a bridge between inner-soul desire and outer-speech assertion.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

The evidence is silent on soul-level location. See T2.2.1.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (S)

Silent. See T2.2.1.

---

##### T2.2.3 — If the evidence is silent on soul-level location, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (S)

The verse evidence is silent on CHAR-1 being constitutionally located in the soul (nephesh/psychē) of its possessor. Confirmed.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (S)

The verse evidence is silent on explicit soul-level location for CHAR-2. Confirmed.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Partial soul-level connection evidenced in Psa 10:3 (vc=33354) — the soul's desires as boasting-content. Not fully silent.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

The verse evidence is silent on explicit soul-level location for CHAR-4. Confirmed.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (S)

The verse evidence is silent on explicit soul-level location for CHAR-5. Confirmed.

---

#### T2.3 — Heart

##### T2.3.1 — Does the verse evidence locate this characteristic in the heart?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes, extensively. M08-A1 (30 verses) was constituted specifically by the heart-location of CHAR-1. The evidence ranges across: Pro 16:5 (vc=12083, M08-A1-VCG-03) — "Everyone who is arrogant in heart is an abomination to the Lord"; Eze 28:2 (vc=34040, M08-A1-VCG-02) — "your heart is proud, and you have said, 'I am a god'"; Pro 18:12 (vc=34041, M08-A1-VCG-03) — "Before destruction a man's heart is haughty"; Jer 49:16 (vc=34054, M08-A1-VCG-03) — "the pride of your heart... I will bring you down"; Jer 48:29 (vc=34603, M08-A1-VCG-03) — Moab's haughtiness "explicitly located in Moab's heart, identifying pride's constitutional seat as the inner person"; Luk 1:51 (vc=33930, M08-A1-VCG-03) — God "scattered the proud in the thoughts of their hearts"; Dan 11:12 (vc=34234, M08-A1-VCG-02) — "his heart shall be exalted"; Dan 5:20 (vc=34129, M08-A1-VCG-02) — "his heart was lifted up." The heart is the most-evidenced constitutional seat of CHAR-1 across the entire 149-verse corpus.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Yes. Three verses explicitly name the heart as CHAR-2's location. 1Sa 17:28 (vc=34112, M08-B-VCG-02): Eliab accuses David of "the arrogance of your heart" (za.don) — locating presumptuous insolence in the heart as an inner disposition. Obd 3 (vc=34108, M08-B-VCG-02): "arrogance is explicitly located in the heart and described as self-deceptive; the inner conviction of invulnerability that pride has planted in the heart." Jer 49:16 (vc=34115, M08-B-VCG-02): "arrogance of your heart has deceived you" — the heart is the seat of the self-deceptive CHAR-2 impulse. The heart-location evidence is primarily in the za.don/zed register (M08-B-VCG-02) rather than in the zid-boiling register (M08-B-VCG-01), suggesting that the heart names the dispositional substrate of CHAR-2, while the will names its active expression.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Yes. 2Cor 5:12 (vc=33872, M08-C-VCG-02): Paul contrasts "boasting about outward appearance" with "what is in the heart" — the heart is named as the authentic interior ground that genuine boasting should reference, against which outward-appearance boasting is measured. Psa 52:1 (vc=33343, M08-C-VCG-01): "boasting of evil" is the "proud inner posture of a powerful person whose will is directed toward harm; it is set against God's steadfast love" — the boast in evil is a heart-posture. The heart is the interior ground from which CHAR-3 either emerges (VCG-01 prideful heart) or to which it appeals (VCG-02 conscience-grounded boasting).

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

The verse evidence does not explicitly name the heart (lev/kardia) as CHAR-4's constitutional seat in §3.C. The vocabulary consistently addresses the mind/cognitive faculty (froneō, nous, fusioō) rather than the heart specifically. CHAR-4 is the cognitive register of pride; the heart is CHAR-1's primary seat.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Yes. Eze 28:5 (vc=34046, M08-E-VCG-02): "your heart became proud" — the heart is the explicit named seat of the pride generated by wealth. Eze 16:30 (vc=57959, M08-E-VCG-02): "how sick is your heart, declares the Lord God, that you did all these things, the deeds of a brazen prostitute" — the imperious self-will (shal.le.tet) is located in a sick heart. Isa 47:8 (vc=9563, M08-E-VCG-02): "you who say in your heart, 'I am, and there is no one besides me'" — the self-sufficiency declaration originates in the heart. Obd 3 (vc=65674, M08-E-VCG-02): "the pride of your heart has deceived you" — heart as the seat of the self-deceptive CHAR-5.

---

##### T2.3.2 — What does the heart-location reveal — what aspect of the heart's integrating function (knowing, willing, feeling, moral awareness) does this characteristic engage?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Heart-location engages multiple aspects of the heart's integrating function. Volitional: Dan 11:36 (vc=34235, M08-A1-VCG-02) — the king exalts himself "by his own will"; Isa 14:13 (vc=34233, M08-A4-VCG-05) — "you said in your heart, 'I will ascend to heaven'" — the heart as the seat of volitional self-declaration. Cognitive/knowing: Jer 48:29 (vc=34603, M08-A1-VCG-03) — pride is the "culminating inner attitude in a list of pride's expressions," the heart naming the identity-claim; Eze 28:17 (vc=34047, M08-A1-VCG-02) — pride in the heart corrupts wisdom — the heart's discernment function is distorted. Moral assessment: Pro 16:5 (vc=12083, M08-A1-VCG-03) — "an abomination to the Lord" — the heart's moral condition evaluated by God as abomination. Identity formation: Eze 28:2 (vc=34040, M08-A1-VCG-02) — "your heart is proud, and you have said, 'I am a god'" — the heart as the seat of the most fundamental self-understanding, CHAR-1 distorting it into a claim of divine status.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Heart-location engages the heart's self-assessment function: Obd 3 (vc=34108, M08-B-VCG-02) — "inner conviction of invulnerability that pride has planted in the heart" — the heart's self-evaluative capacity is distorted by CHAR-2 into a false assessment of the self's power and safety. Jer 49:16 (vc=34115, M08-B-VCG-02) — "the arrogance of your heart has deceived you" — the heart's directional knowledge function is corrupted by CHAR-2 into self-deception. 1Sa 17:28 (vc=34112) — "arrogance and evil of heart together" — the heart as the seat of morally disordered disposition. CHAR-2 in the heart engages the heart's knowing/assessment faculty, distorting it into overconfidence in the self's autonomy.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Heart-location reveals that CHAR-3 has two distinct relationships to the heart: in its condemned form (VCG-01), the heart's prideful orientation (CHAR-1 substrate) generates CHAR-3's self-directed boasting; in its examined form (VCG-02), the heart's integrity and conscience are the ground of legitimate self-commendation (2Cor 1:12, vc=33912: "the testimony of our conscience"). The heart is CHAR-3's interior origin-point for its condemned form and its integrity-ground for its examined form.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

The silence on heart-location for CHAR-4 is analytically significant: it confirms CHAR-4's distinctive constitutional location in the cognitive/mind register, distinguishing it from CHAR-1 (whose primary seat is the heart). The mind (nous) and the cognitive thinking-faculty (froneō) are CHAR-4's named locations, not the heart.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Heart-location reveals that CHAR-5's structural-power medium (wealth, might, height) generates an inner heart-level pride that is constitutionally located at the same depth as CHAR-1's dispositional self-elevation. Eze 28:5 (vc=34046, M08-E-VCG-02): the wealth-triggered heart-pride confirms that CHAR-5 follows CHAR-1's constitutional location (heart) while being distinguished by the specific medium (structural goods) that triggers it. The heart is the seat of the inner pride that the structural goods generate; without the structural goods, the heart-pride of CHAR-5 specifically would not have been triggered.

---

##### T2.3.3 — If the evidence is silent on heart-location, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Heart-location is extensively confirmed across 30 verses in M08-A1. Not silent.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Heart-location is confirmed in three verses (1Sa 17:28, Obd 3, Jer 49:16). Not silent.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Heart-location evidenced (2Cor 5:12; Psa 52:1). Not silent.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

The verse evidence is silent on explicit heart-location for CHAR-4. The mind is the named location (Col 2:18; Rom 12:3). Confirmed.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Heart-location confirmed in four verses (Eze 28:5; Eze 16:30; Isa 47:8; Obd 3). Not silent.

---

#### T2.4 — Mind

##### T2.4.1 — Does the verse evidence locate this characteristic in the mind?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes, in the NT vocabulary specifically. Luk 1:51 (vc=33930, M08-A1-VCG-03): "he has scattered the proud in the thoughts of their hearts" — the Greek dianoiai (thoughts, mind) explicitly names the cognitive-mental faculty as the location of the arrogant self-elevation. Psa 10:4 (vc=34074, M08-A2-VCG-02): "the wicked does not seek him; all his thoughts are, 'there is no God'" — pride operates in the thought-life, restructuring the entire cognitive content away from God. Rom 12:16 (vc=60877, M08-A4-VCG-01): "Do not be haughty, but associate with the lowly. Never be wise in your own sight" — the cognitive self-assessment faculty named as the specific location of the mind-form of CHAR-1.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Partially. Psa 86:14 (vc=34097, M08-B-VCG-02): "they do not set God before them" — the cognitive-evaluative act of positioning God in the mind's awareness is absent; the mind's reference point has excluded God. Luk 3:8 (vc=55578, M08-B-VCG-03): "do not begin to say within yourselves, 'We have Abraham as our father'" — the inner speech of presumptuous ancestral claim involves a cognitive-mind process of self-justification. The mind-location evidence is indirect and limited compared to the heart and will evidence.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Yes, indirectly. 2Cor 10:12 (context of M08-C-VCG-02): "not dare to classify or compare ourselves with some of those who are commending themselves. But when they measure themselves by one another and compare themselves with one another, they are without understanding" — the cognitive process of self-comparison and self-measurement is named as the epistemic mechanism of CHAR-3; its absence of "understanding" is a mind-level failure. 1Cor 4:7 (vc=33871, M08-C-VCG-01): "why do you boast as if you did not receive it?" — a cognitive failure of attribution, a mind-level miscalculation about the origin of one's capacities.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Yes — explicitly and primarily. Col 2:18 (vc=33941, M08-D-VCG-01): "inflated [fusioō] by his sensuous mind [nous tēs sarkos — mind of the flesh]" — nous (the mind) is directly named as the seat of CHAR-4's inflation. Rom 12:3 (vc=60866, M08-D-VCG-02): "do not think [huperfroneō] of yourself more highly than you ought, but think [froneō] with sober judgment" — the froneō faculty (thinking, mind-setting) is addressed. 1Ti 6:4 (vc=33925, M08-D-VCG-02): conceit paired with "understanding nothing [mēden epistamenos]" — the epistemic/knowing faculty. The mind is CHAR-4's primary constitutional seat.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Partially. Isa 47:8 (vc=9563, M08-E-VCG-02): "you who say in your heart, 'I am, and there is no one besides me'" — the heart-declaration of self-completeness involves a cognitive self-assessment that names oneself as ontologically self-sufficient. This is a cognitive claim (about the nature of one's own existence) as well as a dispositional assertion. Obd 3 (vc=65674, M08-E-VCG-02): "the pride of your heart has deceived you" — a cognitive self-deception (parallel to CHAR-4's Col 2:18 "without factual basis" inflation).

---

##### T2.4.2 — What does mind-location reveal — what aspect of the mind's function (thought, discernment, understanding) does this characteristic engage?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Mind-location reveals that CHAR-1 operates in the cognitive faculty primarily through distorted self-assessment — the mind evaluating the self as above others or above God. Psa 10:4 (vc=34074, M08-A2-VCG-02): pride restructures the cognitive content so completely that "all his thoughts are, 'there is no God'" — CHAR-1 in the mind produces a total reorientation of the cognitive field, displacing God from the inner horizon and replacing him with the self's own self-sufficient assessment. Eze 28:17 (vc=34047, M08-A1-VCG-02): "you corrupted your wisdom for the sake of your splendour" — CHAR-1 damages the mind's highest function (wisdom/discernment). Luk 1:51 (vc=33930, M08-A1-VCG-03): arrogance located in the "thoughts" confirms the cognitive register — CHAR-1 is not merely a feeling or impulse but a structured pattern of self-elevating thought.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

The partial mind-location evidence reveals that CHAR-2 involves a cognitive distortion of the self's actual standing: Obd 3 (vc=34108, M08-B-VCG-02) and Jer 49:16 (vc=34115, M08-B-VCG-02) both name "self-deception" as the cognitive consequence of CHAR-2's heart-location — the mind evaluates the self as secure when it is not. Psa 86:14 (vc=34097): the mind's failure to "set God before" it means CHAR-2 operates in a cognitive vacuum where divine authority is absent from the inner perceptual field.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Mind-location reveals that CHAR-3 requires a cognitive process (self-assessment, self-comparison, attribution) to generate its content. The boaster's cognitive faculty evaluates the self as worth boasting about — a specific cognitive act of self-assessment that produces the content of the boast. The failure of this cognitive process (lack of understanding in self-comparison; misattribution of received goods as self-generated) is what makes the VCG-01 boast morally wrong.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Mind-location reveals that CHAR-4 is constitutively an epistemic failure: the mind's self-assessment function is the specific faculty that CHAR-4 distorts. Col 2:18 (vc=33941): "his sensuous mind" — the mind in its fleshly orientation inflates without factual basis. Rom 12:3 (vc=60866): "think with sober judgment, each according to the measure of faith" — the commanded alternative identifies accurate cognitive self-referencing as what CHAR-4 denies. CHAR-4 engages the mind's self-assessment, self-comparison, and self-definition functions — the very faculties that should produce accurate self-knowledge.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

The partial mind-location evidence reveals that CHAR-5's structural-power medium generates a specific cognitive claim of self-sufficiency: the nation or person with structural power makes an inner cognitive assessment of themselves as complete, secure, and above external threat (Obd 3: "who will bring me down?"). This cognitive claim is the mind-level expression of CHAR-5's heart-level pride — and like CHAR-4's fusioō, it is self-deceptive (Obd 3: "the pride of your heart has deceived you").

---

##### T2.4.3 — If the evidence is silent on mind-location, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Mind-location is confirmed in Luk 1:51 (vc=33930), Psa 10:4 (vc=34074), and Rom 12:16 (vc=60877). Not silent.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Partial mind-location evidenced (cognitive self-deception, God-displaced from inner reference). Not fully silent.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Mind-location evidenced via self-comparison/self-assessment mechanism (2Cor 10:12; 1Cor 4:7). Not silent.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Mind-location extensively confirmed (Col 2:18; Rom 12:3; 1Ti 6:4). Not silent.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Partial mind-location evidenced via the cognitive self-sufficiency claim (Isa 47:8; Obd 3). Not fully silent.

---

#### T2.5 — Other Soul Subsets

##### T2.5.1 — Does the verse evidence surface any soul-level location beyond heart and mind for this characteristic?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes — the spirit (ruach), as confirmed in T2.1. Pro 16:18 (vc=34073, M08-A1-VCG-03): "a haughty spirit before a fall"; Ecc 7:8 (vc=12087, M08-A4-VCG-04): "proud in spirit" contrasted with "patient in spirit"; Dan 5:20 (vc=34129, M08-A1-VCG-02): spirit hardening alongside heart lifting. No additional soul-level locations beyond heart, mind, and spirit are evidenced in §3.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (S)

No additional soul-level location beyond heart and the will's volitional register is evidenced in §3.A. The spirit and soul are not explicitly named as CHAR-2's constitutional seats in this corpus.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (S)

No additional soul-level location beyond the soul-desires connection (T2.2) and heart/mind is evidenced in §3.B.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

No additional soul-level location beyond the mind is evidenced in §3.C. The spirit and soul are not explicitly named as CHAR-4's locations; the mind (nous, froneō) is the exclusive named constitutional seat.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (S)

No additional soul-level location beyond the heart is evidenced in §3.D. The spirit and soul are not explicitly named.

---

##### T2.5.2 — If so, what is that location, and what does it reveal?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The spirit-location (confirmed T2.1) reveals that CHAR-1 penetrates to the deepest constitutional stratum of the person. Ecc 7:8 (vc=12087, M08-A4-VCG-04) most directly names the spirit as the seat of a dispositional orientation: "proud in spirit" vs "patient in spirit" — two contrasting fundamental orientations at the spirit level. Dan 5:20 (vc=34129, M08-A1-VCG-02) reveals the most entrenched form of CHAR-1: simultaneous heart-lifting and spirit-hardening, producing the behavioural pattern that led directly to Belshazzar's deposition. The spirit-level location confirms that CHAR-1 is not a surface phenomenon of the outer person but can reach the innermost constitutional depth.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (S)

No additional soul-level location evidenced. See T2.5.1.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (S)

No additional soul-level location evidenced. See T2.5.1.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

No additional soul-level location evidenced. CHAR-4 is constitutionally headquartered in the mind/cognitive faculty alone within §3.C.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (S)

No additional soul-level location evidenced. See T2.5.1.

---

##### T2.5.3 — If the evidence is silent, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Spirit-level location is confirmed. Not silent.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (S)

No additional soul-level location beyond heart evidenced. Confirmed.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (S)

No additional soul-level location beyond heart and soul-desires (Psa 10:3) evidenced. Confirmed.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

No additional soul-level location beyond the mind evidenced. Confirmed.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (S)

No additional soul-level location beyond heart evidenced. Confirmed.

---

#### T2.6 — Body — Significance

##### T2.6.1 — Does the verse evidence link this characteristic to a specific body part?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes, extensively. M08-A2 (11 verses) was constituted by body-part links to CHAR-1. Body parts named: Eyes — Pro 6:17 (vc=34247, M08-A2-VCG-01): "haughty eyes" as first in the list of what God hates; Pro 30:13 (vc=34249, M08-A2-VCG-01): "how lofty are their eyes, how high their eyelids lift"; Psa 18:27 (vc=34242, M08-A2-VCG-01): "the haughty eyes you bring down"; Isa 5:15 (vc=12088, M08-A2-VCG-01): "the eyes of the haughty are brought low." Face/posture — Psa 10:4 (vc=34074, M08-A2-VCG-02): "in the pride of his face the wicked does not seek him." Head — Job 10:16 (vc=33945, M08-A2-VCG-02): "were my head lifted up, you would hunt me like a lion." Neck — Psa 75:5 (vc=34165, M08-A4-VCG-05): "speak with haughty neck." Hand — 1Ki 11:26 (vc=34237, M08-A1-VCG-02): "lifted up his hand against the king." Body-bearing (neck, gait, posture) — Isa 3:16 (vc=34052, M08-A2-VCG-02): daughters of Zion's "outstretched necks, glancing wantonly with their eyes, mincing along as they go."

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Yes. Neh 9:16 (vc=34120, M08-B-VCG-01) and Neh 9:29 (vc=34126, M08-B-VCG-01): "they stiffened their neck" — the neck as the body part that expresses CHAR-2's inner resistance to God's authority; the stiff neck is a somatic indicator of the will's refusal to submit. Exo 21:14 (vc=34122, M08-B-VCG-01): "willful, premeditated attack... plans cunning murder against a neighbour" — the hand as the instrument of CHAR-2's lethal expression. Deu 1:43 (vc=34123, M08-B-VCG-01): "you went up into the hill country" — bodily movement (going up) as the physical expression of the will's presumptuous act.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Yes — the mouth as the primary body-part link. CHAR-3 is primarily a speech-act characteristic; the mouth is its constitutional bodily instrument. The kauchaomai vocabulary presupposes verbal expression. Jer 9:23 (vc=33342, M08-C-VCG-01): the prohibitions against boasting in wisdom, might, and wealth are all speech-act prohibitions — "let not the wise man boast" implies verbal boasting. 1Sa 2:3 context (adjacent to CHAR-2 corpus): "talk no more so very proudly, let not arrogance come from your mouth" — the mouth as the vehicle of proud speech/boasting. CHAR-3's body-part link is to the mouth as the instrument of the speech-act.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

The verse evidence in §3.C does not link CHAR-4 to a specific body part. The characteristic operates entirely in the cognitive/mental register without named body-part expression. Unlike CHAR-1 (which has M08-A2's haughty-eyes body-part register), CHAR-4 is an inner cognitive phenomenon with no evidenced body-part link in §3.C.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Not to an individual body part (eyes, neck, hand) as in CHAR-1's M08-A2, but to spatial/physical elevation as CHAR-5's structural expression. The ma.rom (H4791) vocabulary names physical height as the medium of CHAR-5: Jer 49:16 (vc=34167, M08-E-VCG-02): holding a "high hill" as a physical possession; Obd 3 (vc=65674): "you who live in the clefts of the rock, in your lofty dwelling"; Hab 2:9 (vc=34169): "setting his nest on high." Eze 19:11 (vc=54398, M08-E-VCG-02): qo.mah (height) — "towering stature" as the metaphorical-physical expression of CHAR-5. Physical height and architectural elevation are the structural body-analogues for CHAR-5 at the national-positional level.

---

##### T2.6.2 — If so, what is Scripture doing by making that link — is it emphatic, functional, expressive, indicative, or mediating?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The body-part links are consistently expressive and indicative: the bodily register makes visible the inner pride that the heart and spirit hold. Pro 6:17 (vc=34247, M08-A2-VCG-01) — "haughty eyes... an outward expression of an inward elevation of self that God finds abominable" — the eye-link is expressive: it renders CHAR-1 visible and morally legible for divine assessment and judgment. Isa 2:11 (vc=34089, M08-A2-VCG-01) — "the haughty looks of man shall be brought low" — the looks both express the inner disposition and become the specific target of divine judgment, functioning as indicators of what is being addressed. Isa 3:16 (vc=34052, M08-A2-VCG-02) — "outstretched necks... wanton glances... mincing along" — the body in motion as the full indicative display of the inner haughtiness. The body-part links do not mediate CHAR-1 into the person; they express and indicate it outward.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

The stiff-neck body-part link is expressive and indicative: the neck's stiffening is how CHAR-2's inner resistance to divine authority becomes physically visible and narratively legible. Neh 9:16 (vc=34120, M08-B-VCG-01): "stiffened their neck" pairs with "acted presumptuously" as the somatic expression of the inner volitional refusal. The body-part links in §3.A function as indicators — making the inner will's defiant orientation readable through a physical sign (the stiff neck), a physical action (going up to battle), or a physical instrument (the hand in murder). The bodily expression confirms that CHAR-2 is not merely a cognitive position but a willed act that moves into physical space.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

The mouth-link is functional: CHAR-3 requires speech to be expressed; the boast that remains interior is not yet CHAR-3 in its characteristic form — it becomes CHAR-3 when it is given voice. The mouth-link makes CHAR-3 accountable and addressable: what comes from the mouth can be heard, evaluated, and corrected. Pro 27:1 (vc=33359, M08-C-VCG-01): "do not boast about tomorrow" — the prohibition addresses the speech-act. The mouth is CHAR-3's functional expression-point.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

No body-part link evidenced. See T2.6.1.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Physical height functions as the expressive and indicative form of CHAR-5's structural-power pride: the physical elevation of the high hill, the fortified nest, and the towering stature are what CHAR-5 looks like at the structural level. Obd 3 (vc=65674, M08-E-VCG-02): "lofty dwelling expresses the outward form of inner pride — living in inaccessible heights reinforces the proud heart's conviction of invulnerability." The physical height is both a chosen position (self-securing strategy) and a visible indicator of CHAR-5's inner posture — the same soul-to-body directionality as CHAR-1's haughty eyes but at the structural/architectural rather than the individual body-part level.

---

##### T2.6.3 — If no body-part link is evidenced, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Body-part links are extensively evidenced across eyes, face, head, neck, hand, gait, and eyelids. Not silent.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Body-part links evidenced: stiff neck (Neh 9:16, vc=34120; Neh 9:29, vc=34126), hand (Exo 21:14, vc=34122), bodily movement (Deu 1:43, vc=34123). Not silent.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Body-part link evidenced through the mouth as CHAR-3's speech-act instrument. Not silent.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

The verse evidence is silent on body-part links for CHAR-4. Confirmed.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Structural/physical height link evidenced (Jer 49:16; Obd 3; Hab 2:9; Eze 19:11). No individual body-part link (eyes, neck, hand) evidenced for CHAR-5 in §3.D. Not fully silent.

---

#### T2.7 — Body — Direction

##### T2.7.1 — Where a body-characteristic link exists, which direction does it run — does the soul express through the body, does the body feed back to the soul, or does it run in both directions?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The direction is consistently soul-to-body: the inner pride of the heart and spirit expresses outward through the bodily register. Pro 30:13 (vc=34249, M08-A2-VCG-01): "inner arrogance manifests in the gaze" — manifestation is from interior to exterior. Isa 2:11 (vc=34089, M08-A2-VCG-01): "the outward gaze reflects an inner disposition of self-elevation" — reflection runs from inner disposition outward to the gaze. Isa 3:16 (vc=34052, M08-A2-VCG-02): "their inner exaltation/pride expresses itself outwardly in ostentatious posture and wanton glances" — the direction is explicit. 1Sa 2:3 (vc=12084, M08-A4-VCG-05): "proud talk is the outward expression of an inner arrogance that flows from the mouth" — from inner to vocal/bodily. No verse in §3 evidences the body generating or feeding back CHAR-1 into the inner person. The body is the display surface, not the source.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

The direction is consistently will-to-body: the inner volitional assertion of CHAR-2 expresses itself outward through the body's actions and posture. Neh 9:16 (vc=34120, M08-B-VCG-01): the people's inner presumption ("acted presumptuously") produces the somatic expression ("stiffened their neck") and the physical action ("did not obey your commandments") — the sequence runs from inner to outer. Deu 1:43 (vc=34123): the inner will's defiance expresses through the bodily act of going up. No verse in §3.A evidences the body generating CHAR-2 in the inner person.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Inner to outer: the inner alazoneia disposition and the soul's desires (Psa 10:3, vc=33354) and the heart's prideful orientation generate the speech-act through the mouth outward into the social field. Jam 4:16 (vc=33866): "arrogance" (inner — alazoneia) → "you boast" (outer — speech-act). 1Jo 2:16 (vc=33865): "the pride of life [alazoneia]" is the inner source that produces visible social display. The direction is consistently interior → verbal/social expression.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

No body-characteristic link evidenced in §3.C. Direction question not applicable.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

The direction is consistently inner-to-outer: the heart's pride (Obd 3 — "the pride of your heart has deceived you") generates the choice to occupy elevated physical positions (living in the clefts of the rock) as a structural expression and security-strategy of the inner pride. Jer 49:16 (vc=34167, M08-E-VCG-02): "the height of your dwelling, who hold the height of the hill" — the physical dwelling-height expresses and reinforces the inner CHAR-5. The structural-physical elevation is the inner pride's external form.

---

##### T2.7.2 — What is the consequence of that directionality for understanding the characteristic?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The soul-to-body directionality has two consequences. First, CHAR-1's origin and constitutional seat are interior — in the heart, spirit, and thought-life — and addressing it requires engaging that interior rather than merely correcting bodily expression. Correcting the haughty eyes (pro 6:17, vc=34247) without addressing the heart's elevation would reach only the symptom. Pro 16:5 (vc=12083, M08-A1-VCG-03) states the diagnostic correctly: "arrogant in heart is an abomination" — the heart is what God assesses. Second, the outward body-expression makes CHAR-1 morally visible and judicially accountable: the haughty eyes become the specific target of divine judgment (Isa 2:11, vc=34089, M08-A2-VCG-01: "the haughty looks of man shall be brought low"; Pro 6:17, vc=34247: first in the list God hates). The body-expression is not incidental — it is how CHAR-1 becomes publicly evidenced and addressable.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

The will-to-body directionality means CHAR-2 originates in the inner volitional faculty and requires address there, not merely at the level of the bodily expression. The stiff neck is the indicator; the inner will is the source. Correcting the posture would not address the will's boiling-over orientation. Additionally, the bodily expression makes CHAR-2 publicly evidenced and judicially assessable — Deu 17:12 (vc=34110, M08-B-VCG-02): the presumptuous man who defies the appointed judge is identified through his acted-out defiance, which is then publicly judged.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

The interior-to-exterior directionality means CHAR-3's source is the inner alazoneia disposition and the heart's prideful orientation — the verbal boasting is the expression, not the origin. Addressing only the speech-act (silencing the mouth) without addressing the inner disposition would reach only the symptom. 2Cor 5:12 (vc=33872, M08-C-VCG-02): Paul's boasting is grounded "in the heart" — the interior is what gives the exterior boast its moral quality.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

Not applicable — no body-characteristic link evidenced. The consequence of the silence is that CHAR-4 operates entirely at the inner cognitive level without a somatic expression register in this corpus.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

The soul-to-structural directionality means CHAR-5 must be addressed at the inner heart-level, not merely at the level of structural position-removal. Lev 26:19 (vc=33982, M08-E-VCG-01): God "breaks the pride of your power" — the breaking is of the inner pride, not merely the removal of the structural power. If the structural power is removed without the inner pride being addressed, CHAR-5 would seek new structural grounds for its arrogance.

---

##### T2.7.3 — If no body-characteristic link is evidenced, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Body-characteristic direction confirmed as soul-to-body. Not silent.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Body-characteristic direction confirmed as will-to-body. Not silent.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Body-characteristic direction confirmed as inner-to-outer (alazoneia/heart → speech-act/mouth). Not silent.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

No body-characteristic link evidenced in §3.C. Confirmed.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Structural/physical height confirmed as CHAR-5's body-analogue, running inner-to-outer. Not silent.

---

#### T2.8 — Body — Deposit

##### T2.8.1 — Does sustained operation of this characteristic leave a constitutional deposit in the body or its design — including DNA or generational consequence?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (S)

The verse evidence does not explicitly evidence a constitutional deposit from CHAR-1 in the body's physical design. The consequences evidenced are consistently inner-constitutional (forgetfulness, wisdom corruption, repentance resistance), relational (contempt, isolation), and external (humiliation, judgment, catastrophic collapse) rather than physical-bodily or biological. No verse in §3 names a physical bodily consequence of sustained CHAR-1 as a structural deposit.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (S)

The verse evidence does not explicitly evidence a constitutional body-deposit from CHAR-2. The consequences evidenced are external (disgrace, strife, destruction) and dispositional (the scoffer's identity), not physical-bodily deposits. The stiff-neck idiom is a somatic expression, not a biological deposit.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (S)

The verse evidence does not explicitly evidence a constitutional body-deposit from CHAR-3. The consequences evidenced (community corruption — 1Cor 5:6; social exposure of emptiness — Pro 25:14; Pro 20:14) are relational and social rather than bodily-constitutional.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

The verse evidence does not evidence a constitutional body-deposit from CHAR-4. All consequences are cognitive (epistemic blindness), relational (disorder), and social (controversy). No physical-bodily deposit evidenced.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (S)

The verse evidence does not explicitly evidence a constitutional body-deposit from CHAR-5. The consequences are structural (desolation of the power-base — Eze 33:28), relational (contempt for the vulnerable — Eze 16:49), and judicial (God's breaking of the proud might — Lev 26:19).

---

##### T2.8.2 — What evidence supports or contradicts this?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (S)

No verse in the 149-verse corpus supports a physical bodily constitutional deposit from CHAR-1. The single occurrence of "physical" in §3's meanings refers to the physical height vocabulary as a metaphor for proud elevation, not to a bodily deposit. The national-pride corpus (M08-A3) evidences CHAR-1 as a communal characteristic across generations, but describes cultural-communal transmission rather than biological deposit — e.g., Isa 16:6 (vc=33989, M08-A3-VCG-01): "we have heard of the pride of Moab — how proud he is" — a reported social identity, not a genetic inheritance.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (S)

No verse in §3.A evidences a physical-biological constitutional deposit from CHAR-2. Not evidenced.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (S)

No verse in §3.B evidences a physical-biological body-deposit from CHAR-3. Not evidenced.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

No verse in §3.C evidences a physical-biological body-deposit. Not evidenced.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (S)

No verse in §3.D evidences a physical-biological body-deposit. Not evidenced.

---

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (S)

The verse evidence is silent on constitutional body-deposit from sustained CHAR-1. No physical-biological deposit evidenced. This feeds T5.7: T5.7 will be closed as the deposit prerequisite is not met.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

Evidence silent on body-deposit from CHAR-4. T5.7 will be closed accordingly.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (S)

Evidence silent on body-deposit from CHAR-5. T5.7 will be closed accordingly.

---

#### T2.9 — Origin and Source

##### T2.9.1 — Where does this characteristic originate constitutionally — is it generated from within the person, received from outside, bestowed by God, or carried generationally?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The verse evidence consistently evidences CHAR-1 as generated from within the person. Mar 7:22 (vc=33928, M08-A4-VCG-01): pride listed among "evils that flow out of a person's heart" — the explicit directional language is outward from within; pride is not received but generated. 2Ti 3:2 (vc=1899, M08-A4-VCG-01): filautos (self-love) "heads the list of end-times vices, establishing the inward orientation toward the self as the root from which pride, boasting, and arrogance all flow" — the root is inside the person, not imposed from outside. The external triggers (prosperity — Deu 8:14, vc=34223; power — 2Ch 26:16, vc=34044; beauty — Eze 28:17, vc=34047) function as conditions that activate CHAR-1 from the interior, not as sources that generate it from outside. God does not bestow CHAR-1 — the evidence is entirely silent on God as its source, and consistently evidences God as its opponent.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

CHAR-2 originates from within the person — specifically from the will's volitional self-assertion against an external constraint. The zid root (boiling presumption) names the internal generative force: Deu 18:20 (vc=34119, M08-B-VCG-01) — "the prophet who presumes to speak" — the will authorising itself. Exo 21:14 (vc=34122, M08-B-VCG-01) — "willful, premeditated" — the inner planning quality confirms internal origin. The heart is named as the dispositional seat (1Sa 17:28, vc=34112; Obd 3, vc=34108) from which the will's specific act emerges. The trigger conditions (contempt for law, absence of God-fear) are internal orientations rather than external causes.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

From within the person — specifically from the inner alazoneia disposition and the heart's prideful orientation. 1Jo 2:16 (vc=33865, M08-C-VCG-01): "the pride of life is not from the Father but is from the world" — worldly inner orientation as the source. Jam 4:16 (vc=33866): arrogance (alazoneia) as the inner substrate from which the boasting act flows. 1Cor 4:7 (vc=33871): the illusion of self-origination as the cognitive origin of the boast's content. CHAR-3 originates in the inner person's orientation, dispositions, and cognitive self-assessment — not received from outside.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

From within the person — specifically in the cognitive/mind faculty's self-assessment process. Col 2:18 (vc=33941, M08-D-VCG-01): "inflated by his sensuous mind" — the mind in its fleshly orientation is the origin. The enabling conditions (knowledge received without love — 1Cor 8:1, vc=33935; partisan attachment — 1Cor 4:6, vc=33937; ungrounded spiritual experience — Col 2:18) are occasions that trigger the mind's self-inflation from within rather than external impositions.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

From within the person/community — specifically in the heart, activated by external structural goods. Eze 28:5 (vc=34046, M08-E-VCG-02): "your heart became proud" — the inner heart-pride is the constitutional origin, though it was triggered by the receipt of external wealth. Isa 47:8 (vc=9563, M08-E-VCG-02): "you who say in your heart" — the origin-point is the heart's inner declaration. The external structural goods (wealth, power, fortification) are enabling occasions that trigger the heart's CHAR-5, not the constitutional origin itself.

---

##### T2.9.2 — What does the evidence reveal about whether the origin is singular or multiple?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The evidence reveals a multiple-but-unified origin. Single generative root: 2Ti 3:2 (vc=1899, M08-A4-VCG-01) — filautos as the dispositional ground from which pride and arrogance flow; Mar 7:22 (vc=33928, M08-A4-VCG-01) — CHAR-1 constitutionally within the fallen inner person. Multiple occasion-triggers that activate from this root: prosperity (Deu 8:14, vc=34223, M08-A1-VCG-01), power (2Ch 26:16, vc=34044, M08-A1-VCG-01), beauty (Eze 28:17, vc=34047, M08-A1-VCG-02), military victory (Dan 11:12, vc=34234, M08-A1-VCG-02), and the general condition of simply being human in a fallen state (Rom 1:30, vc=33932, M08-A4-VCG-01: haughtiness among vices of the morally disordered mind generally). The origin is singular at the root (self-love, the fallen inner person) and multiple in the occasions that release it.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

The origin is multiple in trigger but unified in constitutional source. The unified source is the will's self-authorising impulse (zid root) arising from the heart. Multiple trigger-points: contempt for God's law (Psa 119:21, vc=34098 — wandering from commandments), absence of God-fear (Psa 86:14, vc=34097 — "they do not set God before them"), self-deceptive overconfidence (Obd 3, vc=34108 — "the arrogance of your heart has deceived you"), and distorted claim to privilege (Luk 3:8, vc=55578 — "we have Abraham as our father"). All these trigger the same core: the will asserting beyond its authorised limits.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Multiple but unified: the alazoneia disposition (inner substrate, unified), the soul's desires (Psa 10:3, vc=33354), the heart's prideful orientation (CHAR-1 substrate), and the cognitive self-comparison process (2Cor 10:12 context) all contribute to CHAR-3's generation. The unifying source is the inner self's orientation toward its own elevation (CHAR-1), from which the specific boasting act emerges. The occasion triggers vary: wealth (Psa 49:6, vc=33355), religious identity (Rom 2:17, vc=33882), apostolic credentials (2Cor 11:18), creaturely achievements (Jer 9:23).

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Multiple but unified: various occasions activate the same underlying cognitive self-inflation. The unified source is the mind's fleshly orientation (Col 2:18: "nous tēs sarkos") that generates inflation when stimulated by knowledge, partisan loyalty, or spiritual experience. Multiple trigger-occasions (knowledge, partisan attachment, leadership elevation, spiritual experience) activate the same cognitive-inflation dynamic from within.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Multiple-but-unified: the heart is the single constitutional origin-site; multiple structural goods (military power, wealth, fortification, ease) are the multiple occasion-triggers. Lev 26:19 (vc=33982): power; Eze 28:5 (vc=34046): wealth; Jer 49:16 (vc=34167): fortified height; Eze 16:49 (vc=33979): material ease — all activate the same inner heart-pride from different structural occasions.

---

##### T2.9.3 — Does the origin of this characteristic change across different contexts evidenced in Scripture?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The constitutional origin-site is invariant across contexts: CHAR-1 always originates from within the person's heart (Mar 7:22, vc=33928, M08-A4-VCG-01; Pro 16:5, vc=12083, M08-A1-VCG-03). What varies by context is the occasion-trigger: prosperity in Deu 8:14 (vc=34223) and Hos 13:6 (vc=34232); power and strength in 2Ch 26:16 (vc=34044) and Dan 11:12 (vc=34234); beauty in Eze 28:17 (vc=34047); the collective's shared identity in the national-pride corpus (Isa 16:6, vc=33989, M08-A3-VCG-01; Amo 6:8, vc=34002, M08-A3-VCG-03). Across individual, royal, and national contexts, the origin-point (the fallen inner person's heart and self-love) is consistent; only the activating occasion differs.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

The constitutional origin (will's boiling self-assertion from the heart) is invariant across contexts. What varies is the specific occasion: prophetic contexts (Deu 18:20 — unauthorised speech), legal contexts (Deu 17:12 — defying the judge), military contexts (Deu 1:43 — advancing despite prohibition), NT narrative contexts (Mar 8:32, vc=55607 — Peter rebuking Jesus). The occasion shapes the specific form of transgression; the underlying will-assertion is consistent.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

The constitutional origin (inner alazoneia/heart-orientation) is invariant. What changes across contexts is the object of the boast: wisdom/might/wealth (Jer 9:23, vc=33342), religious law-identity (Rom 2:17/23, vc=33882/33883), apostolic credentials (2Cor 10–12), future plans (Pro 27:1, vc=33359), military achievement (1Ki 20:11, vc=33353). The impulse-to-glory is constant; its social-contextual object varies.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

The constitutional origin (the mind's fleshly self-inflation from within) is invariant. What varies by context is the occasion: intellectual/knowledge contexts (1Cor 8:1, vc=33935), community/partisan contexts (1Cor 4:6, vc=33937), leadership contexts (1Ti 3:6, vc=33924), spiritual-experience contexts (Col 2:18, vc=33941). The cognitive inflation dynamic is consistent; its triggering occasion is context-dependent.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

The constitutional origin (heart-pride) is invariant. What changes is the structural medium: national military power (Eze 30:6), accumulated wealth (Eze 28:5), fortified physical positions (Jer 49:16, Obd 3), material ease (Isa 47:8, Eze 16:49), or authority-position (1Ti 6:17 — wealth). The heart generates CHAR-5 through different structural media in different contexts.

---

#### T2.10 — Constitutional Movement

##### T2.10.1 — Does this characteristic move across constitutional levels — from spirit to soul, from soul to body, or across boundaries in other directions?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes. The evidence evidences movement from the deepest constitutional levels outward. Heart and spirit to visible expression: Psa 101:5 (vc=12085, M08-A1-VCG-03) — "a haughty look and an arrogant heart" — both engaged simultaneously, confirming movement from the heart's inner disposition to the eye's outward expression. Dan 5:20 (vc=34129, M08-A1-VCG-02) — "his heart was lifted up and his spirit was hardened so that he dealt proudly" — the inner constitutional states (heart and spirit) moving outward into behavioural expression. Inner conviction to speech: 1Sa 2:3 (vc=12084, M08-A4-VCG-05) — "proud talk... the outward expression of an inner arrogance that flows from the mouth" — from inner arrogance to verbal expression. Heart to corrupted wisdom: Eze 28:17 (vc=34047, M08-A1-VCG-02) — "your heart was proud... you corrupted your wisdom" — CHAR-1 moving from heart to the cognitive/discernment faculty. The direction is consistently from interior constitutional depth outward toward expression and consequence.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Yes. The evidence shows movement from the inner will/heart outward to speech and physical action. Heart (dispositional seat) → will (activation) → speech (Deu 18:20; Jer 43:2, vc=34105) → physical act (Deu 1:43: going up; Exo 21:14: murder) → social consequence (Psa 119:69/85: lying, pitfall-digging). Neh 9:16 (vc=34120, M08-B-VCG-01): the sequence is "acted presumptuously, stiffened their neck, did not obey your commandments" — inner presumption → somatic stiffening → public disobedience.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Yes. The movement is: alazoneia/heart-orientation (inner constitutional level) → cognitive self-assessment process (mind level) → speech-act (verbal expression) → social display (public reception). Jam 4:16 (vc=33866): alazoneia → boasting. 1Jo 2:16 (vc=33865): inner pride-of-life disposition → worldly display. 2Cor 5:12 (vc=33872): what is in the heart → outward appearance boasting (or, for Paul, heart-grounded boasting). The movement is centrifugal — from inner disposition through cognitive process to verbal expression.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Yes — from inner cognitive inflation outward to relational and social consequences. The movement is: mind/cognitive inflation (fusioō inner state) → verbal expression of inflated self-picture (1Cor 4:18–19, vc=33938/33939: "talk" of the arrogant persons) → relational disorder and controversy (1Ti 6:4, vc=33925: controversy-craving; 2Cor 12:20, vc=33942: fusiōsis among relational sins). The constitutional movement is from the cognitive interior outward to social expression and relational consequence.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Yes. From inner heart-pride → outward structural expression → declared self-sufficiency → relational contempt. Eze 28:5 (vc=34046, M08-E-VCG-02): heart becomes proud → (implied) outer expression of that pride in trade/international posture. Isa 47:8 (vc=9563, M08-E-VCG-02): inner heart → "you say" (speech-declaration) → "I shall not sit as a widow" (relational-consequential claim). Eze 16:49 (vc=33979, M08-E-VCG-01): inner pride → behavioural failure (did not aid the poor and needy).

---

##### T2.10.2 — What does the evidence reveal about the sequence or pattern of that movement?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The sequence is evidenced as: interior constitutional origin (heart/spirit) → cognitive-perceptual consequences (wisdom corruption, perceptual closure to God) → expressive manifestation (haughty eyes, proud speech, outward posture) → behavioural actions (pursuit of the poor, rebellion against authority, unfaithfulness) → external consequences (destruction, humiliation, divine reversal). Deu 8:14 (vc=34223, M08-A1-VCG-01) gives the first segment: prosperity → heart lifted → God forgotten. Eze 28:2–17 (vc=34040, vc=34047, M08-A1-VCG-02) gives the full internal sequence: heart proud → wisdom corrupted → public humiliation as divine judgment. Psa 18:27 (vc=34242, M08-A2-VCG-01) confirms the expressive middle stage: haughty eyes as the visible sign of an inner self-elevation. The pattern is consistently centrifugal — outward from the deepest interior to external collapse.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

The sequence is consistently: inner self-authorising impulse (heart/will) → outward expression through speech or physical action → consequential social and divine relational impact. The movement is centrifugal — from inner source to outer expression. No verse evidences CHAR-2 moving from outer expression back to deepen the inner state (inward), though the Neh 9 historical pattern (repeated presumption) implies that the externally enacted CHAR-2 reinforces the inner disposition over time.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

The sequence: inner orientation (alazoneia, heart) → cognitive content (self-assessment of what to boast about) → verbal expression (kauchaomai speech-act) → social reception/consequence (audience response, community effect). This is more structured than CHAR-2's will-to-act sequence: CHAR-3 includes an intermediate cognitive-assessment stage (the boaster evaluates what they have as worth boasting about) before the speech-act. 1Cor 4:7 (vc=33871): the cognitive attribution stage ("as if you did not receive it") is the specific constitutional level at which the error occurs that generates the CHAR-3 speech-act.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

The sequence is: cognitive self-inflation (inner — fusioō/tufoō) → inflated verbal claims and talk (CHAR-3 overlap, 1Cor 4:19) → relational disruption and controversy (1Ti 6:4; 2Cor 12:20) → epistemic blindness deepening (1Ti 6:4: understanding nothing). The cognitive inflation does not correctively adjust in response to the relational dysfunction it produces — the evidence (1Ti 6:4's sustained controversy-craving) suggests CHAR-4 deepens rather than self-corrects.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

The pattern is: external structural good received → heart-pride activated (inner constitutional level) → outward declaration of self-sufficiency (speech/social level) → relational consequences (contempt, failure to serve others). Eze 28:5 (vc=34046) gives the heart-level; Isa 47:8 (vc=9563) gives the declaration-level; Eze 16:49 (vc=33979) gives the relational-consequence level. The movement is consistently from inner activation (structural good → heart-pride) outward to declaration and relational expression.

---

##### T2.10.3 — If no constitutional movement is evidenced, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Constitutional movement is evidenced from interior (heart/spirit) through cognitive-expressive registers (wisdom, eyes, speech) to behavioural and external consequence. Not silent.

---

Constitutional movement evidenced from will/heart through speech and physical act to social consequence. Not silent.

## T3 — Faculty Engagement (33 prompts)

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Constitutional movement evidenced from external structural goods through heart-pride to declaration and relational consequence. Not silent.

**Batch 4 · Tier T2 PASS — 31/31 prompts, [CHAR-5] markers verified. Proceeding to Tier T3.**

## T3 — Faculty Engagement (33 prompts)

---

### T3

#### T3.1 — Perception

##### T3.1.1 — Does this characteristic engage the perceptive faculty — the inner senses including hearing, sight, taste, touch, smell, and spiritual discernment — and if so, which inner sense and how?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes. CHAR-1 engages the perceptive faculty primarily through the inner sense of spiritual sight — the capacity to perceive God, divine majesty, and divine judgment. Two verses name the perceptive closure directly: Psa 10:4 (vc=34074, M08-A2-VCG-02) — "the wicked does not seek him; all his thoughts are, 'there is no God'" — CHAR-1 closes the perceptive faculty for God so completely that seeking God does not occur and God is declared absent from the inner horizon; Isa 26:10 (vc=34024, M08-A4-VCG-05) — "the wicked person's inner perceptual faculty is closed to the Lord's majesty even in a land of uprightness; their corruption prevents them from seeing the greatness that should prompt reverence." CHAR-1 also closes perception of divine judgment: Psa 10:5 (vc=34166, M08-A4-VCG-03) — "God's judgments are on high — at a height that the arrogant wicked cannot perceive or reach, so his pride blinds him to the divine standard that will ultimately judge him." The perceptive sense engaged is spiritual discernment — sight of God and divine reality — which CHAR-1 impairs.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Yes, by impairing the perceptive faculty for God and divine authority. Psa 86:14 (vc=34097, M08-B-VCG-02): "they do not set God before them" — the presumptuous person removes God from the inner perceptive field; the capacity to perceive divine presence and authority is functionally closed. Psa 119:21 (vc=34098, M08-B-VCG-02): the arrogant "wander from your commandments" — the perceptive faculty for the divine standard has been replaced by an orientation that cannot locate the commandment as the binding reference point.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Yes. CHAR-3's VCG-01 form closes the perceptive faculty for moral self-assessment. Rom 2:17 (vc=33882, M08-C-VCG-01): boasting "in God through the Law" while simultaneously breaking the Law — CHAR-3 closes the perception of one's own inconsistency. Rom 2:23 (vc=33883, M08-C-VCG-01): "you who boast in the law dishonour God by breaking the law" — the boaster cannot perceive the dishonour they are inflicting, because the boast occupies the perceptive field that should register the discrepancy.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Yes, by impairing it. 1Ti 6:4 (vc=33925, M08-D-VCG-02): conceit paired directly with "understanding nothing [mēden epistamenos]" — the inflated self-picture closes the perceptive faculty for truth. 1Ti 3:6 (vc=33924, M08-D-VCG-02): the conceited leader falls into "the condemnation of the devil" — implying that the person cannot perceive their actual vulnerability and trajectory. 1Cor 8:1 (vc=33935, M08-D-VCG-01): "knowledge puffs up" — the receipt of knowledge inflates the self-picture while simultaneously distorting the perception of what that knowledge actually means.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Yes, by impairing it. Obd 3 (vc=65674, M08-E-VCG-02): "the pride of your heart has deceived you" — CHAR-5 closes the perceptive faculty for the person's actual vulnerability, producing a false perception of invulnerability. The structural height that CHAR-5 claims as security actively prevents the perception of one's actual exposure to God's judgment. Jer 49:16 (vc=34167, M08-E-VCG-02): "height of your dwelling... who hold the height of the hill" — the physical height functions as a perceptive barrier, making the nation feel secure from above, while God's judgment can reach any height.

---

##### T3.1.2 — Does this characteristic enable, deepen, bypass, or impair the perceptive faculty in the person?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

CHAR-1 impairs the perceptive faculty selectively and severely. Psa 10:4 (vc=34074, M08-A2-VCG-02): "does not seek him; all his thoughts are, 'there is no God'" — total closure of the inner perceptive field to God; Isa 26:10 (vc=34024, M08-A4-VCG-05): "does not see the majesty of the Lord" — the specific perceptive capacity for divine majesty named as what is closed; Psa 10:5 (vc=34166, M08-A4-VCG-03): divine judgments are "out of his sight" — the proud person cannot perceive the standard by which they will be assessed. The impairment is directional: CHAR-1 does not impair all perception but specifically closes the perception of God, divine majesty, and divine judgment. It may enable a narrow self-centred perception — the proud person perceives themselves and their own achievement clearly — while systematically closing the broader perceptual field that would contextualise the self within God's reality.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

CHAR-2 impairs the perceptive faculty in the direction of divine authority specifically. Psa 86:14 (vc=34097, M08-B-VCG-02): God removed from the inner perceptive horizon. 2Pe 2:10 (vc=42739, M08-B-VCG-03): the self-willed "do not tremble before the glorious ones" — the perceptive faculty for spiritual authority (the capacity to perceive what is worthy of reverence) is closed. The impairment is directional: CHAR-2 closes perception of what should constrain the will, while the will's own purposes remain in clear focus.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

CHAR-3 impairs the perceptive faculty for self-consistent moral assessment. Rom 2:23 (vc=33883, M08-C-VCG-01): the boaster in the law who breaks the law cannot perceive their own law-breaking, because the boast constructs a cognitive picture of the self as law-keeper that overrides the perceptive evidence of law-breaking. 1Ki 20:11 (vc=33353, M08-C-VCG-01): premature boasting impairs the perception of future uncertainty — the boaster "perceives" a victory not yet won.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

CHAR-4 impairs the perceptive faculty comprehensively in the direction of truth-about-self and truth-about-reality. 1Ti 6:4 (vc=33925, M08-D-VCG-02): "understanding nothing" — the most sweeping epistemic failure evidenced in M08. Col 2:18 (vc=33941, M08-D-VCG-01): inflation "without factual basis" — the perception of the self is divorced from actual evidence. CHAR-4 specifically impairs the faculty that would deliver accurate self-knowledge — the very perception that would correct the inflated self-picture is disabled by the inflation.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

CHAR-5 impairs the perceptive faculty for vulnerability and for God's power over structural strength. The ga.on proud-might of Egypt is consistently described as something that "will come down" (Eze 30:6, vc=33996; 30:18, vc=33997; 32:12, vc=33998) — but the nation with proud might does not perceive this coming reversal while it is strong. Lev 26:19 (vc=33982, M08-E-VCG-01): God "will break the pride of your power" — the power-holder does not perceive that their power is breakable until God breaks it. CHAR-5 enables the perception of one's own structural strength while closing the perception of its fragility before God.

---

##### T3.1.3 — What does the pattern of engagement or non-engagement with perception reveal about the nature of this characteristic?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The consistent pattern of perceptive impairment reveals that CHAR-1 is a self-sealing characteristic: it closes off the very perceptual capacities that would detect and correct it. The proud person does not see God's standards (Psa 10:5, vc=34166), does not see divine majesty (Isa 26:10, vc=34024), does not seek God (Psa 10:4, vc=34074), and — as will emerge in T3.3 — does not perceive the redemptive history that would generate gratitude (Deu 8:14, vc=34223; Hos 13:6, vc=34232). The perceptive closure means CHAR-1 removes the inputs through which correction could enter. This is why the wisdom corpus (Pro 16:18, vc=34073, M08-A1-VCG-03: "pride goes before destruction") names external catastrophe rather than internal perception as the corrective mechanism — the perceptive faculty that would otherwise generate self-correction has been closed.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

The pattern reveals that CHAR-2, like CHAR-1, is partially self-sealing: it closes the perceptive faculty for divine authority that would check the will's transgression. Psa 86:14 (vc=34097): "they do not set God before them" — removing the perception of God prevents the inner corrective response that God's perceived authority would generate. However, CHAR-2's perceptive impairment is specifically targeted at authority figures (God, "glorious ones," appointed judges) rather than the broader perceptive closure evidenced in CHAR-1.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

The pattern reveals that CHAR-3 selectively impairs the perceptive faculty in the direction of self-inconsistency: the boaster can perceive their achievement but cannot perceive the gap between their self-presentation and their actual state. This is the perceptive analogue of 1Cor 4:7 (vc=33871)'s cognitive misattribution: the boaster misperceives the origin of their goods AND cannot perceive the discrepancy between the boast and reality.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

The pattern confirms CHAR-4 as self-sealing at the cognitive level: the inflated self-picture closes the perceptive faculty that would correct it. 1Ti 6:4 (vc=33925): the conceited person "understands nothing" — the comprehensive epistemic failure means there is no internal perceptive basis for correction. This is the most extreme form of perceptive self-sealing in M08: where CHAR-1 closes perception of God, CHAR-4 closes perception of reality in general (understanding nothing), making it particularly resistant to evidence-based correction.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

The pattern confirms CHAR-5 as self-sealing at the perceptive level in the structural register: the structural power that generates CHAR-5 simultaneously becomes the perceptive barrier that prevents the person from seeing their actual vulnerability. Obd 3 (vc=65674): "the pride of your heart has deceived you" — the deception is perceptual. This makes CHAR-5's reversal particularly sudden from the human perspective: the proud-might nation cannot see the judgment coming until the structural power that was its perceptive barrier is removed.

---

#### T3.2 — Cognition

##### T3.2.1 — Does this characteristic engage the cognitive faculty — knowing, understanding, discerning — and if so, how?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes. CHAR-1 engages the cognitive faculty primarily through distorting the faculties of understanding, discernment, and self-assessment. Eze 28:17 (vc=34047, M08-A1-VCG-02): "your heart was proud because of your beauty; you corrupted your wisdom for the sake of your splendour" — wisdom (the highest cognitive faculty in the Hebrew tradition) is directly corrupted by CHAR-1. Luk 1:51 (vc=33930, M08-A1-VCG-03): arrogance is located "in the thoughts of their hearts" — the cognitive-mental faculty (dianoiai) named as the seat. 1Sa 16:7 (vc=12091, M08-A1-VCG-03; vc=54394, M08-A4-VCG-05): the human cognitive standard prizes outward height, while God's knowing looks at the heart — CHAR-1 in the cognitive register produces wrong standards of assessment. Rom 12:16 (vc=60877, M08-A4-VCG-01): "never be wise in your own sight" — the cognitive self-assessment is the specific pride-form being addressed here, naming a distorted self-knowing as the danger.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Yes. CHAR-2 engages the cognitive faculty through self-deceptive miscalculation of the self's actual position and vulnerability. Obd 3 (vc=34108, M08-B-VCG-02): "arrogance located in the heart as self-deceptive confidence in physical inaccessibility" — the cognitive assessment is distorted into false security. Jer 49:16 (vc=34115, M08-B-VCG-02): "the arrogance of your heart has deceived you" — CHAR-2 as a cognitive distortion that produces confident miscalculation.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Yes, centrally. 1Cor 4:7 (vc=33871, M08-C-VCG-01): "what do you have that you did not receive? If then you received it, why do you boast as if you did not receive it?" — the cognitive attribution process is the specific locus of CHAR-3's error; the boaster cognitively misattributes received goods as self-generated. 2Cor 10:12 (context of M08-C-VCG-02): "when they measure themselves by one another and compare themselves with one another, they are without understanding" — false self-comparison as a cognitive process named as "without understanding" (asunetos).

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Yes — as its primary faculty. CHAR-4 is constitutively a cognitive phenomenon. Col 2:18 (vc=33941, M08-D-VCG-01): "inflated by his sensuous mind [nous]" — the mind is both the seat and the vehicle of CHAR-4. Rom 12:3 (vc=60866, M08-D-VCG-02): the froneō (thinking/mind-setting) faculty is directly addressed — "do not think [huperfroneō] more highly than you ought." 1Cor 8:1 (vc=33935, M08-D-VCG-01): knowledge (gnōsis — a cognitive content) generates the inflation. CHAR-4 is the cognitive faculty malfunctioning as a self-assessment mechanism.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Yes. Isa 47:8 (vc=9563, M08-E-VCG-02): "you who say in your heart, 'I am, and there is no one besides me; I shall not sit as a widow or know the loss of children'" — the cognitive faculty generates an explicit self-ontological claim: CHAR-5 has produced a cognitive picture of the self as ontologically complete and self-sustaining. Obd 3 (vc=65674, M08-E-VCG-02): "who will bring me down?" — a cognitive assessment of invulnerability. These are cognitive self-assessments of the highest order — not merely social standing but ontological self-completeness.

---

##### T3.2.2 — Does this characteristic enable, deepen, bypass, or impair cognition in the person?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

CHAR-1 impairs cognition in two registers. First, wisdom/discernment: Eze 28:17 (vc=34047, M08-A1-VCG-02) — "you corrupted your wisdom for the sake of your splendour" — CHAR-1 directly corrupts the highest cognitive faculty, so that what the person discerns and understands is distorted by the self's elevation.
