## T5 — Transformational Dynamics (21 prompts)

---

### T5

#### T5.1 — Nature of Transformation

##### T5.1.1 — Does this characteristic produce transformation in the person — and if so, does it change the person's condition, the person's orientation to their condition, or both?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes. CHAR-1 produces transformation in both dimensions. It changes the person's condition: Eze 28:17 (vc=34047, M08-A1-VCG-02) — "your heart was proud... you corrupted your wisdom for the sake of your splendour" — the person's cognitive capacity is structurally altered; Pro 16:18 (vc=34073, M08-A1-VCG-03) — "pride goes before destruction" — the person is moved toward catastrophic external collapse. It changes the person's orientation to their condition: Deu 8:14 (vc=34223, M08-A1-VCG-01) — prosperity received becomes the occasion for pride and forgetfulness rather than gratitude — the person's fundamental orientation to their situation is reordered away from God-directed thankfulness toward self-satisfied self-sufficiency. Dan 5:20 (vc=34129, M08-A1-VCG-02) — "his heart was lifted up and his spirit was hardened so that he dealt proudly" — both condition (spirit hardened) and orientation (dealing proudly) are transformed. The transformation driven by CHAR-1 is progressive and comprehensive, affecting both inner constitution and relational-positional orientation simultaneously.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Yes. CHAR-2 transforms both condition and orientation. Condition: Jer 50:32 (vc=34117, M08-B-VCG-02): "arrogance results in a fall with no one to restore the fallen" — the person's external condition is collapsed and cannot be restored. Eze 7:10 (vc=34118, M08-B-VCG-02): arrogance "has blossomed, pride has budded" — the internal condition deepens organically over time. Orientation: Neh 9:29 (vc=34126, M08-B-VCG-01): "even after warnings, they acted presumptuously again, combining inner arrogance with a stubborn shoulder and deaf ears" — the orientation toward divine authority is progressively hardened, not softened, by repeated acts of CHAR-2. The transformation is primarily downward and deepening.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Yes. VCG-01 produces: (a) community corruption (1Cor 5:6, vc=33903, M08-C-VCG-01: leaven spreading through the lump — condition of the community); (b) social exposure of emptiness (Pro 25:14, vc=33358: clouds and wind without rain — the boaster's social condition exposed as hollow). VCG-02 examined boasting produces: the transformation of the boasting-impulse itself from self-directed to examined-legitimate (2Cor 11:30, vc=33873: boasting in weaknesses — the characteristic's orientation transformed). VCG-03 produces: relational joy and mutual commendation (2Cor 7:4, vc=33917: overflowing joy; 1Th 2:19, vc=33913: community as boast-object before Christ). Transformation is evidenced across all three VCG registers, in three different directions.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Yes. Condition: 1Ti 6:4 (vc=33925, M08-D-VCG-02): "understanding nothing" — the comprehensive epistemic blindness is a changed cognitive condition produced by sustained CHAR-4. 1Ti 3:6 (vc=33924, M08-D-VCG-02): falling into "the condemnation of the devil" — a changed judicial condition. Orientation: 1Ti 6:4: "an unhealthy craving for controversy" — the person's orientation toward knowledge and discourse is transformed from truth-seeking to self-validating controversy. 2Cor 12:20 (vc=33942, M08-D-VCG-02): fusiōsis among relational disorder — the person's relational orientation is transformed toward contention and disorder.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Yes. Condition: Eze 33:28 (vc=33999, M08-E-VCG-01): "the land shall become a desolation and a waste, and the proud might shall come to an end" — the condition is radically transformed when God removes the structural power-base. Eze 28:5 (vc=34046, M08-E-VCG-02): "your heart became proud" — the inner condition of the heart is transformed by received wealth. Orientation: Isa 47:8 (vc=9563, M08-E-VCG-02): the progression from received ease to "you who say in your heart, 'I am, and there is no one besides me'" evidences a transformation of orientation from external good received to inner self-declaration of self-sufficiency.

---

##### T5.1.2 — Is the transformation produced by this characteristic reversible or irreversible in the verse evidence?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Both are evidenced. Reversible: 2Ch 32:26 (vc=34076, M08-A1-VCG-01) — "Hezekiah humbled himself for the pride of his heart, both he and the inhabitants of Jerusalem, so that the wrath of the Lord did not come upon them in the days of Hezekiah" — the transformation is reversed through humbling before catastrophic consequence arrives; Dan 4:37 (vc=34094, M08-A4-VCG-04) — Nebuchadnezzar, after being humbled by God's intervention, "praises and extols and honours the King of heaven" — the transformation through CHAR-1 and its subsequent reversal leads to a reoriented inner posture. Irreversible: Isa 14:11 (vc=33988, M08-A3-VCG-02) — "your pomp is brought down to Sheol, the sound of your harps; maggots are laid as a bed beneath you, and worms are your covers" — the transformation produced by the king of Babylon's pride reaches its terminus in death and total disgrace; Dan 5:20 (vc=34129, M08-A1-VCG-02) — Belshazzar's deposition and loss of glory. The determining factor appears to be whether the person receives divine humbling while reversal is still possible, or whether CHAR-1 is permitted to run to its catastrophic structural end.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

The evidence leans strongly toward irreversibility within §3.A. Jer 50:32 (vc=34117, M08-B-VCG-02): "arrogance results in a fall with no one to restore the fallen" — no restoration evidenced. Mal 4:1 (vc=34107, M08-B-VCG-02): "the day that is coming shall set them ablaze... it will leave them neither root nor branch" — total eschatological destruction with no remnant. Neh 9:16/29: the pattern of repeated warnings followed by repeated presumption suggests the transformation CHAR-2 produces is not easily reversed — the Neh 9 historical narrative evidences no sustained reversal within the pattern of presumption. The contrast with CHAR-1's Nebuchadnezzar and Hezekiah reversals is notable: §3.A does not evidence a comparable restoration after CHAR-2. The irreversible end is most prominent.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Both are evidenced, and uniquely to CHAR-3, the transformation can be positive and deliberate. For VCG-01 → VCG-02 transformation: the examination and redirection of the boasting-impulse (Gal 6:14, vc=33869; 2Cor 10:13, vc=33888) is an explicit, sustained transformation that is reversible in principle (the person could revert to VCG-01) but is evidenced as a settled apostolic posture in Paul. For the Pauline examined → God-directed transformation: 1Cor 1:31 (vc=33878, M08-C-VCG-03): "let the one who boasts, boast in the Lord" — commanded as a settled orientation. Unlike CHAR-1 and CHAR-2, CHAR-3 has evidenced positive transformational pathways (VCG-01 → VCG-02 → VCG-03) within the same characteristic.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

The evidence leans toward deepening and difficult reversibility. 1Ti 6:4 (vc=33925, M08-D-VCG-02): "understanding nothing" — comprehensive epistemic blindness is a deeply entrenched state; a person who understands nothing cannot easily self-correct since the cognitive faculty that would generate self-correction is the faculty that is impaired. 1Ti 3:6 (vc=33924, M08-D-VCG-02): the condemnation of the devil as the trajectory — judicial finality. No verse in §3.C evidences a restoration or reversal after CHAR-4 has produced its consequences. The counter-mechanisms (love — 1Cor 8:1; sober judgment — Rom 12:3) are preventive rather than curative in the evidence.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Both are evidenced. Irreversible instances: Jer 51:53 (vc=65670, M08-E-VCG-02): even if Babylon fortifies to heaven, "destroyers would come from me against her" — no structural height can prevent God's judgment; Eze 32:12 (vc=33998, M08-E-VCG-01): Egypt's proud might "shall be destroyed" without mention of restoration. Reversible implication: Lev 26:19 (vc=33982, M08-E-VCG-01) is part of the covenant stipulations that include restoration conditions (Lev 26:40–45 — broader covenant context implies restoration is possible after repentance). The evidence leans toward irreversibility in the prophetic-judgment corpus but implies reversibility in the covenantal context.

---

##### T5.1.3 — If the evidence is silent on transformation, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Transformation is extensively evidenced as both reversible (2Ch 32:26, vc=34076; Dan 4:37, vc=34094) and irreversible (Isa 14:11, vc=33988; Dan 5:20, vc=34129). Not silent.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Transformation evidenced as deepening and primarily irreversible. Not silent.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Transformation extensively evidenced across all three VCG registers with both negative (VCG-01 corruption) and positive (VCG-02/03 redirection) pathways. Not silent.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Transformation evidenced as deepening toward epistemic blindness (1Ti 6:4) and judicial condemnation (1Ti 3:6). Not silent.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Transformation evidenced as irreversible in prophetic-judgment contexts (Jer 51:53; Eze 32:12; 33:28) with covenantal-implied reversibility (Lev 26:19). Not silent.

---

#### T5.2 — Sequence of Inner States

##### T5.2.1 — Does the verse evidence describe a sequence of inner states through which this characteristic moves the person — a before, during, and after?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes. The evidence evidences two distinct sequential patterns. First, the prosperity-sequence: before — fullness/satisfaction received (Hos 13:6, vc=34232, M08-A1-VCG-01: "when they had grazed, they became full, they were filled"); during — heart lifted in response (Hos 13:6: "their heart was lifted up"; Deu 8:14, vc=34223, M08-A1-VCG-01: "then your heart will be lifted up"); after — God forgotten (Hos 13:6: "therefore they forgot me"; Deu 8:14: "and you forget the Lord your God"). Second, the strength/achievement-sequence: before — growing strong or accomplished (2Ch 26:16, vc=34044, M08-A1-VCG-01: "when he was strong"; Eze 28:17, vc=34047, M08-A1-VCG-02: beauty as the trigger); during — heart growing proud, wisdom corrupting (2Ch 26:16: "he grew proud, to his destruction; for he was unfaithful"; Eze 28:17: "you corrupted your wisdom for the sake of your splendour"); after — catastrophic reversal (2Ch 26:16: unfaithfulness leads to judgment; Eze 28:17: "I cast you to the ground").

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Yes. The Neh 9 corpus provides the clearest sequential evidence: before-state — covenant blessing received, God's law given; during-state — presumptuous acting, stiff neck, deaf ears (Neh 9:16, vc=34120; Neh 9:29, vc=34126); warning-state — corrective intervention from God; after-state — further presumption despite warnings. A second sequence is the growth-organic pattern: Eze 7:10 (vc=34118, M08-B-VCG-02) — arrogance "has blossomed, pride has budded" — implying a seed-stage, growth-stage, and full-bloom stage. And the wisdom-consequence sequence: Pro 11:2 (vc=34109, M08-B-VCG-02) — CHAR-2 → disgrace; Pro 13:10 (vc=34113) — CHAR-2 → strife.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Yes. Jam 4:13–16 (context of vc=33886, M08-C-VCG-01) provides the clearest negative sequence: before — "today or tomorrow we will go into such and such a town" (planned future); during — "you boast in your arrogance" (CHAR-3 active); after — "all such boasting is evil" (divine evaluation). A positive sequence: 1Cor 1:26–31 (context of vc=33877/33878): before — human wisdom, might, and nobility as boasting-grounds; during — God's election evacuating those grounds; after — boasting in the Lord as the only legitimate orientation. The Pauline examined discourse (2Cor 10–12) narrates a sustained sequence from VCG-01 rivals' boasting → Paul's examined VCG-02 boasting → VCG-03 boasting in weakness.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Yes. 1Cor 8:1 (vc=33935, M08-D-VCG-01) gives the initiation: knowledge received → cognitive self-inflation (fusioō) — the receipt of knowledge is the before-state; the inflation is the during-state. 1Ti 6:4 (vc=33925, M08-D-VCG-02) gives the sustained state and consequence: conceit (during) → understanding nothing + controversy-craving (after). 1Ti 3:6 (vc=33924, M08-D-VCG-02): rapid leadership elevation → CHAR-4 activation (puffed up with conceit) → condemnation.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Yes. Eze 28:5 (vc=34046, M08-E-VCG-02) gives the clearest individual sequence: wealth gained → heart became proud. Isa 47:8 (vc=9563, M08-E-VCG-02) gives the full sequence for Babylon: before — voluptuous ease and pleasures (a.din); during — "you who say in your heart, 'I am, and there is no one besides me'" (CHAR-5 active as self-declaration); after — God's judgment bringing loss of children and widowhood (the very relational losses CHAR-5 had denied as possibilities). Eze 16:49 (vc=33979, M08-E-VCG-01): before — excess of food and prosperous ease; during — pride (CHAR-5 active); after — failure to aid the poor and needy (relational consequence).

---

##### T5.2.2 — What are those states, and what does the sequence reveal about how this characteristic works?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The states across both sequences: before-state = material or experiential fullness (prosperity, military success, beauty, strength); during-state = heart lifted, spirit hardened, wisdom corrupting — CHAR-1 active and deepening but internally invisible; after-state = catastrophic external collapse (destruction — Pro 16:18, vc=34073, M08-A1-VCG-03; humiliation — Pro 29:23, vc=33960, M08-A4-VCG-04; descent to Sheol — Isa 14:11, vc=33988, M08-A3-VCG-02). The sequence reveals two analytically significant features. First, CHAR-1 is triggered by blessing rather than by adversity — what activates it is the receipt of good things (prosperity, success, beauty) which are then misattributed as self-generated. Second, the during-state is phenomenologically invisible to the possessor (T1.5.3): the person in the middle of the sequence feels elevated and successful, not in danger. This is what makes the sequence so catastrophic — the gap between the person's self-perception (successful, elevated, wisdom-capable) and the actual trajectory (moving toward collapse) is maximal during the dangerous middle period.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Before: divine command/authority is present and known; during: the will's self-authorising boil-over against the known limit; after: external consequence (disgrace, strife, fall, death, eschatological destruction) and dispositional deepening (the scoffer's settled identity). The sequence reveals that CHAR-2 is not a one-time event but an escalating pattern: Neh 9:16/29 evidences multi-generational escalation, while Eze 7:10's organic growth imagery and Pro 21:24's scoffer identity confirm that repeated acts of CHAR-2 produce a stable dispositional identity that generates further acts.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Negative sequence (VCG-01): before — creaturely assets/achievements treated as boasting-grounds (Psa 49:6, vc=33355: wealth; Jer 9:23: wisdom/might/wealth); during — self-directed boasting act; after — exposure of emptiness or community corruption. Positive sequence (VCG-02→VCG-03): before — the boasting-impulse present and unexamined; during — cross-formation evacuating worldly grounds (Gal 6:14); after — the impulse redirected toward God, community, and legitimate self-commendation (VCG-03 joy; VCG-02 conscience-testimony). The sequence reveals that CHAR-3, uniquely among M08 characteristics, has an evidenced positive transformational trajectory within the same characteristic.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Before: receipt of a cognitive good (knowledge, spiritual experience, leadership responsibility). During: cognitive self-inflation without the anchoring of love or sober judgment. After: comprehensive epistemic blindness (understanding nothing), controversy-craving, relational disorder, judicial condemnation. The sequence reveals that CHAR-4 is triggered by received goods — like CHAR-1 (triggered by prosperity/power/beauty), CHAR-4 is generated when cognitive goods (knowledge, spiritual experience) are received without the proper anchoring (love, sober judgment) that would prevent inflation. The characteristic corrupts the receipt of cognitive goods.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Before: receipt of genuine structural goods (military power, wealth, ease, fortified position). During: the heart's CHAR-5 activation — "your heart became proud" (Eze 28:5); the self-sufficient declaration (Isa 47:8). After: relational contempt (Eze 16:49 — not aiding the poor); divine reversal (Eze 30:6 — Egypt's proud might comes down); desolation (Eze 33:28). The sequence reveals that CHAR-5's inner dynamic is triggered by actual structural goods — the before-state is genuine prosperity, not delusion. The characteristic is the misuse of real goods, which makes its reversal particularly dramatic: the structural goods that generated the CHAR-5 are removed, and the inner self-sufficient posture collapses with them.

---

##### T5.2.3 — If the evidence is silent on sequence, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Sequence of inner states evidenced in two distinct patterns (prosperity-sequence and strength-sequence). Not silent.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Sequence evidenced in Neh 9 (historical pattern), Eze 7:10 (organic growth), and wisdom-consequences. Not silent.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Sequence evidenced in both negative (VCG-01 corruption) and positive (VCG-02/03 transformation) directions. Not silent.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Sequence evidenced from received knowledge → inflation → epistemic blindness/condemnation. Not silent.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Sequence evidenced from structural goods received through heart-pride to divine reversal and desolation. Not silent.

---

#### T5.3 — Mechanism of Change

##### T5.3.1 — What mechanism does this characteristic use to produce change in the person — discipline, encounter, gradual formation, sudden transformation, or something else?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The primary mechanism by which CHAR-1 itself produces change is gradual dispositional deepening. 2Ch 26:16 (vc=34044, M08-A1-VCG-01): Uzziah's pride "grew" as he became strong — the progression is incremental, not sudden. Dan 4:37 (vc=34094, M08-A4-VCG-04): pride described as something one "walks in" — a habitual gait that develops over time as the inner posture is repeatedly enacted. The counter-mechanism — through which CHAR-1 is reversed — is externally-imposed divine humbling: Luk 1:51 (vc=33930, M08-A1-VCG-03) — God "scattered the proud in the thoughts of their hearts"; 2Sa 22:28 (vc=34236, M08-A4-VCG-02) — "your eyes are on the haughty to bring them down"; Job 40:11–12 (vc=33949, vc=33951, M08-A4-VCG-02) — God's challenge to "look on everyone who is proud and abase him... look on everyone who is proud and bring him low." The counter-mechanism is direct divine action (encounter/reversal) rather than gradual formation — CHAR-1's self-sealing quality (T3.1.3) makes gradual internal formation insufficient as a counter-mechanism.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

The primary mechanism of CHAR-2 itself is dispositional escalation: repeated acts of presumptuous defiance deepen the inner posture. The counter-mechanism (correcting CHAR-2) is external divine-judicial action: Deu 17:12 (vc=34110, M08-B-VCG-02): public death of the presumptuous person; Deu 17:13 (vc=34124): the people hearing and fearing as a consequence; Neh 9:10 (vc=34125): God's "signs and wonders" against Egypt's CHAR-2. The mechanism of correction is not gradual internal formation but sudden, public, corrective judgment designed to generate fear (Deu 17:13: "all the people shall hear and fear").

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

For VCG-01 → corruption: the mechanism is social spreading — 1Cor 5:6 (vc=33903): "a little leaven leavens the whole lump" — CHAR-3 in community produces exponential moral decay through social contagion. For VCG-01 → VCG-02/03 transformation: the mechanism is cross-formation — Gal 6:14 (vc=33869): the cross evacuating all worldly boasting-grounds is the transformative mechanism; 1Cor 1:29 (vc=33877): God's sovereign election removes the basis for human boasting. The counter-mechanism is specifically theological: the cross's evacuation of credential-ground and the commanded redirection to God as the only legitimate object of glorying.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Gradual cognitive inflation deepening without self-correction: the inflated self-picture progressively obscures the cognitive faculty's truth-access, leading to the terminal state of "understanding nothing" (1Ti 6:4, vc=33925, M08-D-VCG-02). The counter-mechanism evidenced is love as an anchor for knowledge (1Cor 8:1, vc=33935: "love builds up" rather than inflates) and God-referenced sober judgment (Rom 12:3, vc=60866: thinking within God-assigned measure). Both counter-mechanisms are preventive — they anchor the cognitive faculty before inflation occurs rather than correcting it after.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

The primary mechanism is the structural-goods-to-heart-pride sequence: actual power/wealth/position received → heart elevated → self-sufficiency claim entrenched. The counter-mechanism (correcting CHAR-5) is structural removal: Lev 26:19 (vc=33982, M08-E-VCG-01) — God "will break the pride of your power" — breaking the structural foundation causes the inner pride to collapse. Eze 33:28 (vc=33999, M08-E-VCG-01): "proud might shall come to an end" paired with total desolation. The mechanism of correction is not internal formation (CHAR-5 provides no internal corrective mechanism) but external structural removal.

---

##### T5.3.2 — Does the evidence distinguish between mechanisms in different contexts?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes. For individuals in covenant relationship, the evidence shows two different outcomes: (a) humbling received before catastrophic collapse — Hezekiah (2Ch 32:26, vc=34076, M08-A1-VCG-01): warns himself, wrath averted; Nebuchadnezzar (Dan 4:37, vc=34094): humbled by God's intervention, then restored and God-directed. (b) CHAR-1 permitted to reach its terminus — Uzziah (2Ch 26:16, vc=34044): pride → unfaithfulness → struck with leprosy (narrative context); Belshazzar (Dan 5:20, vc=34129): deposed and glory taken in the same narrative. For collective/national subjects (M08-A3), the mechanism is consistently imperial collapse as divine judgment — Babylon's fall (Isa 13:19, vc=33987), Moab's dispossession (Zep 2:10, vc=34004), Assyria's humbling (Zec 10:11, vc=34006) — where the external military defeat is the instrument of divine reversal at the national scale.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Yes. For the individual presumptuous person (Deu 17:12, vc=34110): death as the corrective mechanism, designed to purge the evil and generate community-wide fear. For the presumptuous nation (Jer 50:31–32, vc=34116/34117): "the proud one stumbles and falls" — national collapse as the corrective. For the eschatological register (Mal 4:1, vc=34107): total fiery destruction as the final corrective. The mechanism scales with the scope of the CHAR-2: individual → legal-judicial death; national → imperial collapse; eschatological → total destruction.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Yes. For the faith community: the cross as the transformative mechanism (Gal 6:14; 1Cor 1:29). For the apostolic context: examined self-discipline within God-assigned spheres (2Cor 10:13, vc=33888 — Paul's volitional constraint). For the wisdom context: the proverb's corrective observation (1Ki 20:11, vc=33353: the fool who boasts before taking off the armour — wisdom literature's correction through memorable observation). The mechanism differs by context: theological (cross), volitional (discipline), and wisdom (observation).

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Yes. In community contexts: partisan inflation (1Cor 4:6, vc=33937) corrected by Paul's apostolic authority (1Cor 4:19, vc=33939: Paul will come and expose the power-gap). In leadership contexts: formation (avoiding new-convert leadership — 1Ti 3:6, vc=33924) is the preventive mechanism. In knowledge contexts: love as the anchor (1Cor 8:1, vc=33935) prevents knowledge-conceit. In general: God-assigned measure of faith (Rom 12:3, vc=60866) as the cognitive corrective standard.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Yes. For national collective CHAR-5: military defeat by God-directed enemies (Eze 30:12 — "I will bring strangers against her"; Eze 32:12 — "the ruthless of nations"). For individual wealth-CHAR-5: the uncertain nature of riches as the corrective mechanism (1Ti 6:17, vc=60878: "the uncertainty of riches" — wealth's inherent instability as the natural counter to hupsēlofroneō). For fortification-CHAR-5: divine judgment overcoming the fortified position (Jer 51:53: "destroyers would come from me against her"). The mechanism differs by structural medium: military defeat for national might; wealth's uncertainty for individual wealth-pride; divine penetration for fortification-pride.

---

##### T5.3.3 — If the evidence is silent on mechanism, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Mechanism evidenced as gradual internal deepening (for CHAR-1's operation) and externally-imposed divine reversal (for CHAR-1's counter). Not silent.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Mechanism evidenced as escalating CHAR-2 internally and external divine judgment as correction. Not silent.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Mechanism evidenced as social contagion (VCG-01) and cross-formation/volitional discipline (VCG-02/03 transformation). Not silent.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Mechanism evidenced as gradual cognitive inflation + love/sober-judgment as preventive counter-mechanisms. Not silent.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Mechanism evidenced as structural-goods-removal (military defeat, wealth's uncertainty, divine judgment). Not silent.

---

#### T5.4 — Suffering and Affliction

##### T5.4.1 — Does the verse evidence show this characteristic operating in relation to suffering or affliction — as a response to it, a product of it, or a context for it?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The evidence consistently shows CHAR-1 as affliction's antithesis rather than its product or response. CHAR-1 operates characteristically in conditions of ease, fullness, and prosperity — not in suffering. Psa 123:4 (vc=33953, M08-A4-VCG-03): the proud are "those who are at ease" whose contempt crushes the psalmist — ease is the context of their CHAR-1, suffering is what they inflict on others. Deu 8:14 (vc=34223, M08-A1-VCG-01): prosperity and fullness trigger the heart's lifting — the pre-condition is blessing received, not adversity. Dan 11:12 (vc=34234, M08-A1-VCG-02): military victory (success, not suffering) lifts the heart. The evidence for suffering in relation to CHAR-1 runs in the opposite direction: suffering and external humbling are God's instruments for correcting CHAR-1 (Dan 4:37, vc=34094: Nebuchadnezzar's humbling through affliction restores his God-directed posture), not for generating it.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

CHAR-2 characteristically operates from a position of felt power and security rather than from suffering. Obd 3 (vc=34108, M08-B-VCG-02): the arrogant's "inner conviction of invulnerability" — power is the enabling condition. Mar 10:42 (vc=55588, M08-B-VCG-03): "rulers who lord it over others" — structural power. Mat 24:49 (vc=55613, M08-B-VCG-03): the servant acts presumptuously when assuming the master is absent (perceived absence of accountability). CHAR-2 produces suffering in others (Psa 119:85: pitfalls for the godly) but does not arise from suffering in the one exercising it.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Yes — uniquely among M08 characteristics, CHAR-3 has a direct positive relationship to suffering. 2Cor 12:9 (vc=33870, M08-C-VCG-02): Paul "gladly boasts of weaknesses so that the power of Christ may rest upon" him. 2Cor 11:30 (vc=33873, M08-C-VCG-02): "if I must boast, I will boast of the things that show my weakness." Rom 5:3 (vc=33875, M08-C-VCG-03): "we rejoice in our sufferings, knowing that suffering produces endurance" — suffering is explicitly the ground of the examined boasting. CHAR-3's VCG-02 form is directly generated by suffering rather than ease.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Partially. Col 2:18 (vc=33941, M08-D-VCG-01): inflation "by his sensuous mind" in the context of claimed angel-worship and ascetic practices — the ascetic/suffering context is the occasion for the ungrounded spiritual-experience inflation. The person claiming superior spiritual experience through ascetic discipline (self-denial as suffering) is generating CHAR-4 from that experience. CHAR-4 in this context arises from claimed suffering-experience rather than from ease.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

CHAR-5 characteristically operates from conditions of ease and abundance, not from suffering. Eze 16:49 (vc=33979, M08-E-VCG-01): "prosperous ease" as CHAR-5's generative condition. Isa 47:8 (vc=9563, M08-E-VCG-02): a.din (voluptuous ease, love of pleasures) as the affective ground. CHAR-5 produces suffering for others (exploitation — Hab 2:9; neglect — Eze 16:49) and receives suffering as its consequence (desolation — Eze 33:28; widowhood — Isa 47:9 context). CHAR-5 is consistently generated by ease and ends in suffering, not generated by suffering.

---

##### T5.4.2 — Does suffering deepen, test, reveal, or produce this characteristic in the person?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The evidence consistently shows suffering and affliction as the mechanism that corrects CHAR-1 rather than deepening or producing it. Dan 4:37 (vc=34094, M08-A4-VCG-04): the broader narrative context evidences Nebuchadnezzar's affliction (being driven from his kingdom to eat grass as an animal) as the mechanism through which his pride was broken and his God-directed recognition restored — suffering corrects CHAR-1. 2Ch 32:26 (vc=34076, M08-A1-VCG-01): Hezekiah's humbling (recognising his own pride) averts the suffering that would otherwise come — self-humbling forestalls affliction as divine correction. Pro 16:18 (vc=34073, M08-A1-VCG-03): "pride goes before destruction" — CHAR-1 produces the conditions that generate suffering (destruction, fall), rather than suffering producing CHAR-1. The causal arrow runs from CHAR-1 to suffering (as consequence), not from suffering to CHAR-1 (as product).

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

The evidence suggests that anticipated suffering as consequence corrects CHAR-2 (Deu 17:13: fear from hearing of punishment) rather than suffering producing it. The Neh 9 pattern (repeated presumption despite warnings and consequences) suggests that experienced suffering does not reliably correct CHAR-2 in a hardened person — "even after warnings, they acted presumptuously again" (Neh 9:29, vc=34126). Suffering's relationship to CHAR-2 is primarily corrective-potential rather than generative.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Suffering produces VCG-02 and VCG-03 boasting: 2Cor 12:9 (vc=33870): weakness (the result of suffering/thorn) produces the ground for boasting in God's power; Rom 5:3 (vc=33875): sufferings produce endurance which produces character, which the believer then rejoices in. 2Cor 7:4 (vc=33917): overflowing joy "in all our affliction" — affliction is the context of the God-directed boasting. This is directly contrary to VCG-01's dynamic (which arises from ease and creaturely assets): VCG-02/03 boasting arises from suffering and weakness.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Col 2:18 (vc=33941, M08-D-VCG-01) evidences that claimed ascetic experience (a form of self-imposed suffering) can generate CHAR-4 when the person interprets that experience as a ground for cognitive superiority ("inflated by his sensuous mind... without factual basis"). Suffering in this context does not correct CHAR-4 but generates it when misinterpreted. This distinguishes CHAR-4's relationship to suffering from CHAR-1's (where suffering corrects) and from CHAR-3 VCG-02's (where suffering is the positive ground for God-directed boasting): for CHAR-4, claimed suffering-experience can be a trigger for cognitive inflation.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Suffering functions as the consequence of CHAR-5 rather than its producer. Eze 33:28 (vc=33999, M08-E-VCG-01): desolation as the consequence; Isa 47:9 (context of vc=9563): "these two things shall come to you in a moment, in one day; the loss of children and widowhood" — the relational suffering that CHAR-5's self-declaration denied as possibility arrives suddenly as consequence. Suffering does not generate CHAR-5 in §3.D — it reverses it or arrives as its judgment.

---

##### T5.4.3 — If the evidence is silent on the relationship to suffering, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The relationship to suffering is evidenced as inverse: ease and blessing generate CHAR-1; affliction and humbling correct it. Not silent.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

CHAR-2's relationship to suffering: arises from felt power, produces suffering in others, is potentially corrected by consequential suffering; not generated by suffering. Not silent.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

CHAR-3's relationship to suffering is distinctive: VCG-01 arises from ease; VCG-02/03 arises from suffering and weakness. Not silent.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

CHAR-4's relationship to suffering is partially evidenced via Col 2:18 (ascetic experience generating CHAR-4) — distinct from other M08 characteristics' relationships to suffering. Not fully silent.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

CHAR-5's relationship to suffering evidenced as inverse: ease generates CHAR-5; suffering arrives as its consequence. Not silent.

---

#### T5.5 — Formation and Sanctification

##### T5.5.1 — Does the verse evidence show this characteristic participating in the longer arc of character formation and sanctification — shaping the person over time toward greater likeness?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes — as the characteristic that opposes and obstructs the formation arc rather than advancing it. CHAR-1 is the primary barrier to sanctification in the evidence: it blocks hearing God's word (Jer 13:15, vc=34053, M08-A4-VCG-04: "be not proud, for the Lord has spoken" — the warning implies that CHAR-1 prevents reception of what God says); it blocks repentance and return (Hos 7:10, vc=34001, M08-A3-VCG-03: "yet they do not return to the Lord their God" — CHAR-1 as the active barrier); it corrupts wisdom (Eze 28:17, vc=34047, M08-A1-VCG-02 — the faculty through which formation occurs is damaged). The formation arc cannot proceed through the person's interior while CHAR-1 holds these faculties closed. What the evidence does show is the positive formation arc becoming possible after CHAR-1 is reversed: Dan 4:37 (vc=34094, M08-A4-VCG-04) — after Nebuchadnezzar's pride is humbled, he praises "the King of heaven" and testifies to divine justice — a genuine transformation of inner orientation.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Yes — as the characteristic that breaks the formation arc. CHAR-2's repeated pattern in Neh 9 shows the barrier it presents to formation: despite "warnings" (corrective divine action) the ancestors "acted presumptuously again" (Neh 9:29, vc=34126) — the formation arc is interrupted at the point where submitted response to correction should occur. Deu 18:20 (vc=34119, M08-B-VCG-01): the false prophet speaks "presumptuously" — speaking beyond God's word is the formation arc's inverse; formation is being shaped by God's word, while CHAR-2 is claiming authority over it.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Yes — CHAR-3 is uniquely the characteristic most directly evidenced as a site of formation within M08. The VCG-02 examined boasting discourse (2Cor 10–12) is essentially the formative discipline of the boasting-impulse: the impulse is not suppressed but examined, bounded, and redirected. Gal 6:4 (vc=33908, M08-C-VCG-02): "let each one test his own work" — self-examination before boasting as a formative discipline. Gal 6:14 (vc=33869): the cross as the formative event that evacuates self-boasting grounds. The formation arc is from VCG-01 (unexamined, self-directed) through VCG-02 (examined, bounded) to VCG-03 (God-directed, grace-grounded).

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Yes — as the characteristic that short-circuits formation by substituting inflated cognitive self-assessment for the gradual accurate self-knowledge that genuine formation requires. 1Ti 3:6 (vc=33924, M08-D-VCG-02): the new convert given leadership too quickly — formation (time, experience, testing) is the proper developmental arc that CHAR-4 prevents by enabling premature cognitive inflation. 1Cor 8:1 (vc=33935, M08-D-VCG-01): "knowledge puffs up, but love builds up" — genuine formation is the "building up" of love; CHAR-4 substitutes the inflation of knowledge for the patient construction of love-shaped character.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Yes — as a formation-barrier through the structural-power medium. 1Ti 6:17 (vc=60878, M08-E-VCG-02) provides the most direct formation evidence: "as for the rich in this present age, charge them not to be haughty [hupsēlofroneō], nor to set their hopes on the uncertainty of riches, but on God" — the formation arc requires reorienting hope from structural goods to God as their source. This is the positive formation instruction that CHAR-5 resists. Eze 16:49 (vc=33979): the formation failure of Sodom evidences CHAR-5 as the root sin that prevented the formation of neighbour-service.

---

##### T5.5.2 — What does the evidence reveal about the role of this characteristic in that longer arc?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

CHAR-1 functions as the primary obstacle in the formation arc — the inner characteristic that must be addressed (humbled, reversed) before God-directed formation can proceed. Three specific obstructions are evidenced: forgetfulness displacing the memory of God's provision (Deu 8:14, vc=34223; Hos 13:6, vc=34232) — without which gratitude and responsiveness cannot form; perceptive closure to God (Psa 10:4, vc=34074; Isa 26:10, vc=34024) — without which encounter with God cannot occur; wisdom corruption (Eze 28:17, vc=34047) — without which discernment-based growth cannot proceed. The positive formation pattern emerges from the negative: Dan 4:37 (vc=34094) demonstrates that the post-CHAR-1 posture (after divine humbling) is precisely what formation is moving toward — God-directed acknowledgment, rightful creature-Creator orientation, praise of the King of heaven. CHAR-1 is the anti-formational core that must be dissolved before the formation arc can be traversed.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

CHAR-2 is the barrier in the formation arc at the specific point of submission to divine correction. Formation requires receiving God's corrective word and bowing to divine authority — precisely what CHAR-2 refuses. Neh 9:29 (vc=34126, M08-B-VCG-01): "they acted presumptuously again, combining inner arrogance with a stubborn shoulder and deaf ears" — the deaf ears and stubborn shoulder are the formation-failure indicators: they refuse to hear (the formative word) and bear the yoke (the formative discipline). CHAR-2 is the anti-formational characteristic at the obedience-to-authority node.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Unlike CHAR-1 and CHAR-2 (which are primarily formation-barriers), CHAR-3 is both a formation-barrier (VCG-01) and a formation-site (VCG-02) and a formation-goal (VCG-03). The VCG-02 examined discourse shows that the boasting-impulse itself is the raw material of formation — it does not merely need to be suppressed but redirected and disciplined. The formation goal (VCG-03) is the glorying-impulse fully oriented toward God and his grace.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

CHAR-4 is the formation-arc's short-circuit at the cognitive level: it substitutes a premature inflated self-assessment for the patient development of accurate self-knowledge. 1Ti 3:6 (vc=33924): the formation that would have prevented the new convert's CHAR-4 is the gradual development that provides accurate cognitive grounding in one's actual spiritual standing. CHAR-4 bypasses this gradual development, generating a false picture of spiritual maturity that the formation arc is designed to produce genuinely.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

CHAR-5 is the formation-barrier specifically at the stewardship-of-structural-goods node: the person who receives power, wealth, or position must develop the formation posture of stewardship (1Ti 6:18: "ready to share") rather than CHAR-5's posture of self-sufficient elevation. The formation arc moves through received structural goods toward God-directed stewardship; CHAR-5 short-circuits this by generating self-sufficient heart-pride from the received goods instead.

---

##### T5.5.3 — If the evidence is silent on formation and sanctification, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

CHAR-1's role in the formation arc is evidenced as obstruction and barrier. The post-reversal formation posture (Dan 4:37, vc=34094) provides the positive contrast. Not silent.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

CHAR-2's formation-blocking role evidenced in Neh 9:16/29 pattern and Deu 18:20. Not silent.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

CHAR-3's formation role is extensively evidenced as both barrier (VCG-01) and site/goal (VCG-02/03). Not silent.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

CHAR-4's formation-arc role evidenced as formation-short-circuit (1Ti 3:6) and love-building-up as the proper formative alternative (1Cor 8:1). Not silent.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

CHAR-5's formation role evidenced as barrier at stewardship node (1Ti 6:17; Eze 16:49). Not silent.

---

#### T5.6 — Eschatological Trajectory

##### T5.6.1 — Does the verse evidence point this characteristic toward an eschatological fullness — a future state toward which its present operation is oriented?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes — but toward eschatological reversal, not fullness. The day-of-the-Lord material in M08-A3-VCG-04 constitutes the primary eschatological evidence: Isa 2:12 (vc=33957, vc=65778, M08-A3-VCG-04) — "the Lord of hosts has a day against all that is proud and lofty, against all that is lifted up — and it shall be brought low" — CHAR-1 as the comprehensive target of the eschatological day. Isa 2:11 (vc=34089, vc=34601): "the haughty looks of man shall be brought low, and the lofty pride of men shall be humbled, and the Lord alone will be exalted in that day" — CHAR-1's universal humbling as the eschatological event. Eze 31:14 (vc=54400, M08-A3-VCG-04): "God's judgment is designed to prevent any future tree from aspiring to such elevation, ending the cycle of proud growth" — the eschatological terminus of CHAR-1 is not fullness but permanent closure of the cycle. Pro 16:18 (vc=34073, M08-A1-VCG-03): "pride goes before destruction" — the structural eschatological trajectory of CHAR-1 is toward destruction, not toward fullness.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Toward eschatological destruction, not fullness. Mal 4:1 (vc=34107, M08-B-VCG-02): "the arrogant and all evildoers will be stubble; the day that is coming shall set them ablaze... it will leave them neither root nor branch" — total eschatological destruction as CHAR-2's terminus. Jer 50:31–32 (vc=34116/34117, M08-B-VCG-02): Babylon ("the most proud one," "arrogance") — "the proud one stumbles and falls, and none will raise him up" — the irreversible fall at the national scale anticipating the eschatological.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Yes — uniquely among M08 characteristics, CHAR-3's VCG-03 form has a positive eschatological orientation. 1Th 2:19 (vc=33913, M08-C-VCG-03): "what is our hope or joy or crown of boasting before our Lord Jesus at his coming? Is it not you?" — the community-boasting is explicitly eschatological, oriented toward Christ's parousia. Phili 2:16 (vc=33910, M08-C-VCG-03): "my pride on the day of Christ" — the examined boasting is oriented toward the eschatological day. 2Cor 1:14 (vc=33907, M08-C-VCG-03): mutual boasting "on the day of our Lord Jesus."

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Toward eschatological judgment, not fullness. 2Ti 3:4 (vc=33926, M08-D-VCG-02): tufoō (being swollen with conceit) in the end-times vice character list — CHAR-4 as a characteristic of the eschatological final days' moral collapse. 1Ti 3:6 (vc=33924, M08-D-VCG-02): "the condemnation of the devil" as the judicial trajectory — the eschatological endpoint is condemnation, not fullness.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Toward eschatological desolation and shame, not fullness. Eze 33:28 (vc=33999, M08-E-VCG-01): "proud might shall come to an end" as the eschatological trajectory of all national power-pride. Jer 51:53 (vc=65670, M08-E-VCG-02): even the highest fortification Babylon could build cannot prevent divine judgment. Hab 2:9 (vc=34169, M08-E-VCG-02): "shame on him who builds his house by unjust gain" — shame, not security, is the eschatological end. Lev 26:19 (vc=33982, M08-E-VCG-01): God will "break the pride of your power" — eschatological breaking.

---

##### T5.6.2 — What does the present experience of this characteristic anticipate about its future fullness?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The present experience of CHAR-1 anticipates its own reversal and judgment, not a positive future state. Isa 14:11 (vc=33988, M08-A3-VCG-02): "your pomp is brought down to Sheol, the sound of your harps; maggots are laid as a bed beneath you" — the present display of CHAR-1 (pomp, grandeur) anticipates its terminus in degradation and death. Pro 29:23 (vc=33960, M08-A4-VCG-04): "one's pride will bring him low" — the present experience of self-elevation structurally anticipates humiliation as its outcome. Isa 2:11 (vc=34089, M08-A2-VCG-01; vc=34601, M08-A3-VCG-04): "the haughty looks of man shall be brought low" — the present posture of haughty-eyed self-elevation anticipates the eschatological day when those looks will specifically be brought down. CHAR-1's present experience offers no anticipation of a positive future fullness — every eschatological trajectory evidenced in the corpus runs toward reversal, humiliation, and the establishment of God's sole exaltation in place of the creature's self-elevation.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

The present experience of CHAR-2 anticipates its eschatological annihilation. Mal 4:1 (vc=34107): the present arrogance ("the arrogant" who are currently calling evildoers blessed — Mal 3:15, vc=34106) anticipates the day when they become "stubble" consumed by fire. Pro 11:2 (vc=34109, M08-B-VCG-02): "when arrogance comes, disgrace follows" — the present experience of CHAR-2 structurally anticipates disgrace as its immediate trajectory. Jer 50:32 (vc=34117): "a fall with no one to restore" — the present self-willed defiance anticipates total and unrecoverable collapse.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

VCG-03 present boasting anticipates the eschatological boasting before Christ (1Th 2:19; Phili 2:16) — the present relational commendation of community members is a foretaste of the eschatological presentation before the Lord. VCG-01 present boasting anticipates exposure and empty consequence (Pro 25:14: clouds and wind without rain; 1Cor 5:6: the corruption spreading). The present experience of CHAR-3 anticipates either eschatological boasting before Christ (VCG-03) or the exposure of its emptiness (VCG-01).

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

The present experience of CHAR-4 anticipates: (a) Epistemic deepening toward blindness: 1Ti 6:4 (vc=33925, M08-D-VCG-02) — the present inflation anticipates the terminal state of understanding nothing; (b) Judicial condemnation: 1Ti 3:6 (vc=33924) — the conceited person's present inflation anticipates the adversarial condemnation-category. (c) Communal disorder: 2Cor 12:20 (vc=33942) — the present conceit anticipates the relational collapse that Paul fears finding.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

The present experience of CHAR-5 anticipates: (a) The sudden removal of the structural foundation: Isa 47:8 (vc=9563, M08-E-VCG-02): Babylon says "I shall not sit as a widow" — the present confident denial anticipates the sudden arrival of exactly what was denied ("these two things shall come to you in a moment" — context of v.9); (b) Total desolation when power is stripped: Eze 33:28 (vc=33999): the present proud might anticipates the desolation that follows its removal; (c) The exposure of structural security as false: Obd 3 (vc=65674): "who will bring me down?" — the present confident question anticipates the answer: God will.

---

##### T5.6.3 — If the evidence is silent on eschatological trajectory, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The eschatological trajectory is extensively evidenced as universal reversal and judgment in the day-of-the-Lord corpus (Isa 2:11–12, 2:17; Isa 10:33; Eze 31:14; M08-A3-VCG-04). Not silent.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Eschatological trajectory evidenced as destruction and unrecoverable fall (Mal 4:1; Jer 50:31–32). Not silent.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Eschatological trajectory evidenced as positive (VCG-03: boasting before Christ) and negative (VCG-01: exposure of emptiness). Not silent.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Eschatological trajectory evidenced as epistemic blindness, judicial condemnation, and communal disorder. Not silent.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Eschatological trajectory evidenced as desolation, shame, and structural removal (Eze 33:28; Jer 51:53; Hab 2:9; Lev 26:19). Not silent.

#### T5.7 — Deposit Consequence

##### T5.7.1 — Where T2.8 has identified a constitutional deposit from sustained operation of this characteristic, what developmental consequence does that deposit produce over time?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (S)

T2.8 found no constitutional body-deposit from sustained CHAR-1. The verse evidence was silent on physical-biological deposit. T5.7 is therefore closed: no deposit developmental consequence to trace from the current evidence base.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (S)

T2.8 found no constitutional body-deposit from CHAR-2. T5.7 is therefore closed.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (S)

T2.8 found no constitutional body-deposit from CHAR-3. T5.7 is therefore closed.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

T2.8 found no constitutional body-deposit from CHAR-4. T5.7 is therefore closed.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (S)

T2.8 found no constitutional body-deposit from CHAR-5. T5.7 is therefore closed.

---

##### T5.7.2 — Does the evidence indicate generational consequence — a deposit carried forward beyond the individual?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (S)

The verse evidence does not explicitly evidence generational biological transmission of CHAR-1. What is evidenced in the national-pride corpus (M08-A3) is communal-cultural transmission: Isa 16:6 (vc=33989, M08-A3-VCG-01) — "we have heard of the pride of Moab" — a corporate identity transmitted as social characteristic across the community rather than as biological deposit; Hos 5:5 (vc=34000, M08-A3-VCG-03) — "the pride of Israel testifies to his face" — collective pride as a communally-held inner characteristic. This communal transmission pattern is distinct from biological/generational deposit. The §3 evidence does not address intergenerational biological transmission as a dimension of CHAR-1's consequence.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

The Neh 9 corpus evidences communal-generational transmission of CHAR-2. Neh 9:16 (vc=34120, M08-B-VCG-01): "our ancestors acted presumptuously"; Neh 9:29 (vc=34126): "even after warnings, they acted presumptuously again" — the pattern crosses generations as a communal characteristic. This is cultural-communal transmission (the pattern persists across the community's historical memory) rather than biological deposit.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

1Cor 5:6 (vc=33903, M08-C-VCG-01): "a little leaven leavens the whole lump" — community boasting produces communal corruption that spreads through the relational whole, which is a form of communal transmission (not biological). The community inherits the moral-cultural corruption generated by its members' boasting. This is social-communal transmission rather than biological deposit.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (S)

The verse evidence does not evidence generational biological transmission of CHAR-4. The community-spreading dynamic of 1Cor 5:6 context (leaven) may apply analogously to CHAR-4, but §3.C does not directly evidence generational transmission.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

The national/collective corpus (ga.on proud-might — Eze 30:6/30:18/32:12/33:28: Egypt's proud might across multiple historical instances) evidences CHAR-5 as a generational-communal characteristic of nations — a multi-generational cultural posture rather than a biological deposit. Eze 16:49 (vc=33979, M08-E-VCG-01): Sodom's pride as a communal-generational character. This is cultural-structural transmission rather than biological generational deposit.

---

##### T5.7.3 — If T2.8 found no deposit, note this explicitly and close T5.7.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (S)

T2.8 found no constitutional body-deposit. T5.7 is closed. Communal-cultural transmission of CHAR-1 across peoples and generations is evidenced in M08-A3 (national collective register) but biological/constitutional deposit is not evidenced. This finding does not affect the T5.7 closure.

---
