## T6 — Relationships with Other Characteristics (24 prompts)

---

### T6

#### T6.1 — Co-occurrence

##### T6.1.1 — Which adjacent characteristics appear most frequently alongside this one in the verse evidence?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Three adjacent characteristics appear consistently alongside CHAR-1 in the verse evidence. First, boasting/self-display (CHAR-3, M08-C): Isa 16:6 (vc=33969, vc=33989, M08-A3-VCG-01) — "we have heard of the pride of Moab — how proud he is — of his arrogance, his pride, and his insolence; in his idle boasting he is not right" — the foundational pride (CHAR-1) and the idle boasting (CHAR-3) appear together as dispositional root and verbal expression; Jer 48:29 (vc=33950, vc=34603, M08-A1-VCG-03) — the same accumulation of pride terms culminating in "the haughtiness of his heart"; 2Ti 3:2 (vc=33933, vc=1899, M08-A4-VCG-01) — filautos/self-love, huperēfanos/arrogance, and boasting in the same vice catalogue sequence. Second, violence and predatory aggression: Psa 73:6 (vc=33959, M08-A2-VCG-02) — "pride is their necklace; violence covers them as a garment" — paired in the same verse as inner disposition and its social expression; Psa 10:2 (vc=33963, M08-A4-VCG-03) — arrogance as the driving force of predatory pursuit of the poor. Third, humility (M09) as the structural opposite named alongside CHAR-1: Jam 4:6 (vc=33931, M08-A4-VCG-01) and 1Pe 5:5 (vc=33934, M08-A4-VCG-01) — "God opposes the proud but gives grace to the humble" — both characteristics named in the same breath as structural opposites; Psa 131:1 (vc=34059, vc=34224, M08-A1-VCG-03, M08-A2-VCG-01) — CHAR-1's absence named through the heart and eyes not lifted.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Three adjacent characteristics co-occur consistently. First, deceitfulness/lying: Psa 119:69 (vc=34100, M08-B-VCG-02): "the insolent smear me with lies"; Psa 119:78 (vc=34101): "the insolent have wronged me with falsehood"; Jer 43:2 (vc=34105, M08-B-VCG-02): "the insolent men said to Jeremiah, 'You are telling a lie'" — deception co-occurs with zed/za.don insolence as its social instrument. Second, contemptuous speech: Psa 119:51 (vc=34099, M08-B-VCG-02): "the insolent utterly deride me"; Pro 21:24 (vc=34096, M08-B-VCG-02): the scoffer's contemptuous posture. Third, domineering social aggression: Mar 10:42 (vc=55588, M08-B-VCG-03): lording over; Mat 24:49 (vc=55613, M08-B-VCG-03): beating fellow servants — CHAR-2 regularly accompanies aggressive authority-assertion.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Three adjacent characteristics co-occur consistently. First, CHAR-1 (Arrogant self-elevation): Jam 4:16 (vc=33866, vc=33886, M08-C-VCG-01): "you boast in your arrogance [alazoneia]" — arrogance (CHAR-1 substrate) and boasting (CHAR-3 expression) appear in the same verse as source and expression. 2Ti 3:2 (vc=33868, M08-C-VCG-01): huperēfanos (arrogance — CHAR-1) listed immediately before alazōn (braggart — CHAR-3) in the same vice catalogue. Second, worldly orientation/love-of-world: 1Jo 2:16 (vc=33865, M08-C-VCG-01): alazoneia paired with "the desires of the flesh and the desires of the eyes" — CHAR-3 as one of three worldly orientations. Third, self-love (filautos): 2Ti 3:2 (vc=33868): filautos (self-love) → huperēfanos (arrogance) → alazōn (boasting) — the vice catalogue places all three in direct sequence.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Three adjacent characteristics co-occur consistently. First, the absence of love (M09-adjacent): 1Cor 8:1 (vc=33935, M08-D-VCG-01): "knowledge puffs up, but love builds up" — CHAR-4 and love are placed in direct structural opposition; 1Cor 13:4 (vc=33936, M08-D-VCG-01): "love is not arrogant [fusioō]" — love's absence is CHAR-4's enabling condition. Second, relational disorder (co-occurring in 2Cor 12:20, vc=33942, M08-D-VCG-02): fusiōsis among quarreling, jealousy, anger, hostility, slander, gossip — CHAR-4 as embedded in and generating relational disorder. Third, CHAR-1 (arrogant self-elevation) as the dispositional substrate: CHAR-4 is the cognitive expression of CHAR-1's dispositional elevation (the same self-elevation that CHAR-1 holds as a posture, CHAR-4 holds as a cognitive self-picture).

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Three adjacent characteristics co-occur consistently. First, social neglect of the vulnerable (adjacent to social-justice clusters): Eze 16:49 (vc=33979, M08-E-VCG-01) — CHAR-5 paired directly with failure to aid the poor and needy — the structural contempt for the vulnerable is CHAR-5's consistent relational co-occurrence. Second, exploitation/unjust-gain: Hab 2:9 (vc=34169, M08-E-VCG-02) — CHAR-5 co-occurs with the deliberate accumulation of position through unjust means toward social others. Third, CHAR-1 (arrogant self-elevation) as the dispositional substrate: CHAR-5 is CHAR-1 expressed through the structural-power medium — the heart becoming proud (Eze 28:5, vc=34046) is CHAR-1's dispositional movement, with the structural goods as the specific occasion.

---

##### T6.1.2 — What does the pattern of co-occurrence reveal about this characteristic's place in the inner-being landscape?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The co-occurrence pattern reveals three things about CHAR-1's place in the inner-being landscape. First, CHAR-1 is a generative disposition: it consistently appears as the dispositional root from which CHAR-3 (boasting) and predatory agency flow — the co-occurrence is causal (CHAR-1 as source) rather than merely associative. Second, CHAR-1 sits at the centre of a cluster of moral failures: Mar 7:22 (vc=33928, M08-A4-VCG-01) places it among "wickedness, deceit, sensuality, envy, slander, pride, foolishness" as co-products of the fallen heart — CHAR-1 is one member of a broader inner-being disorder cluster, not an isolated vice. Third, CHAR-1 is definitionally paired with M09 (humility) as its structural opposite — the two characteristics are conceptually inseparable in the evidence; every explicit naming of one tends to entail reference to the other (Jam 4:6; 1Pe 5:5; Pro 29:23, vc=33960; Psa 131:1). This pairing reveals that CHAR-1 occupies one pole of a fundamental inner-being polarity whose other pole is M09.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

The pattern reveals that CHAR-2 (presumptuous defiance against authority) consistently generates two downstream expressions: deception (using lies to undermine the authority-bearers and their standards) and social domination (asserting self-willed authority over others). These are CHAR-2's characteristic outward expressions: against God's standards (deceit dismisses prophetic truth — Jer 43:2) and against social others (domination replaces legitimate relational structure). The co-occurrence is causal — CHAR-2's self-authorising will naturally produces both deceptive self-justification and domineering social assertion.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

The co-occurrence pattern reveals that CHAR-3 consistently appears downstream of CHAR-1 in the same catalogues and verses — it is CHAR-1's verbal/social expression. The 2Ti 3:2 sequence (filautos → huperēfanos → alazōn) confirms the programme's structural mapping: self-love (root) → arrogant self-elevation (CHAR-1 disposition) → boasting/self-display (CHAR-3 expression). CHAR-3's consistent co-occurrence with worldly orientation (1Jo 2:16) and self-love confirms that it is constitutively embedded in the broader M08 cluster rather than standing as an isolated vice.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

The co-occurrence pattern reveals that CHAR-4 consistently: (a) generates relational disorder (2Cor 12:20) as its social consequence; (b) excludes love (1Cor 8:1; 13:4) as its structural relational opposite; (c) follows CHAR-1's dispositional self-elevation as its cognitive expression. CHAR-4 is not an isolated vice but the cognitive member of the M08 cluster's dispositional (CHAR-1), transgressive (CHAR-2), verbal (CHAR-3), cognitive (CHAR-4) progression.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

The co-occurrence pattern reveals that CHAR-5's structural-power pride consistently generates social injustice as its relational consequence: the pride-of-power produces indifference to the poor (Eze 16:49), exploitation of others (Hab 2:9), and imperial contempt for weaker nations (the ga.on Egypt corpus — Eze 30–32). The co-occurrence with social neglect and exploitation is not incidental — it is structural to CHAR-5: the self-sufficiency conviction ("I am, and there is no one besides me" — Isa 47:8, vc=9563) generates the relational posture that excludes the neighbour in need from the moral horizon.

---

##### T6.1.3 — If no significant co-occurrence patterns emerge, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Significant co-occurrence patterns are evidenced across three adjacent characteristics (CHAR-3, violence/predatory aggression, and M09 as structural opposite). Not silent.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Significant co-occurrence patterns evidenced (deception, contemptuous speech, domineering aggression). Not silent.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Significant co-occurrence patterns evidenced (CHAR-1 as source, self-love as root, worldly orientation as context). Not silent.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Significant co-occurrence patterns evidenced (absence of love, relational disorder, CHAR-1 as substrate). Not silent.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Significant co-occurrence patterns evidenced (social neglect, exploitation, CHAR-1 as dispositional substrate). Not silent.

---

#### T6.2 — Sequential Relationships

##### T6.2.1 — Does the verse evidence show this characteristic consistently preceding, following, or accompanying another characteristic in a sequence?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes. CHAR-1 consistently precedes three outcomes in sequentially-evidenced relationships. First, destruction/fall: Pro 16:18 (vc=34073, M08-A1-VCG-03) — "pride goes before destruction, and a haughty spirit before a fall" — the sequential relationship is stated as a structural law; Pro 18:12 (vc=34041, M08-A1-VCG-03) — "before destruction a man's heart is haughty, but humility comes before honour" — CHAR-1 placed immediately before destruction in the sequence. Pro 16:18 (vc=33978, M08-A4-VCG-04) repeats the same structural law: pride precedes destruction. Second, forgetfulness of God: Deu 8:14 (vc=34223, M08-A1-VCG-01) — heart lifted → God forgotten; Hos 13:6 (vc=34232, M08-A1-VCG-01) — fullness → heart lifted → "therefore they forgot me" — a tight causal sequence. Third, unfaithfulness and moral failure: 2Ch 26:16 (vc=34044, M08-A1-VCG-01) — growing strong → growing proud → unfaithfulness to God; Eze 28:17 (vc=34047, M08-A1-VCG-02) — heart proud → wisdom corrupted → humiliation. The sequence runs consistently in one direction: CHAR-1 precedes and causes these downstream states, not the reverse.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

CHAR-2 consistently precedes: (a) Disgrace: Pro 11:2 (vc=34109, M08-B-VCG-02): "when arrogance [za.don] comes, disgrace follows" — sequential causal law; (b) Strife: Pro 13:10 (vc=34113, M08-B-VCG-02): "by insolence [za.don] comes nothing but strife" — stated as an invariant sequential consequence; (c) Irreversible fall: Jer 50:32 (vc=34117, M08-B-VCG-02): "arrogance results in a fall with no one to restore"; (d) Eschatological destruction: Mal 4:1 (vc=34107, M08-B-VCG-02): CHAR-2 preceding the day of fire. The sequence is structurally causal, not merely correlational.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

CHAR-3 consistently follows CHAR-1 (as its verbal expression) and precedes: (a) community corruption (1Cor 5:6, vc=33903, M08-C-VCG-01: leaven → whole lump); (b) social exposure of hollowness (Pro 25:14, vc=33358: clouds/wind without rain); (c) divine judgment (Jam 4:16, vc=33923: "all such boasting is evil"). Additionally, in the positive sequence: CHAR-3 (VCG-02/03) follows the cross-formation evacuation of worldly grounds (Gal 6:14) and precedes the eschatological boasting before Christ (1Th 2:19; Phili 2:16).

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

CHAR-4 consistently precedes: (a) Relational disorder: 2Cor 12:20 (vc=33942, M08-D-VCG-02): fusiōsis preceding the cluster of relational sins; (b) Epistemic blindness: 1Ti 6:4 (vc=33925, M08-D-VCG-02): conceit preceding "understanding nothing" and "controversy-craving"; (c) Judicial condemnation: 1Ti 3:6 (vc=33924, M08-D-VCG-02): conceit preceding "the condemnation of the devil." CHAR-4 follows the receipt of cognitive goods without love-anchor (1Cor 8:1, vc=33935: knowledge received → CHAR-4 activated).

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

CHAR-5 consistently follows received structural goods (military power, wealth, ease, fortified position) and precedes: (a) Social injustice: Eze 16:49 (vc=33979, M08-E-VCG-01): CHAR-5 → failure to aid the poor and needy; (b) Divine reversal: Lev 26:19 (vc=33982): CHAR-5 → God's breaking of the power; Eze 30:6 (vc=33996): CHAR-5 → "her proud might shall come down"; (c) Desolation: Eze 33:28 (vc=33999): CHAR-5 → total desolation. The sequential structure is: structural goods received → CHAR-5 activated → social injustice and divine reversal.

---

##### T6.2.2 — What does the sequence reveal — is the relationship causal, developmental, or correlational?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The relationship is causal. The wisdom tradition frames it as a structural causal law: Pro 16:18 (vc=34073, M08-A1-VCG-03) — "pride goes before destruction" — stated without exception as a governing principle, not as a statistical correlation. Job 22:29 (vc=34093, M08-A4-VCG-04) — "when they are humbled you say, 'it is because of pride'" — retrospective causal attribution: humiliation is explained by pride as its cause. Deu 8:14 (vc=34223) provides the tightest causal chain: prosperity → heart lifted (CHAR-1 activated) → God forgotten (next state caused). The mechanism of causation is the perceptive/cognitive closure CHAR-1 produces (T3.1, T3.2, T3.3): CHAR-1 closes off the inner faculties (perception of God, memory of divine provision, wisdom) that would prevent forgetfulness, unfaithfulness, and the subsequent catastrophic consequences. The sequence is causal, not merely developmental or correlational.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Causal. Pro 11:2 (vc=34109) states it as a structural law: "when arrogance comes, disgrace follows" — no qualification, no exception. Pro 13:10 (vc=34113): "by insolence comes nothing but strife" — stated causally. The mechanism is social: CHAR-2's wilful transgression of authority and limits provokes response from the authority-bearing structures (divine judgment, social opposition, relational conflict), and that response is the disgrace, strife, and fall that follows.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

The sequence confirms CHAR-3 as CHAR-1's verbal/social outwork: CHAR-1 generates the inner elevation (disposition); CHAR-3 enacts it publicly through speech and self-display. In the VCG-01 direction, CHAR-3 then produces corruption and exposure. In the VCG-03 direction, God-directed boasting produces relational joy and eschatological confidence. The sequence reveals CHAR-3 as the pivot between inner disposition (CHAR-1) and social consequence — the characteristic through which inner elevation becomes publicly enacted.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

The sequence confirms CHAR-4 as: (a) downstream from received cognitive goods misprocessed without love (1Cor 8:1); (b) upstream from relational disorder, epistemic blindness, and judgment. The sequential position of CHAR-4 places it as the cognitive-mediation stage through which received goods become relational damage — the inflated self-picture generated from knowledge/experience then produces the downstream harm.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

The sequence confirms CHAR-5 as the proud inner posture activated by received structural goods and generating two downstream consequences: social injustice (relational direction) and divine reversal (divine-judicial direction). The sequence is causal: the structural-power pride causes the social contempt (Eze 16:49) and invites the divine breaking (Lev 26:19). The consistency of this sequence across Egypt, Israel, Sodom, Babylon, Edom, and Tyre confirms it as a structural causal law rather than a situational correlation.

---

##### T6.2.3 — If no sequential pattern is evidenced, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Sequential causal pattern extensively evidenced (CHAR-1 → forgetfulness → unfaithfulness → destruction). Not silent.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Sequential causal pattern evidenced: CHAR-2 → disgrace, strife, fall, destruction. Not silent.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Sequential pattern evidenced: CHAR-1 → CHAR-3 → corruption/exposure (VCG-01) or CHAR-3 → eschatological boasting (VCG-03). Not silent.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Sequential pattern evidenced (knowledge received → CHAR-4 → disorder/blindness/condemnation). Not silent.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Sequential pattern evidenced: structural goods → CHAR-5 → social injustice + divine reversal. Not silent.

---

#### T6.3 — Causal and Constitutive Relationships

##### T6.3.1 — Does this characteristic produce another characteristic in the verse evidence — and if so, which one, and by what mechanism?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes. CHAR-1 produces two downstream characteristics directly evidenced in the same verses. First, boasting/self-display (CHAR-3, M08-C): Isa 16:6 (vc=33969, vc=33989, M08-A3-VCG-01) — Moab's foundational pride (CHAR-1) generates "his insolence; in his idle boasting" — the boasting flows from the pride as its verbal/public expression; the mechanism is that the inner elevation of self (CHAR-1) naturally seeks external affirmation through proclamation of that elevated status (CHAR-3). 2Ti 3:2 (vc=33933, M08-A4-VCG-01) — "proud, arrogant, abusive" — pride and arrogance preceding boasting and abusive speech in the same sequence. Second, predatory aggression (adjacent to CHAR-2, Presumptuous defiance): Psa 10:2 (vc=33963, M08-A4-VCG-03) — "in arrogance the wicked hotly pursue the poor" — CHAR-1 as "the inner driving force" that generates the pursuing action; the mechanism is that CHAR-1's elevated self-position over others removes the relational constraint that would prevent treating others as objects to be dominated.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

CHAR-2 produces the scoffer identity as its dispositional maturation. Pro 21:24 (vc=34096, vc=34114, M08-B-VCG-02): "haughty, arrogant, 'scoffer' is his name; he acts with arrogant pride [za.don]" — sustained CHAR-2 generates the stable scoffer persona whose defining characteristic is contemptuous disregard for all authority and moral standard. Additionally, CHAR-2 produces relational strife (Pro 13:10: za.don → strife) and the social conditions of oppression for the godly (Psa 119:85: CHAR-2 → pitfall-setting against the law-keepers).

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

VCG-01 CHAR-3 produces community moral corruption (1Cor 5:6, vc=33903: leaven spreading) and social hollow reputation (Pro 25:14; Pro 20:14, vc=33357 — the buyer's duplicity that is eventually exposed). For VCG-02/03: CHAR-3 examined and redirected produces the relational commendation and eschatological joy evidenced in Paul's community relationship — a positive social product rather than a harmful one.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

CHAR-4 produces: (a) Verbal boasting/self-display (CHAR-3): 1Cor 4:19 (vc=33939, M08-D-VCG-01): the arrogant persons' "talk" — the inflated cognitive self-picture generates verbal self-assertion (CHAR-3's domain); (b) Relational controversy and disorder: 1Ti 6:4 (vc=33925, M08-D-VCG-02): "unhealthy craving for controversy and for quarrels about words" — CHAR-4 drives verbal combat; (c) Communal dysfunction: 1Cor 4:6 (vc=33937): partisan inflation disrupting community unity; 1Cor 5:2 (vc=33940): collective CHAR-4 preventing appropriate community moral response.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

CHAR-5 produces: (a) Self-sufficient speech and declaration — Isa 47:8 (vc=9563, M08-E-VCG-02): the power-pride generates the verbal self-declaration "I am, and there is no one besides me" — overlapping with CHAR-3's verbal expression; (b) Imperious self-will — Eze 16:30 (vc=57959, M08-E-VCG-02): shal.le.tet, brazen unrestrained self-assertion from structural position; (c) Exploitative agency — Hab 2:9 (vc=34169, M08-E-VCG-02): unjust-gain strategy enabled by CHAR-5's structural confidence. These are the downstream characteristic expressions that CHAR-5's structural-power pride generates.

---

##### T6.3.2 — Is this characteristic produced by another — and if so, which one?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes. The verse evidence evidences self-love (filautos) as the root that produces CHAR-1. 2Ti 3:2 (vc=1899, M08-A4-VCG-01) — "people will be lovers of self [filautos], lovers of money, proud, arrogant, abusive" — filautos heads the list from which arrogance and pride flow; the mechanism is that the inward orientation of the self toward itself as the primary value (self-love) generates the upward movement of that self above others (CHAR-1). Mar 7:22 (vc=33928, M08-A4-VCG-01) confirms the internal origin: pride is among "the evil things that flow out of a person" — originating from within the fallen inner person, not from outside. The occasion-triggers (prosperity — Deu 8:14, vc=34223; power — 2Ch 26:16, vc=34044; beauty — Eze 28:17, vc=34047) activate filautos into CHAR-1's specific self-elevating form.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

CHAR-2 is produced by CHAR-1 (arrogant self-elevation) as its dispositional substrate. As established in the programme's characteristic mapping (and consistent with T6.5 in the CHAR-1 findings): CHAR-1's elevated self-regard generates the will's assumption of authority over its own actions (CHAR-2's self-authorising claim). The enabling conditions for CHAR-2 (absence of God-fear, contempt for law, self-deceptive overconfidence in one's position — T1.7.1) are themselves downstream from CHAR-1's heart-elevation. The za.don/zed corpus of M08-B-VCG-02 shares the dispositional substrate with CHAR-1's ga.on/huperēfanos register.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

CHAR-3 is produced by CHAR-1 (arrogant self-elevation) as its verbal/social expression. Jam 4:16 (vc=33866): alazoneia (inner CHAR-3 substrate) generates the boasting act; but alazoneia itself is grounded in the CHAR-1 arrogance that precedes it. 2Ti 3:2 (vc=33868): the sequence filautos → huperēfanos → alazōn confirms the generative chain: self-love → CHAR-1 arrogance → CHAR-3 boasting. CHAR-3 is the downstream verbal product of CHAR-1's inner elevation.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

CHAR-4 is produced by CHAR-1 (arrogant self-elevation) as its cognitive expression: the dispositional self-elevation of CHAR-1 generates the inflated cognitive self-picture of CHAR-4. Additionally, CHAR-4 is triggered by received cognitive goods misprocessed through the absence of love: 1Cor 8:1 (vc=33935, M08-D-VCG-01): "knowledge puffs up" — the receipt of knowledge (without love) is the direct trigger. Partisan attachment (1Cor 4:6, vc=33937) and ungrounded spiritual experience (Col 2:18, vc=33941) are further occasion-triggers that activate CHAR-4 from the CHAR-1 dispositional substrate.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

CHAR-5 is produced by CHAR-1 (arrogant self-elevation) as its structural-power sub-form: the same dispositional self-elevation that CHAR-1 expresses generally, CHAR-5 expresses through the specific medium of received structural goods. Eze 28:5 (vc=34046, M08-E-VCG-02): "your heart became proud" — the heart-elevation (CHAR-1's dispositional territory) is generated by received wealth, producing CHAR-5's structural-power form. Additionally, CHAR-5 is produced by the receipt of genuine structural goods without proper God-directed stewardship — the enabling condition (received power/wealth/ease) is necessary for CHAR-5 to arise.

---

##### T6.3.3 — Is this characteristic a constituent element of another, or does another characteristic constitute part of this one?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Two constitutive relationships are evidenced. First, CHAR-1 constitutes the dispositional ground from which CHAR-3 (boasting) emerges as its expressive form: Isa 16:6 (vc=33969, vc=33989, M08-A3-VCG-01) — the pride is the inner root (CHAR-1) from which the boasting is the outer expression (CHAR-3); the two stand in a constitutive relationship as ground and expression. Second, filautos (self-love) constitutes part of CHAR-1's generative base as its root: 2Ti 3:2 (vc=1899) — self-love is the inner orientation that CHAR-1 requires; CHAR-1 is self-love turned outward into competitive self-elevation above others. Additionally, CHAR-1 appears to constitute the dispositional precondition for CHAR-2 (presumptuous defiance — M08-B): the will's settled elevation of self (CHAR-1) is the inner state from which the specific volitional act of defying a divine boundary (CHAR-2) can emerge — CHAR-1 as dispositional ground, CHAR-2 as its activated form in the face of a specific limit.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

CHAR-1 constitutes part of CHAR-2's substrate: CHAR-2's self-authorising will arises from the elevated self-regard (CHAR-1) that has not been submitted to divine authority. In the opposite direction, CHAR-2 may be a constituent expression of CHAR-1's dispositional energy when it encounters a specific divine limit — CHAR-2 is what CHAR-1's unconstrained volition does when it hits an authority boundary. The relationship is constitutive: CHAR-1 generates the dispositional ground; CHAR-2 is one of its characteristic activations.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

CHAR-1 constitutes CHAR-3's dispositional ground (the arrogance from which the boasting emerges). CHAR-3 constitutes the expressive form of CHAR-1 — it is CHAR-1 made public and verbal. The relationship is constitutive in both directions: CHAR-1 provides CHAR-3's inner substrate; CHAR-3 is CHAR-1's outer expression. The VCG-03 form of CHAR-3 may constitute part of M22 (praise/glorying of God) — the God-directed boasting of VCG-03 is adjacent to the praise-register of M22, sharing vocabulary and direction. (See carry-forward observation below.)

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

CHAR-1 constitutes the dispositional ground of CHAR-4: the same self-elevation that CHAR-1 holds as a general posture, CHAR-4 embodies as a cognitive self-assessment. CHAR-4 is CHAR-1's cognitive sub-form — it is the specific expression of dispositional self-elevation through the mind's self-assessment faculty. CHAR-4 in turn constitutes the inner cognitive stage from which CHAR-3 (verbal boasting) emerges as expression: CHAR-4 is the inner cognitive reality; CHAR-3 is what it produces when verbalized.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

CHAR-1 constitutes CHAR-5's dispositional ground: CHAR-5 is the specific form of CHAR-1's dispositional self-elevation when that elevation is mediated through and sustained by structural power. CHAR-5 in turn constitutes a misuse-form of M23 (strength/power/dominion): the cross-register flag (M23) identifies that CHAR-5's primary terms (ga.on proud-might, ma.rom, shal.le.tet, archō) carry their primary register in M23's legitimate strength faculty; CHAR-5 is the corruption of the M23 faculty when that strength becomes the ground for self-aggrandisement. CHAR-5 constitutes the M08 manifestation of the M23 faculty's potential misuse.

---

##### T6.3.4 — If no causal or constitutive relationship is evidenced, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Causal and constitutive relationships are evidenced: CHAR-1 produces CHAR-3 (boasting) and predatory aggression; CHAR-1 is produced by filautos (self-love); CHAR-1 constitutes the dispositional ground for CHAR-2 (presumptuous defiance). Not silent.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Causal and constitutive relationships evidenced: CHAR-2 produces scoffer-identity and strife; CHAR-2 is produced by CHAR-1's dispositional substrate; CHAR-1 constitutes CHAR-2's generative ground. Not silent.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Causal and constitutive relationships evidenced: CHAR-3 produced by CHAR-1; CHAR-3 constituted by CHAR-1 as its inner ground; CHAR-3 VCG-03 adjacent to M22 praise register. Not silent.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Causal and constitutive relationships evidenced: CHAR-4 produced by CHAR-1 (cognitive expression of dispositional elevation); CHAR-4 produces CHAR-3 (verbal expression of cognitive inflation); CHAR-1 constitutes CHAR-4's dispositional ground. Not silent.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Causal and constitutive relationships evidenced: CHAR-5 produced by CHAR-1's dispositional ground; CHAR-5 is CHAR-1 through structural medium; CHAR-5 constitutes the M23 faculty's misuse-form within M08. Not silent.

---

#### T6.4 — Vocabulary and Root Sharing

##### T6.4.1 — Does this characteristic share vocabulary terms with other characteristics in the programme?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes. The primary vocabulary terms of CHAR-1 are shared with at least two other clusters. First, M22 (Divine Majesty and Exaltation): rum (H7311A) spans both CHAR-1's human self-elevation register and M22's divine exaltation register — confirmed by the Phase 5.5 set-aside of 122 M22-register verses from rum, ga.on, ga.vah, ga.a.vah, ge.ut, go.vah, ga.ah. The same Hebrew terms that name God's legitimate exaltation (M22) also name the creature's illegitimate self-elevation (M08/CHAR-1). Second, M09 (Humility): huperēfanos (G5244) appears in M08-A4-VCG-01 (CHAR-1's arrogance) and in Jam 4:6 and 1Pe 5:5 where it is placed directly against M09's tapeinophrosynē (humility) — the vocabulary of CHAR-1 is definitionally entangled with the vocabulary of M09. Third, ga.on (H1347) spans M08's national-pride register and M22's divine-glory register (the 122 M22 set-asides included ga.on as a term with dual-register function).

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

The primary zid/za.don/zed vocabulary of CHAR-2 is largely distinctive to M08-B within the M08 cluster — it does not span multiple clusters in the way CHAR-1's rum/ga.on vocabulary does. However, za.don/zed/zid carry both the M08-B (presumptuous defiance) register and an adjacent arrogance register that overlaps with CHAR-1 at the edges: Isa 13:11 (vc=34104, M08-B-VCG-02): "the arrogant [zed] person" appears in a verse whose broader context also carries CHAR-1 material. The Greek authadēs (G0829) and tolmētēs (G5113) are not evidenced in other M08 characteristics' vocabulary sets in the current corpus.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Yes, extensively. The kauchaomai family (kauchaomai/kauchēma/kauchēsis) spans all three of CHAR-3's VCGs and crosses the M08–M22 boundary: the same verb that names self-directed condemned boasting (VCG-01) also names God-directed glorying (VCG-03) and Pauline examined self-commendation (VCG-02). The ha.lal root similarly spans M08's self-boasting sense (VCG-01) and M22's praise-of-God register (the 22 ha.lal praise verses in M22). This is the most extensive vocabulary sharing in M08: CHAR-3 shares its primary vocabulary with M22 (Divine Praise and Thanksgiving) at the root level.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

The primary fusioō/tufoō/huperfroneō vocabulary of CHAR-4 is largely distinctive within M08. Fusioō does not appear in CHAR-1's rum/ga.on vocabulary set or in CHAR-2's zid/za.don vocabulary — it is specific to the cognitive-inflation register. Huperfroneō (to think above) belongs to the same huper- prefix family as huperēfanos (above + appear — CHAR-1's Greek vocabulary), suggesting root-level proximity without term-sharing. The conceptual overlap between CHAR-1's self-elevation and CHAR-4's cognitive self-inflation is confirmed by the shared huper- prefix etymology.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Yes, extensively. Ga.on (H1347) spans M08-CHAR-5 (proud-might subset) and M22 (divine majesty — confirmed by the 122 M22-register ga.on/rum set-aside at Phase 5.5). Ma.rom (H4791) spans M08-CHAR-5 (fortified-elevation register) and M23 (strength/height in its legitimate exercise). Hupsēlofroneō (G5309) contains the huper- prefix shared with CHAR-1's huperēfanos (G5244) and CHAR-4's huperfroneō (G5252) — the huper- prefix family spans CHAR-1 (dispositional above-others appearance), CHAR-4 (cognitive above-measure thinking), and CHAR-5 (wealth-grounded above-others haughtiness). This is the most cross-characteristic vocabulary overlap in M08's Greek evidence.

---

##### T6.4.2 — Does vocabulary sharing extend to root-level architecture — a shared root that generates terms across two or more characteristics?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes. The Hebrew g-'-h root is the most extensive cross-characteristic root sharing evidenced. From this root: ga.ah (H1342, to rise/soar — Job 10:16, vc=33945, M08-A2-VCG-02), ga.on (H1347, pride/majesty — extensive M08-A3 use), ga.a.vah (H1346, arrogance/pride — M08-A4-VCG-03 extensive), ga.vah (H1361, to exalt/be proud — M08-A1 extensive), ga.vo.ah (H1364, high/haughty — M08-A1-VCG-03), ge.eh (H1343, proud — M08-A4-VCG-02), ge.ah (H1344, pride — M08-A4-VCG-04), ge.ut (H1348, majesty/pride — M08-A3-VCG-02), ge.vah (H1466, pride/height — M08-A4-VCG-04). This single root generates the majority of CHAR-1's Hebrew vocabulary and simultaneously generates terms used in the M22 divine-majesty register. The rum (r-w-m) root similarly generates terms across M08 (CHAR-1), M22 (divine exaltation), and the positive "God lifts up the humble" register (M39 adjacent). Two root families span both human self-elevation (CHAR-1) and divine genuine exaltation (M22).

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

The z-d root family (zid, za.don, zed) is primarily distinctive to CHAR-2 within M08, without the cross-register spanning of CHAR-1's roots. The closest root-level sharing is the conceptual overlap between za.don/zed (insolent disregard for divine law) and CHAR-1's ga.on/ge.eh vocabulary (self-elevation above divine limits) — both root families describe the self exceeding its proper creaturely station, but through different conceptual paths (za.don through wilful law-contempt; ga.on through dispositional self-elevation). They share a conceptual family without sharing specific roots.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Yes. The kauchaomai root (Greek) and the ha.lal root (Hebrew) both span M08-CHAR-3 and M22 (divine praise/glorying). The register-distinction is direction (self-directed vs God-directed), not root. This is the carry-forward observation from the brief: M08-C ↔ M22 register-adjacency through shared vocabulary. The Phase 7 VCG design addressed this by separating the three VCG registers within CHAR-3: VCG-01 (condemned self-boasting), VCG-02 (Pauline examined), VCG-03 (God-directed glorying — M22 cross-register). The same root/word, different directions.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Yes, at the prefix level. Huperfroneō (CHAR-4) and huperēfanos (CHAR-1's Greek primary term) both use the huper- (above, over) prefix — confirming that both characteristics operate in the "above proper station" semantic domain, with huperēfanos naming the visible social expression (appearing above others) and huperfroneō naming the cognitive expression (thinking above what is warranted). The huper- prefix family spans CHAR-1 (huperēfanos), CHAR-4 (huperfroneō), and the relational register (huperoraō, huperairō). This root-level architecture confirms M08's self-elevation characteristics as organised around the same spatial-metaphorical core (above/over), differentiated by faculty (disposition, cognition, social visibility).

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Yes. The ga.on/ga.vah root (g-'-h family) spans M08-CHAR-1 (dispositional self-elevation), M08-CHAR-5 (proud-might subset), and M22 (divine majesty) — the same root family generates terms across three registers. The huper- prefix spans CHAR-1, CHAR-4, and CHAR-5 in Greek. The ma.rom/rum root spans M08-CHAR-5 and M22 (God's exaltation). The carry-forward observation (M08-E ↔ M23) is evidenced at the root level: ga.on, ma.rom, shal.le.tet, and archō all carry their primary lexical register in M23 (strength/power/dominion); they remain in M08-CHAR-5 because the §3.D verses evidence the M23 faculty corrupted into self-exaltation.

---

##### T6.4.3 — What does vocabulary sharing reveal about the conceptual relationship between characteristics?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The vocabulary sharing between CHAR-1 and M22 reveals that arrogant self-elevation is conceptually parasitic on divine genuine exaltation: the creature uses the same vocabulary — the same spatial metaphor of upward elevation — that Scripture reserves for God's legitimate exaltation, but applies it to the creature's illegitimate claim. Isa 2:11 (vc=34601, M08-A3-VCG-04) states the resolution: "the Lord alone will be exalted in that day" — the shared vocabulary creates a narrative tension that is resolved eschatologically when the proper subject of the elevation terms (God alone) is re-established and the improper subject (the creature) is brought low. This conceptual parasitism also explains why the Phase 5.5 set-aside was structurally necessary: the same terms appear in both M08 and M22 because CHAR-1 is the creature's mirror-inversion of M22, operating with M22's vocabulary in the wrong direction and with the wrong subject.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

The relative distinctiveness of CHAR-2's vocabulary (z-d root family) from CHAR-1's vocabulary (g-'-h and r-w-m roots) confirms the analytical distinction between the two characteristics: they are constitutively related (CHAR-1 generates CHAR-2's dispositional ground) but lexically distinguished (the zid "boiling" vocabulary specifically names the act-of-transgression that goes beyond the dispositional-elevation named by ga.on/rum). The vocabulary confirms that Scripture distinguishes the inner disposition (CHAR-1) from the transgressive act (CHAR-2) through different root families.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

The vocabulary sharing between CHAR-3 and M22 reveals that boasting/glorying and praising/glorying are the same inner-being impulse directed differently: toward the self (CHAR-3 VCG-01) or toward God (M22). The impulse to exult in, celebrate, and publicly affirm something is a created human capacity; the direction of its expression determines whether it is M08 (self-directed) or M22 (God-directed). This conceptual relationship makes CHAR-3 the most direct M08 ↔ M22 bridge: the condemned boasting of VCG-01 and the God-directed glorying of VCG-03 are the same faculty expressed in opposite directions. The VCG-03 verses are in CHAR-3's corpus because they address the boasting-impulse's redirection — they belong here as the examined contrast, while their fully God-directed form will be addressed when M22 opens.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

The huper- prefix shared between CHAR-1's huperēfanos and CHAR-4's huperfroneō reveals that these two characteristics are the same spatial-metaphorical movement (self-elevation above proper station) applied to two different faculties: CHAR-1 in the dispositional-social register (appearing above others) and CHAR-4 in the cognitive register (thinking above what is warranted). CHAR-4 is the cognitive form of CHAR-1 at the vocabulary level — confirmed by the shared prefix root.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

The vocabulary sharing between CHAR-5 and M23 reveals that CHAR-5 is structurally parasitic on M23's legitimate strength faculty: the same ga.on that names God's genuine majesty (M22) and legitimate human strength (M23) names the creature's self-exaltation based on that strength (CHAR-5). The conceptual relationship is the same as between CHAR-1 and M22 (rum spanning both): CHAR-5 is what happens to M23's strength-faculty when it becomes the ground for self-aggrandisement rather than God-serving stewardship. This makes CHAR-5 the M08 characteristic most directly dependent on M23's content for understanding — CHAR-5 is M23's misuse-pole, as CHAR-1 is M22's misuse-pole.

---

##### T6.4.4 — If no significant vocabulary sharing is evidenced, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Vocabulary sharing is extensively evidenced between CHAR-1 (M08) and M22, between CHAR-1 and M09, and at root level through the g-'-h and r-w-m root families spanning multiple clusters. Not silent.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

CHAR-2's vocabulary is largely distinctive within M08; conceptual overlap with CHAR-1 is evidenced without root-level sharing. Vocabulary relationship evidenced as conceptually adjacent but lexically distinguished. Not fully silent.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Vocabulary sharing extensively evidenced between CHAR-3 (M08-C) and M22 through the kauchaomai and ha.lal root families. This is the carry-forward observation for CHAR-3 addressed. Not silent.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Vocabulary sharing evidenced at the huper- prefix level (huperfroneō/huperēfanos shared root, CHAR-4/CHAR-1 relationship confirmed). Not silent.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Vocabulary sharing extensively evidenced: ga.on/ma.rom spanning M08-CHAR-5 and M22/M23; huper- prefix family spanning CHAR-1, CHAR-4, and CHAR-5 in Greek. The carry-forward observation (M08-E ↔ M23) is confirmed through vocabulary analysis. Not silent.

---

#### T6.5 — Distinctions

##### T6.5.1 — Which adjacent characteristic most closely resembles this one — and what precisely distinguishes them?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

CHAR-2 (Presumptuous defiance — M08-B) most closely resembles CHAR-1. The precise distinction: CHAR-1 is the settled inner dispositional elevation of the self above its proper creaturely station — what the self fundamentally is and claims to be (above God and others). CHAR-2 is the specific volitional act of the self asserting itself against a known divine limit or authority — what the self wilfully does against an external constraint. CHAR-1 is disposition; CHAR-2 is act. The M08-A4-VCG-05 evidence that sits closest to the CHAR-1/CHAR-2 boundary: Num 15:30 (vc=65731, M08-A4-VCG-05) — acting "with a high hand" describes "an inner posture of defiant self-exaltation against God" — it was assigned CHAR-1 because the primary evidence is the elevated inner posture; the M08-B zid/za.don/zed vocabulary names the act of boiling over against a specific divine command, which is constitutionally adjacent but functionally distinct. Dan 11:36 (vc=34235, M08-A1-VCG-02) — "the king shall do as he wills; he shall exalt himself" — sits in CHAR-1 because the primary evidence is the inner volitional self-exaltation (dispositional), though the act-form (doing as he wills) is also present.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

CHAR-1 (Arrogant self-elevation) most closely resembles CHAR-2. The distinction (established also in CHAR-1's T6.5 findings): CHAR-1 is the settled inner disposition of self-elevation (what the self fundamentally is and claims — above God and others); CHAR-2 is the specific volitional act of the self asserting itself against a known divine limit or appointed authority (what the self wilfully does against an external constraint). Deu 18:20 (vc=34119, M08-B-VCG-01) is paradigmatically CHAR-2: the prophet speaks a word God did not command — the act against a named boundary. Pro 16:5 (M08-A1-VCG-03, CHAR-1 corpus) is paradigmatically CHAR-1: arrogant in heart — the dispositional condition without a specific named transgression.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

CHAR-4 (Vain conceit — M08-D) most closely resembles CHAR-3 in that both involve cognitive self-assessment processes. The distinction: CHAR-4 is the inner cognitive over-evaluation of the self (thinking more highly of oneself than warranted — huperfroneō, Rom 12:3 context) — an inner-dwelling phenomenon. CHAR-3 is the outer verbal/social expression of self-elevation — the boasting act and self-display. CHAR-4 stays inside the cognitive-evaluative register; CHAR-3 moves outside into speech and social display. 2Cor 10:12 (M08-C-VCG-02 context): "when they measure themselves by one another... they are without understanding" — the self-comparison cognitive process sits at the CHAR-3/CHAR-4 boundary; when it stays inner it is closer to CHAR-4; when it generates a public claim it crosses into CHAR-3.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

CHAR-3 (Boasting and self-display) most closely resembles CHAR-4 within M08. The distinction: CHAR-4 is the inner cognitive inflated self-picture (the mind's wrong assessment of itself — fusioō, huperfroneō: what the person thinks about themselves); CHAR-3 is the verbal/social expression of that inflated self-picture (kauchaomai: what the person says publicly about themselves). 1Cor 4:19 (vc=33939, M08-D-VCG-01) illustrates the boundary: Paul distinguishes between the arrogant persons' "talk" (CHAR-3's territory) and their actual "power" (which CHAR-4 has misjudged) — the talk is CHAR-3; the misjudgment of actual power is CHAR-4.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

CHAR-1 (Arrogant self-elevation) most closely resembles CHAR-5. The distinction: CHAR-1 is the general dispositional elevation of the self as a posture (the heart lifted above proper creaturely station, regardless of structural medium — Pro 16:5, vc=12083: "arrogant in heart" as a universal condition). CHAR-5 is CHAR-1 expressed through and sustained by a specific structural medium — received power, wealth, military might, or positional elevation. CHAR-1 can exist in a person with no structural power (the heart can be lifted without structural backing); CHAR-5 specifically requires the structural medium as its generative occasion and its inner anchor (remove the structural goods and CHAR-5 collapses — Eze 33:28: "proud might shall come to an end" when the structural power is removed).

---

##### T6.5.2 — Where the evidence shows apparent overlap, what is the precise boundary?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The precise boundary is between inner posture (CHAR-1's domain) and specific transgressive act against a named limit (CHAR-2's domain). Num 15:30 (vc=65731, M08-A4-VCG-05) illustrates the boundary: "acting with a high hand" is treated as CHAR-1 because the evidence focuses on the inner posture of raised self-assertion ("an inner posture of defiant self-exaltation against God, where the will deliberately overrides divine command") — the high-hand idiom names the orientation, not the specific act of transgressing a named divine prohibition. The M08-B za.don/zed corpus names the specific wilful transgression of an established divine boundary (the presumptuous sin as a specific category of deliberate violation). The boundary is therefore: if the evidence emphasises the elevated inner posture as the primary datum → CHAR-1; if the evidence emphasises the specific wilful transgression of a named divine limit as the primary datum → CHAR-2. The same person may exhibit both simultaneously, but they remain analytically distinct characteristics.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Verses like Neh 9:16 (vc=34120, M08-B-VCG-01) — "they acted presumptuously and stiffened their neck and did not obey your commandments" — sit at the boundary: the stiff neck is dispositional (CHAR-1 territory); the specific act of disobeying commandments is CHAR-2. The verse is in CHAR-2's corpus because the primary datum is the act of disobedience (the zid boiling-over against a specific commandment), not a general self-elevation. The boundary is the presence of a specific named divine limit against which the will is asserting — when that is present, CHAR-2 is named; when it is absent (the general posture of self-elevation), CHAR-1 is named.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

The boundary is between inner cognitive self-assessment (CHAR-4) and public verbal/social assertion of that assessment (CHAR-3). Rom 12:16 context (M08-D): "never be wise in your own sight" — an inner cognitive overclaim that remains in the evaluative register. Jam 4:16 (vc=33886): "you boast" — the same overclaim made public through speech. CHAR-3 is CHAR-4 that has been externalised into speech and social display; CHAR-4 is the inner cognitive stage from which CHAR-3 emerges when it is verbalised.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

The boundary is between inner cognitive state (CHAR-4) and outer verbal/social expression (CHAR-3). 1Cor 8:1 (vc=33935, M08-D-VCG-01): knowledge inflating (fusioō) — the inner cognitive state is CHAR-4; when that inflation is then expressed through claims about one's knowledge to others (self-display of cognitive superiority), it crosses into CHAR-3. The cognitive self-inflation can exist before any verbal expression — that pre-verbal state is purely CHAR-4. When it becomes speech, the speech is CHAR-3.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

The boundary is the presence of structural goods as the generating occasion and inner anchor. Eze 28:5 (vc=34046, M08-E-VCG-02): "wealth gained through wisdom caused the heart to become proud" — the wealth is the generating occasion for the heart-pride; without the wealth, this specific form of heart-pride (CHAR-5) would not have been generated. A person with CHAR-1 but no structural power has the dispositional elevation without the structural medium. A person with structural power who develops CHAR-5 has CHAR-1's dispositional pattern instantiated through the specific structural medium. CHAR-5 is CHAR-1 plus structural medium.

---

##### T6.5.3 — Is the distinction between this characteristic and its nearest neighbour one of degree, kind, direction, or constitutional level?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The distinction is primarily one of kind (disposition vs. specific transgressive act) and secondarily of direction (CHAR-1's elevation is inward/upward — the self lifted; CHAR-2's defiance is outward/against — the will asserting itself against an external authority). It is not a distinction of degree (more or less of the same thing) nor of constitutional level (both CHAR-1 and CHAR-2 are located in the heart and will at the same constitutional depth — Dan 5:20, vc=34129, shows the heart and spirit engaged simultaneously in CHAR-1, while the M08-B corpus similarly locates CHAR-2 in the will). The distinction of kind means CHAR-1 can exist without any specific act of transgression (the proud dispositional walk of Dan 4:37, vc=34094, is CHAR-1 without a named specific divine limit being violated) while CHAR-2 requires a specific transgression-event. CHAR-1 is the inner climate; CHAR-2 is the storm.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Primarily kind (disposition vs. specific transgressive act) and, secondarily, specificity of the opposing authority (CHAR-1's elevation is general — above all; CHAR-2's defiance is specific — against this law, this judge, this divine word). The distinction is not of degree (one is not more intense than the other) or of constitutional level (both are located in the heart and will). The kind distinction (settled being vs. activated doing) is the primary analytical marker.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Primarily kind (inner cognitive vs outer verbal/social) and constitutional level (inner-evaluative level for CHAR-4; expressive/communicative level for CHAR-3). Not primarily degree (both can be equally intense at their respective levels). The direction is the same (both are self-directed); the constitutional level and expression mode differ.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Primarily constitutional level (inner cognitive vs outer verbal/social) and kind (epistemic vs communicative). Not degree (both can be equally intense at their level). The direction is the same (both self-directed). Constitutional level distinction: CHAR-4 operates at the mind level; CHAR-3 at the speech/social level. CHAR-4 is the inner cognitive stage from which CHAR-3 emerges when the self-assessment becomes verbalised.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Primarily kind (general dispositional elevation vs structural-medium-specific dispositional elevation) and structural medium (CHAR-5 requires structural goods; CHAR-1 does not). The direction is the same (both self-directed, both upward-elevation). The constitutional level is the same (both heart-dispositional). The distinction is in the specificity of the generating occasion and the structural anchoring: CHAR-5 is CHAR-1 with a structural-power medium; CHAR-1 is the universal dispositional form of which CHAR-5 is the structural-power sub-form.

---

##### T6.5.4 — If no significant distinction work is required, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

CHAR-1 / CHAR-2 distinction is evidenced and requires analytical work (see T6.5.1–3) given the shared volitional vocabulary and boundary-adjacency of Num 15:30. Not silent.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

CHAR-1/CHAR-2 distinction is analytically significant and evidenced. Not silent.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

CHAR-3/CHAR-4 distinction is analytically significant (inner cognitive vs outer verbal/social expression). Not silent.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

CHAR-4/CHAR-3 distinction is analytically significant (inner cognitive vs outer verbal/social). Not silent.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

CHAR-5/CHAR-1 distinction is analytically significant (structural-medium requirement vs universal dispositional form). Not silent.

---

#### T6.6 — Shared Verse Anchors

##### T6.6.1 — Does any verse in this characteristic's evidence base also function as a primary anchor in another characteristic's study?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Yes. Jam 4:6 (vc=33931, M08-A4-VCG-01) and 1Pe 5:5 (vc=33934, M08-A4-VCG-01) — "God opposes the proud but gives grace to the humble" — function as primary anchors for both CHAR-1 (M08) and M09 (humility): they define CHAR-1 precisely through its named structural opposite within the same verse. Both characteristics require these verses. Pro 16:18 (vc=34073, vc=33978, M08-A1-VCG-03, M08-A4-VCG-04) — "pride goes before destruction, and a haughty spirit before a fall" — is the primary anchor for CHAR-1's consequence register and will likely also anchor any programme study of moral collapse or destructive inner-being states in adjacent clusters. Mar 7:22 (vc=33928, M08-A4-VCG-01) — the heart-sourced evil-things list — is a foundational anchor for M08's theological framing of multiple characteristics (CHAR-1, and potentially CHAR-4 vain conceit and CHAR-5) since it attributes all as constitutively internal products of the fallen heart. CC to confirm specific cross-cluster anchor assignments when other characteristics' Phase 9 work is complete.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Psa 19:13 (vc=34095, M08-B-VCG-02) — "keep back your servant also from presumptuous sins; let them not have dominion over me, then I shall be blameless" — is a potential shared anchor with M09 (humility/servant posture) since it names the humble servant orientation that blocks CHAR-2 and that M09 will need to articulate. Mar 10:42 (vc=55588, M08-B-VCG-03) — Jesus' naming of domineering authority patterns — is the foundational verse for any programme study of servant-leadership models (possibly M31 or adjacent cluster), since it defines CHAR-2's pattern as the inverse of what Jesus models. CC to confirm cross-cluster anchor assignments when adjacent characteristics' Phase 9 work is complete.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Yes. 1Cor 1:31 (vc=33878, M08-C-VCG-03): "let the one who boasts, boast in the Lord" — will anchor M22 (Divine Praise) studies as the commanded redirection of the boasting-impulse toward God; this verse defines both the M08 condemned direction and the M22 approved direction. Jer 9:23 (vc=33342, M08-C-VCG-01): the wisdom prohibition against boasting in wisdom/might/wealth will anchor discussions of false confidence and its alternatives across multiple clusters. 1Cor 4:7 (vc=33871, M08-C-VCG-01): "what do you have that you did not receive?" — a potential anchor for M39 (Blessing/Favour/Grace) when it examines the received quality of all divine gifts.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Rom 12:3 (vc=60866, M08-D-VCG-02): "do not think of yourself more highly than you ought, but think with sober judgment, each according to the measure of faith God has assigned" — will likely anchor discussions of the spiritual gifts discourse in Romans 12 (where it introduces the body-of-Christ ordering of gifts) and may anchor M09 (humility) studies as a mind-level corrective. 1Cor 8:1 (vc=33935, M08-D-VCG-01): "knowledge puffs up, but love builds up" — will likely anchor discussions of love (M10 or adjacent) and the knowledge-love relationship across clusters. 1Cor 13:4 (vc=33936): "love is not arrogant [fusioō]" — a primary anchor for any programme study of love's inner-being definition.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Yes. Eze 16:49 (vc=33979, M08-E-VCG-01): "this was the guilt of your sister Sodom: she and her daughters had pride, excess of food, and prosperous ease, but did not aid the poor and needy" — will anchor social-justice cluster discussions (the failure to aid the poor as a structural consequence of power-pride); may also anchor M46 (Abundance/Prosperity/Wealth) as evidencing the corruption of abundance through pride. 1Ti 6:17 (vc=60878, M08-E-VCG-02) — will anchor M46 (wealth/prosperity) discussions as the primary NT instruction on wealth's proper orientation. The verse spans M08-CHAR-5 (hupsēlofroneō) and M46 (material prosperity as the context).

---

##### T6.6.2 — What does the shared anchor reveal about the relationship between the two characteristics?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The shared anchors in Jam 4:6 (vc=33931) and 1Pe 5:5 (vc=33934) reveal that CHAR-1 and M09 (humility) are structurally co-defined: neither can be understood without reference to the other. The same verse names both the characteristic (God opposes the proud — CHAR-1) and its structural opposite (gives grace to the humble — M09) as a single divine relational logic. This means CHAR-1 is not merely one characteristic among others but is definitionally constituted by its polarity with M09: to know CHAR-1 fully requires knowing M09, and vice versa. The shared anchor indicates that Scripture's primary treatment of the pride-humility polarity is relational (God's differentiating response — opposition vs grace) rather than merely psychological (inner states in isolation). Pro 16:18's potential cross-cluster anchoring similarly reveals CHAR-1's consequence register as a cross-characteristic diagnostic — wherever moral collapse appears in the biblical material, CHAR-1 is evidenced as a structural precursor.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Psa 19:13 (vc=34095) shared with M09 reveals that CHAR-2 and M09 are definitionally related through the servant-who-needs-divine-restraint pattern: the humble servant (M09) is defined in part by their vulnerability to CHAR-2's dominion-seeking impulses and their dependence on God to hold those impulses back. Mar 10:42 (vc=55588) shared with the servant-leadership register reveals that CHAR-2 is the pattern that Jesus' authority model explicitly inverts — naming the christological significance of CHAR-2's relational-authority form.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

1Cor 1:31 (vc=33878) shared with M22 reveals that CHAR-3 and M22 are definitionally structured around the same verse as the hinge between the condemned and the commanded: "let the one who boasts, boast in the Lord" is both CHAR-3's commanded redirection and M22's commanded expression. The verse serves both clusters because it names the boundary between them. 1Cor 4:7 (vc=33871) shared with M39 reveals that CHAR-3 is the distortion of the proper response to received grace — acknowledging the received quality of gifts (M39) is what CHAR-3's condemned form denies.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Rom 12:3 (vc=60866) shared with body-of-Christ ordering and M09 reveals that CHAR-4 is constitutively addressed within the context of the spiritual-gifts community — the proper cognitive measure is defined relationally (within the body of Christ, each with a God-assigned measure). 1Cor 8:1 (vc=33935) and 1Cor 13:4 (vc=33936) shared with love studies reveals that CHAR-4 and love are definitionally co-defined: love is named by the absence of fusioō (CHAR-4); CHAR-4 is named by the absence of love.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Eze 16:49 (vc=33979) shared with social-justice clusters reveals that CHAR-5 is directly implicated in the structural roots of social injustice — the pride-of-power characteristic is what prevents the powerful from seeing and responding to the needs of the vulnerable. 1Ti 6:17 (vc=60878) shared with M46 reveals that CHAR-5 and the proper stewardship of wealth are defined against each other within the same verse: hupsēlofroneō (CHAR-5's wealth-form) and "richly provides everything to enjoy" (the proper recognition of God as provider) are the two poles of the wealthy person's formation challenge.

---

##### T6.6.3 — If no shared verse anchors are identified, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Shared verse anchors confirmed: Jam 4:6 (vc=33931) and 1Pe 5:5 (vc=33934) shared with M09; Pro 16:18 (vc=34073) likely shared with moral-collapse registers across clusters; Mar 7:22 (vc=33928) potentially shared with multiple M08 characteristics. Not silent.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Potential shared anchors identified (Psa 19:13 with M09; Mar 10:42 with servant-leadership cluster). Not silent.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Shared anchors confirmed: 1Cor 1:31 with M22; 1Cor 4:7 with M39. Not silent.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Potential shared anchors confirmed: Rom 12:3 with M09 and body-of-Christ ordering; 1Cor 8:1 and 13:4 with love studies. Not silent.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Shared anchors confirmed: Eze 16:49 with social-justice clusters and M46; 1Ti 6:17 with M46. Not silent.

---

#### T6.7 — Dimensional Sharing

##### T6.7.1 — How many of this characteristic's confirmed analytical dimensions are shared with another characteristic in the programme?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (G)

Full dimensional comparison data is not yet available: only CHAR-1 has been processed at Phase 9 in this session, and the programme's cross-cluster dimensional mapping requires all Phase 9 characteristic work to be complete before systematic comparison is possible. Preliminary from the verse evidence within M08: the volitional dimension (T1.8, T3.6) is shared with CHAR-2 (Presumptuous defiance — M08-B) since CHAR-2's specific transgressive act emerges from the same volitional faculty that CHAR-1 occupies as a disposition; the dispositional dimension (T1.8) is shared with CHAR-4 (vain conceit — M08-D), which appears to be CHAR-1's cognitive sub-form (self-elevation specifically located in the thought/opinion faculty). Full count of shared dimensions across the programme is a gap pending completion.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (G)

Full dimensional comparison data is not yet available — only CHAR-1 and CHAR-2 have been processed at Phase 9 in this session. Preliminary: the volitional dimension is shared with CHAR-1 (both operate constitutionally through the will, though CHAR-1 is the dispositional-volitional claim and CHAR-2 is the act-volitional assertion). The relational dimension is shared with CHAR-1 (both impair relational capacity in the authority-bearing direction). The agency dimension is shared with CHAR-1 (both energise agency toward self-serving ends). Full dimensional count pending completion of all five CHAR Phase 9 studies.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (G)

Full dimensional comparison data is not yet available — only CHAR-1, CHAR-2, and CHAR-3 have been processed in this session. Preliminary: the communicative/expressive dimension is uniquely CHAR-3 within M08 (neither CHAR-1 nor CHAR-2 is primarily communicative); the dispositional dimension (alazoneia substrate) is shared with CHAR-1; the cognitive dimension (self-assessment process) is shared with CHAR-4 (nearest neighbour). Full dimensional count pending.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (G)

Full dimensional comparison data not yet available. Preliminary: CHAR-4's primary cognitive/epistemic dimension is unique within M08 — no other M08 characteristic is primarily cognitive. The relational dimension (1Cor 8:1; 13:4; 2Cor 12:20) is shared with CHAR-1, CHAR-2, CHAR-3. The dispositional dimension (underlying CHAR-1 ground) is shared with CHAR-1.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (G)

Full dimensional comparison data not yet available — all five M08 characteristics have now been processed, enabling a preliminary cross-characteristic summary. Preliminary: the dispositional dimension is shared with CHAR-1 (both are heart-dispositional); the volitional dimension (shal.le.tet — imperious self-will) is shared with CHAR-2 (volitional transgressive act); the cognitive dimension (Isa 47:8 — self-sufficiency claim) is shared with CHAR-4 (cognitive self-assessment); the communicative dimension (Isa 47:8 — "you say in your heart") is shared with CHAR-3 (verbal expression). The uniquely CHAR-5 dimension is the structural-collective register: CHAR-5 is the only M08 characteristic extensively evidenced at the national-collective level across multiple nations and generations.

---

##### T6.7.2 — What does the pattern of dimensional sharing reveal about the relationship between this characteristic and those it shares dimensions with?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (G)

Preliminary from available evidence: the shared volitional dimension with CHAR-2 confirms the functional relationship evidenced in T6.5 — CHAR-1 (disposition) and CHAR-2 (act) share the will as their common constitutional seat, making CHAR-2 the activated form of CHAR-1's volitional energy in the face of a specific divine limit. The shared dispositional dimension with CHAR-4 suggests that CHAR-4 (vain conceit) may be CHAR-1's cognitive sub-expression — the same self-elevation operating specifically through the thought-assessment faculty (thinking more highly of oneself than warranted, per Rom 12:3 context in M08-D) as a narrower form of CHAR-1's broader dispositional self-elevation. Full dimensional pattern analysis pending completion of all five M08 characteristic Phase 9 studies.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (G)

Preliminary: the shared volitional and agency dimensions with CHAR-1 confirm that the two characteristics are constitutively related at the faculty level — they share the same constitutional machinery (will and agency) but differ in their functional expression (disposition vs act). The relational dimension's shared engagement with CHAR-1 further confirms they operate in the same relational domain (authority-bearing relationships) from different positions (CHAR-1 as the elevated self; CHAR-2 as the self transgressing the limit).

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (G)

Preliminary: the unique communicative/expressive primary dimension of CHAR-3 distinguishes it from all other M08 characteristics — it is the only M08 characteristic whose primary dimension is the speech-act/social display. The shared dispositional dimension with CHAR-1 confirms the generative relationship; the shared cognitive dimension with CHAR-4 confirms the inner/outer expression pairing.

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (G)

CHAR-4's unique primary cognitive dimension confirms it as the cognitive sub-form of CHAR-1 — the dispositional self-elevation (CHAR-1) is expressed through different faculties: cognitive (CHAR-4), verbal (CHAR-3), volitional-transgressive (CHAR-2). Full cross-characteristic dimensional mapping pending.

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

The dimensional sharing pattern across all five M08 characteristics reveals CHAR-5 as the most extensively cross-dimensional of the five: it shares the dispositional dimension with CHAR-1, the volitional dimension with CHAR-2, the communicative dimension with CHAR-3, and the cognitive dimension with CHAR-4. What CHAR-5 uniquely contributes is the structural-collective register — the only characteristic evidenced as a multi-generational collective characteristic of entire nations. The carry-forward observation (M08-E ↔ M23) is the dimensional expression of this uniqueness: CHAR-5 uniquely links the M08 pride cluster to the M23 strength/power/dominion cluster.

---

## T7 — Lexical, Literary, and Scientific Analysis (20 prompts)

---

### T7

#### T7.1 — Lexical and Semantic Analysis

##### T7.1.1 — What are the primary Hebrew and Greek terms for this characteristic — and what do their root meanings reveal?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

The CHAR-1 corpus draws on two primary Hebrew root families and one primary Greek word-family. First, the g-'-h root family: ga.ah (H1342, to rise/soar), ga.on (H1347, rising grandeur/pride), ga.a.vah (H1346, arrogance/pride), ga.vah (H1361, to exalt/rise proudly), ga.vo.ah (H1364, high/haughty), ge.eh (H1343, proud — person-type adjective), ge.ah (H1344, pride — noun), ge.ut (H1348, majesty/pride), ge.vah (H1466, pride/height), gav.hut (H1365, haughtiness). This root family generates both M08's pride vocabulary and M22's divine-majesty vocabulary — the root meaning is elemental upward movement: to swell, to rise, to tower. Second, the r-w-m root family: rum (H7311A, verbal — to be high, to lift up, to rise) and its noun form H7312; also ma.rom (H4791, height/lofty place). The root meaning is spatial elevation: to be in or move to a higher position. Third, the Greek huperēfanos (G5244, from huper — above, over — + phainomai — to appear, to be visible): the one who appears above others; huperēfania (G5243): the quality of appearing above others. The root meaning adds the social-visibility dimension the Hebrew height vocabulary does not emphasise explicitly. Across all primary terms, the definitional core is the same: upward movement of the self beyond proper creaturely station, whether named through spatial metaphor (Hebrew) or social-visibility metaphor (Greek).

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Primary Hebrew terms: zid (H2102) — root meaning: to boil, to seethe, to act presumptuously; the metaphor of a liquid boiling over its container names the will's self-assertive overflow beyond its legitimate containment by divine command (Deu 18:20, vc=34119, M08-B-VCG-01: "the prophet who presumes [zid] to speak"). Za.don (H2087) — noun of insolence/presumptuousness; the inner quality of deliberate defiance of authority (Pro 13:10, vc=34113, M08-B-VCG-02: "by insolence [za.don] comes nothing but strife"; Pro 11:2, vc=34109: za.don brings disgrace). Zed (H2086) — adjective/noun: the arrogant/insolent person as a type; one who treats divine law and authority with contempt (Psa 119:21, vc=34098, M08-B-VCG-02: "the insolent [zed], accursed ones, who wander from your commandments"). Primary Greek terms: authadēs (G0829) — self-pleasing, self-willed; etymology from auto (self) + hēdomai (to please oneself) — the one who satisfies their own will without constraint from legitimate authority (Tit 1:7, vc=42740, M08-B-VCG-03). Tolmētēs (G5113) — one who dares recklessly; from tolmaō (to dare, to be bold) — reckless presumptuous boldness directed against what should command reverence (2Pe 2:10, vc=4670). Archō (G0757) — to begin, to be first, to rule; in M08-B-VCG-03 used for the onset of presumptuous relational assertions (Mar 8:32, vc=55607; Mar 10:42, vc=55588). Root convergence: all primary terms name the self's self-authorising transgression against an established external authority.

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Primary Hebrew term: ha.lal (H1984H) in its self-directed boasting sense — root meaning: to shine, to make bright, to celebrate, to praise; the term spans the entire shine-celebrate-praise spectrum; in its self-directed form (VCG-01) the "shining" is the self's own display. 1Ki 20:11 (vc=33353, M08-C-VCG-01): "let not him who puts on his armour boast [ha.lal]." Jer 9:23 (vc=33342): the prohibition against boasting in wisdom, might, wealth uses ha.lal for all three. Ro.hav (H7296, Psa 90:10, vc=34222, M08-C-VCG-01): prideful excess — what life's best span amounts to ("toil and trouble"), undercutting any inner boast about its worth. Primary Greek terms: kauchaomai (G2744) — to boast, exult, glory; from uncertain root (possibly related to kata + auchēn, lowering the neck = assuming a proud posture) or to aucheō (to boast); the verb is primarily Pauline and its dominant use is in 2 Corinthians. Kauchēma (G2745) — the object or ground of boasting; kauchēsis (G2746) — the act of boasting. Alazoneia (G0212) — inner boasting disposition, arrogant display; from alazōn (one who wanders or roams — possibly from the idea of travelling around making inflated claims). Alazōn (G0213) — the braggart as person-type. Root convergence: ha.lal and kauchaomai both name the act of publicly asserting glory/worth; their distinctiveness is that ha.lal spans the full praise-spectrum (including God-directed praise) while kauchaomai spans the full boasting-spectrum (from condemned VCG-01 through God-directed VCG-03).

**[CHAR-4] Vain conceit** (E)

Four primary Greek terms constitute CHAR-4's vocabulary. Fusioō (G5448): to inflate, to puff up — from phusaō (to blow, to inflate with air); the pneumatic metaphor names inflation beyond actual substance, like a bladder inflated with air beyond its natural shape. 1Cor 8:1 (vc=33935, M08-D-VCG-01): "knowledge puffs up [fusioō]." Tufoō (G5187): to be wrapped in smoke, to be puffed up — from tuphō (to raise smoke/steam); the obfuscation metaphor names cognitive clouding alongside inflation. 1Ti 6:4 (vc=33925, M08-D-VCG-02): conceit paired with "understanding nothing" — the smoke-metaphor explains the comprehensive epistemic blindness: the conceited mind is enveloped in cognitive smoke. Fusiōsis (G5450): the nominalized form of fusioō — the quality or state of inflation as it manifests in community disorder. 2Cor 12:20 (vc=33942, M08-D-VCG-02): "conceit [fusiōsis]" in the relational-disorder cluster. Huperfroneō (G5252): to think above (huper + froneō) what is warranted — the compound names the cognitive act of exceeding the proper measure. Rom 12:3 (vc=60866, M08-D-VCG-02): "do not think of yourself more highly [huperfroneō] than you ought." Root convergence: all primary terms name cognitive inflation through different metaphors — air-inflation (fusioō), smoke-obfuscation (tufoō), above-measure thinking (huperfroneō).

**[CHAR-5] Pride of power and position** (E)

Seven primary terms constitute CHAR-5's vocabulary. Ga.on (H1347) in the proud-might subset: from the g-'-h root (to rise, swell, be exalted) — names the inner national-collective confidence that rises from structural power. Eze 30:6 (vc=33996, M08-E-VCG-01): "Egypt's proud might." Ma.rom (H4791): height, lofty place — from rum (H7311A, to be high, to rise) — names the physical-structural elevation used as a power-strategy. Jer 49:16 (vc=34167, M08-E-VCG-02): "the height of your dwelling." Ga.vah (H1361): to be exalted/proud — from the g-'-h root — names the heart's elevation generated by received wealth. Eze 28:5 (vc=34046, M08-E-VCG-02): "your heart became proud [ga.vah]." Shal.le.tet (H7986): imperious self-will, domineering — from shalat (to dominate, to rule) — names the unrestrained exercise of will from structural power. Eze 16:30 (vc=57959, M08-E-VCG-02): "impetuousness." A.din (H5719): voluptuous ease, self-indulgence — from the root of pleasure/ease — names the affective condition of material abundance that generates self-sufficiency. Isa 47:8 (vc=9563, M08-E-VCG-02): "you who love pleasures [a.din]." Qo.mah (H6967): height, stature — names the visible physical dominance of rulers as a pride-indicator. Eze 19:11 (vc=54398, M08-E-VCG-02): "towering stature." Hupsēlofroneō (G5309): from hupsēlos (high) + froneō (to think) — haughty thinking grounded in material elevation. 1Ti 6:17 (vc=60878, M08-E-VCG-02): "not to be haughty [hupsēlofroneō]." Root convergence: all terms name the same pattern — structural elevation (height, power, wealth, ease) generating inner arrogant self-confidence.

---

##### T7.1.2 — What is the grammatical range of the primary term (noun, verb, adjective, participle) — and what does that range reveal about how the characteristic operates?

**[CHAR-1] Arrogant self-elevation** (E)

Taking rum (H7311A) as the primary verb-form term: it operates across verbal, nominal, and adjectival registers. Verbal active: the will lifting itself or being lifted (Dan 11:36, vc=34235, M08-A1-VCG-02: "he shall exalt himself"; Isa 14:13, vc=34233, M08-A4-VCG-05: "I will ascend"). Verbal passive/reflexive: the heart being lifted in response to conditions (Deu 8:14, vc=34223, M08-A1-VCG-01: "your heart will be lifted up"). Nominal: H7312 as a noun naming the quality of lofty pride (Psa 21:4 context; Isa 2:11, vc=34601, M08-A3-VCG-04: "the lofty pride of men"). Taking ga.vah (H1361) as the primary heart-seat verb: it describes a state of being proud/haughty (Eze 28:2, vc=34040: "your heart is proud") and the act of becoming proud (2Ch 26:16, vc=34044: "he grew proud"). The grammatical range across verb (act and state), noun (quality), and adjective (person-type — ge.eh, ga.vo.ah) confirms that CHAR-1 is grammatically comprehensive: it operates as an act performed by the will, a state inhabited by the heart, and a quality characterising the person. This grammatical range reflects the three-level finding of T1.2: CHAR-1 is simultaneously act, disposition, and constitutive quality.

**[CHAR-2] Presumptuous defiance** (E)

Taking zid (H2102) as the primary verb: it operates primarily in the verbal register (to act presumptuously, to boil over — Deu 1:43, vc=34123: "you acted presumptuously [zid]"; Deu 18:20, vc=34119: "the prophet who presumes [zid] to speak"). Za.don (H2087) operates as a noun (the quality of presumptuousness — Pro 11:2: "when arrogance [za.don] comes") and as an adverbial phrase in contexts (Pro 13:10: "by insolence [za.don]"). Zed (H2086) operates as an adjective/substantive naming the person-type (Psa 119:21: "the insolent [zed]"; Isa 13:11, vc=34104: "the arrogant [zed] person"). The grammatical range covers: verbal act (zid), dispositional quality (za.don), and person-type (zed) — confirming that CHAR-2 is grammatically an act performed by the will (zid), a quality inhabiting the inner person (za.don), and a type that characterises the habitual defier (zed).

**[CHAR-3] Boasting and self-display** (E)

Kauchaomai (G2744) operates primarily as a verbal infinitive and finite verb: "to boast," "to glory in," "to exult in." It takes a direct object or prepositional phrase naming the boasting-ground (en — "in": "boasting in the Lord" — 1Cor 1:31, vc=33878; "boasting in the law" — Rom 2:23, vc=33883; "boasting in weaknesses" — 2Cor 12:9, vc=33870).
